The Two Spirits enfold purity, resplendent before sun and moon.
The One Qi waxes and wanes, blending beyond heaven and earth.
Mystery upon mystery—tracing its traces is endless.
Wonder within wonder—profound thought cannot fathom it.
Hui Shi could debate, yet his words failed to capture its form.
Duanmu could speak, yet his speech could not open its gate.
Li Lou excelled in sight; though he widened his eyes in daylight,
blinking to gaze, he could not perceive its shape.
Shi Kuang excelled in hearing; though he turned his head at night,
listening intently, he could not catch its sound.
To surpass the elite, rise above the crowd,
is to be first among things—yet never fully grasp its principle.
To forget one’s qi, to refine the spirit,
is to perfect the discipline of the Dao, merging with the Great Beginning—
yet never exhaust its mechanism.
Thus, jade-refined and gold-visaged, pure truth flourishes.
Precious patterns in jade caskets dissolve impure substance.
Sea spirits congeal in splendor, images emerge in cinnabar radiance.
The Three-in-One blends seamlessly, essence flows through celestial secrets.
Within, it harmonizes with star-hung jeweled banquets—
the realm before the unbegun.

**Eulogy:**
The Dao of Supreme Clarity—pure, true, and steadfast.
Heaven’s winds are lofty and unsullied, the sea’s moon is clear and solitary.
Ascending the empyrean, traces vanish; bending near, all plans are forgotten.
Jade ridges rise steep, pools gleam with lustrous virtue.
Mysterious essence shines like jade, wondrous substance is numinous and boundless.
Luminous splendor roams freely, auspicious qi forms propitious signs.
The Primal blends in splendor, cinnabar images stream like pearls.
Within, starry hues are contained, roaming the divine capital.

**Inscription on the Celestial Round Image Uniting with the Spirit:**
The Dao—silent, without sound; vast, without color.
From ancient times it spans to the present, standing alone and unchanging.
Formless form—approaching, one does not see its front.
Imageless image—following, one does not see its rear.
Spoken of as vast, it encompasses heaven and earth, yet this is not its greatness.
Called subtle, it pierces grains of sand, yet this is not its smallness.
Tracing its traces knows no method; pursuing it, it grows ever more distant.
Profound thought stirs a response; measuring it, it grows ever nearer.
Obscure as twilight, listening within, one’s hearing sharpens.
Dim and distant, it conceals the utmost essence.
Brilliant and solitary, one sees clearly without—
elusive and indistinct, it moves through the utmost spirit.
The spiritual source is one, guiding transformation in three accomplishments:
First, it seizes the qi of yin and yang;
second, it illumines the essence of sun and moon;
third, it draws forth the splendor of heaven and earth.
Those who cultivate it through refinement reach fruition in a thousand days.
Blending with it, one becomes enlightened through the Image-Web.
The Image-Web penetrates the mysterious, piercing metal and stone.
Swimming through water, treading fire, walking blades, crossing peril—
myriad transformations, endless in number.
Encountering things without fear—what is this called?
It is the steadfast guarding of pure qi.
Those who achieve this are called cultivators of true virtue,
adepts of divine and sagely attainment.

**Eulogy:**
Within, it harmonizes with the distant and obscure;
without, it connects with celestial radiance.
The Dao is this One and None—
virtue, these Three Reflections.
Mysterious images manifest brightness, the subtle mind shines at the solstice.
The Four Qi gleam in clarity, the Five Spirits rest in emptiness.
Crowned with flowered canopies, their forms ride cloud-borne chariots.
Beyond heaven, winds are pure; in the heart of the pool, the moon is cool.
Vast as twilight, silent as a flame—
hidden and manifest, distinct and clear.
Wondrous! Auspicious and blessed.

**Inscription on the Precious Flourishing Star of the Great Mystery:**
The Primal One imparts teachings—no response is unanswered.
The Dao and virtue open the origin—nothing is left unborn.
The Great Void stretches boundless and without limit;
heaven and earth loom vast and with form.
Qian and Kun embrace transformation, the ten thousand things flow into shape.
Yin and yang receive qi, alternating in mutual dependence.
Those who receive transformation are not limited to one life;
those who contain embryos are not confined to one form.
In heaven, images descend—auspicious and ominous omens appear.
On earth, forms take shape—the principles of being and nonbeing are discerned.
In humans, changes occur—the mechanisms of movement and stillness are revealed.
Buddhist disciples call it the Buddha;
Confucian scholars, the Sage;
Daoist adepts, the Immortal.
Different paths, one source—the Dao is singular.
Thus, celestial spirits and earthly deities,
divine luminaries and sovereign lords,
sun, moon, and stars,
immortals, perfected beings, and supreme sages,
jade maidens and golden youths,
officials, generals, and marshals,
ancient buddhas and arhats,
the Eight Divisions of Heavenly Dragons,
the Four Kindnesses and Three Realms,
mountains, rivers, and great marshes,
the Yangtze, Huai, and Ji rivers,
pearls, jade, gold, and stone,
mystery and yellow, sweet and bitter—
even those born from wombs, eggs, moisture, or transformation,
those with form or without,
with appearance or without,
with transformation or without,
neither transforming nor not transforming—
all who revere the One are revering the supreme Dao.
Those who transform and unite with it are the spirit of the Infinite.
This spirit—below, it becomes ghosts;
in the middle, humans;
above, stars.
Stars dissolve without form, returning to the era before the Great Simplicity.
Before heaven, without ancestry—
yet uniting with it is called the origin of the supreme Dao.

**Eulogy:**
Profound and pure, the celestial truth is subtle and hidden.
Confucian, Buddhist, and Daoist winds—heaven, earth, and humans all embrace them.
Divided into three, they wondrously return to the essence of the One.
Grasping being, rooted in nonbeing—embodying emptiness as if substantial.
Forms dissolve, clarity and hearing unite;
wisdom connects with the numinous substance.
The spirit roams the corners of the sea, the soul soars through celestial realms.
Embracing jade-like radiance in intoxication, sleeping on clouds beneath the sun.
Nine-colored stellar vapors—all dharmas are complete.

**Inscription on the Vast Obscurity and Luminous Tranquility of the Primal Spirit:**
The Dao is the substance of emptiness and nonbeing.
Virtue is the function of spirit and transformation.
Substance and function require each other—
this is called the Great Communication.
The Great Communication lies in the principles of true qi and spirit.
This qi is light, clear, simple, and wondrous.

Its essence is unbounded and soaring.
Its spirit is vast and profoundly deep.
In silence, it dims into obscurity yet intent remains;
in illumination, it blazes radiantly yet the heart is forgotten.
In subtle completion, it unfolds the dark and yellow hues of heaven and earth;
in upright transformation, it reveals the mechanisms of yin-yang’s block and flow.
Elusively it follows the rise and fall of wind and clouds,
mightily it traverses the waves of rivers and seas.
Congealed, it veils the beauty of mountains and rivers;
lushly it embraces the flourishing of grasses and trees.
Resplendent, it emits the brilliance of gold and jade;
abundant, it stirs the transformations of fish and dragons.
Thus, it colors without dye,
shapes without carving,
speeds without haste,
achieves without acting.
No can and no cannot,
no ability and no inability.
Mysterious beyond mystery,
wondrous in its very wonder.
The spirit roams the islet’s essence,
penetrating the boundless expanse.

**Inscription:**
The supreme vehicle of the Dao, transmitted by ancestral sages—
without clinging to forms, what need for names and words?
The use of the useless,
the spontaneous arising.
The two spirits initiate the wondrous,
the one qi communicates the profound.
Dragons soar the azure heavens,
phoenixes wing the cinnabar skies.
Luminous radiance illumines the jeweled realm,
light shines upon the field of sacred mushrooms.
Upright and firm, pure and unalloyed—
prior to the beginning, before the Emperor of Images.

**Inscription on Ascending the Celestial Constellation in the Jade Clarity of the Mysterious Above:**
The Dao illumines the mysterious vision, beginning before the primordial.
The Emperor of Images emerges from myriad Brahmās,
initiating qi to govern the Three Origins.
Heaven and earth become limpid,
sun and moon grow bright.
Its essence shines boundlessly,
subtly wondrous and profoundly connected.
It cherishes beings and benefits life,
harmonious yet not excessive.
In sudden enlightenment, it becomes effortlessly divine;
in intuitive insight, it attains the formless form.
Aspiration congeals in the cosmos,
merging into the Central Origin.
The empty chamber generates whiteness—
this is the omen of auspiciousness.
Its Dao, still, generates spirit;
its spirit, moved, communicates with the Dao.
Neither seen nor heard,
it manifests in celestial portents,
enriching the divine and sagely without limit.
Neither moving nor still,
in the clarity of emptiness,
it bestows the responsive grace of the Numinous Treasure.
Silent and desolate, it conceals within all functions.
Vague and indistinct, it reveals to all benevolence.
Wondrous indeed is the mysterious Dao,
supreme virtue and divine power—
vastly unfolding, it follows the origin of stellar brilliance.

**Inscription:**
In the Jade Clarity of the Mysterious Above,
the Primal Unity ascends the celestial constellation.
Chaos darkens the ford,
the Primordial Crimson Script.
The Cinnabar Sovereign rides in splendor,
the Numinous Treasure flourishes in purity.
Spirit congeals in the cosmos,
the mysterious shines upon the celestial winds.
Yellow blossoms flow in purity,
essence gleams in the jade register.
Forgetting form to accord with images,
harmonizing with the Dao to generate spirit.
Intermingled light blazes resplendently,
luminous and pure as jade’s brilliance.
The Central Origin’s wondrous image—
this is called the Mysterious Real.

**Eulogy:**
In former years, my heart-source was dimmed and closed;
today, my Dao-eye opens clearly.
Joyfully I see the azure sky like a jade table—
the twin wheels have ground apart the white clouds’ heap.

**Inscription on the Roaming of the Primal Spirit in the Supreme Mystery:**
To enter the Dao and cultivate the real,
revere the Three Treasures,
honor the two parents,
abandon jealousy and arrogance,
dissolve greed and timidity.
Encounter the Three Teachings without fostering division,
meet the Four Assemblies to forge good affinity.
All sentient beings receiving transformation
are like parents—reverence and sincerity.
In communal dwelling, be humble and cautious in speech;
in solitude, advance wisdom and guard the heart.
Walk with measured steps,
speak in a low voice.
See as if not seeing,
gazing upon the great image’s formlessness—
formlessness is called the Dao flourishing in utmost clarity,
this is the wondrous principle of communicating with spirit.
Hear as if not hearing,
listening to the great sound’s rare tone—
the rare tone is called virtue.
In clarity, utmost acuity—
this is the mysterious mechanism of entering sageliness.
Internally, all is harmonious and fused,
flesh and bone as one,
pure essence without image,
lustrous as pristine frost.
Externally, forget form and flow in purity,
merge qi and incline toward yang,
vastly empty and still,
pure as celestial light.
Thus, internal and external unite,
circulating through the six directions,
easily encountering the profound mystery,
achieving the beauty of beauty.
Li Shifang, forgetting water and moon, ascends the real.
Lie Yukou, mastering the numinous wind, enters sageliness.
The Dao is not far from humanity—
humanity distances itself from the Dao.
Alas! The scions of noble houses,
many are deluded by wine and sensuality,
wholly infatuated with fame and fortune—
losing the root-source of the wondrous Dao,
they fall into the evil destinies of suffering.
If they would turn their heads to reflect,
purify their hearts like cold ashes,
receive the supreme Dao,
trace their steps back to the origin,
they would ascend the celestial constellation and shed their forms,
rising into the wondrous realm.

**Inscription:**
Embracing the Dao and cherishing virtue,
excellence and beauty beyond compare.
The precious mirror within the mysterious,
the luminous pearl within the eyelash.
Expel poisonous miasmas,
eradicate sharp arrogance and boasting.
Preserve the real and release the false,
uphold the upright and dispel the perverse.
The furnace glows with phoenix radiance,
the cauldron smelts dragon sands.
The Southern Aster shines resplendently,
the Northern Emperor flows with rosy clouds.
The spirit roams the celestial weave,
the stars traverse the Central Flower.
The Jade Capital and Golden Gates—
the abode of the Primordial Beginning.

**Inscription on the Supreme Simplicity Generating Spirit and Transforming Images:**
The Dao is mysterious, virtue is wondrous—
the whole spirit meets the numinous.
Floating and sinking through heaven and earth,
ascending and descending through yin and yang.
Governing the creation of the Three Powers,
uniting the production of the Four Seasons.
Communicating with the origin to benefit qi,
merging beings to flow essence.
Applied, mountains and rivers grow resplendent;
moved, sun and moon grow bright.
Shining yet not dazzling,
silently accordant with the true source.
Acting yet not relying,
carving and shaping all forms.
Form and spirit both wondrous,
each attains its real.
Nurturing spirit with the five qi—
these qi are azure, cinnabar, green, white, and black.
Nurturing form with the five flavors—
these flavors are sour, bitter, sweet, pungent, and salty.
Flavor without flavor—
this is called true flavor.
Color without color—
this is called true color.
Sound without sound—
this is called true sound.
Great without incompleteness,
subtle without failure to respond.
Responding to heaven is called clarity,
responding to earth is called tranquility.
Responding to mountains is called elegance,
responding to water is called coolness.
Responding to emptiness and whiteness is transformation,
responding to beings is called life.
Responding to form is called substance,
responding to images is called stars.
Stars hang high and pure,
positioned in the resplendent clarity.
The mysterious and green endure in vision,
treasured blessings extend life.

The host of perfected beings enjoy their blessings,
all owing to the wind of the Most High.

In praise:
Following the movement of heaven’s Dao,
it transforms and harmonizes human relations.
Majestic and manifesting virtue,
radiant and embracing truth.
In serene subtlety, wondrous principle converges,
gathering essence and unifying spirit.
Clear and congealed, the treasured talismans,
wisdom connects with the misty vapors.
The primal numinous treasure shines,
its refined substance resplendent.
The hundred clans in daily use,
the myriad things transform in purity.
The sun’s countenance shines bright,
the spirit’s visage is serene and spacious.
The cloud-cloaked feathered scholar,
the Perfected One of the Dark Valley.

*Inscription on the Precious Mirror of the Great Void’s Containing Spirit*

Now, to establish virtue and cultivate benevolence,
to illuminate the practice of the Dao and its teachings,
to accumulate spiritual merit in quiet intervals,
to settle the mind and halt thoughts,
to still concerns and forget schemes—
conceal brilliance as jade hidden within stone,
obscure traces like clams parted from their pearls.
With eyes like mugwort and a heart like tumbleweed,
many are deluded by semblances of dharma.
Yet with the eye of wisdom and the wellspring of spirit,
one broadly attains the unborn.
Embodying heaven, one practices the Dao,
following the sun and moon in their lofty course.
Emulating earth’s patterns,
one employs the turning pivot of the celestial sphere.
The three palaces wondrously open,
the six caves mysteriously illumine.
Discerning the principles of floating and sinking in being and non-being,
examining the mechanisms of ascent and descent in movement and stillness.
The golden crucible’s fire blazes, advancing the yang radiance,
pervading the body of the Dao.
The jade cauldron’s broth boils, frothing like snowflakes,
nourishing and benefiting the spirit’s flesh.
Vacuous and white, resplendent and fair,
soft and weak, floating and light—
entering water, one does not drown;
treading fire, one does not scorch.
Roaming the great expanse,
passing through mountains and marshes without stumbling.
Embodying perfect clarity,
crossing clouds and mist without hindering one’s gaze.
Beyond the five phases,
before the ten thousand dharmas.
Near and far, intimate and distant,
left and right, one encounters the primal.
The primal division has no beginning,
gazing, one does not see its form.
The Dao attains mysterious essence,
listening, one does not hear its sound.
Neither non-being nor being,
in a single day or ten thousand ages, it does not decay.
Unmoving and unshaken,
it abides in quiescent unity, enduring forever.
Opening and entering it,
no thing remains unordered.
Extending and practicing it,
the Dao is nowhere obstructed.
Communicating with the primal and augmenting qi,
qi augments essence,
essence augments images,
images augment stars.
The stars’ splendor shines brilliantly,
roaming and soaring in the Great Clarity.
Subtle and without superior,
this is called perfect completion.

In praise:
The Great Dao is formless,
ever dwelling in profound obscurity.
At first, the one qi divides,
its pattern received in threefold completion.
Heaven and earth luxuriantly flourish,
the sun and moon brilliantly refine essence.
Spirits intermingle in magnificent radiance,
things shine in perfect clarity.
Yang radiance gathers in the crucible,
yin substance departs from form.
Serene and subtly wondrous,
moved, it communicates with the numinous.
Pure and immaculate,
primal, prosperous, advantageous, and steadfast.
Firm and strong, centered and upright,
soft and yielding, light and clear.
Ascending the mysterious to enter sageliness,
the jade heavens’ luminous stars.

*Inscription on the Gathering Treasure of the Great Mystery of the Upper Clarity*

The *Yin Convergence Scripture* states: "The mechanism lies in the eye."
The Yellow Emperor said: "I do not know that the mechanism lies in the eye."
What does this mean?

The Heavenly Perfected One of the Celestial Truth said: "The Dao that is distant lies beyond the eight wilds, yet the Dao that is near lies between the brows and lashes. Vast, it encompasses heaven and earth; minute, it penetrates the finest hair. Guangchengzi said: 'The spirit’s mechanism moves within, the eyelashes fly like lead.' Thus, the spirit’s mechanism lies in the eye. When the eye’s spirit-light stirs, it resides in the eye. The secret mechanism of the nine heavens emerges from the mechanism before one’s eyes—this mechanism is the transformation of stirring movement. Summoning yang and calling forth yin, grasping the origin’s authority, emerging from clarity and entering the mysterious—thus, the two great corners of the eyes are called the brows. The green cavity ascends, connecting to the mud pill, descending to the two kidneys, which are the gates of mao and you. Kangcangzi said: 'My body harmonizes with the heart, the heart harmonizes with qi, qi harmonizes with spirit, spirit harmonizes with non-being.' There is the sound of *jieran*, the tone of *weiran*. Though distant beyond the eight wilds or near between the brows and lashes, whatever comes to me, I must know it. Yet this is not the awareness of my seven apertures and four limbs, nor the knowledge of my heart, abdomen, and six viscera—it is self-knowing alone."

Liezi said: "Spirit pertains to heaven’s portion, bones and frame to earth’s portion. What belongs to heaven is clear and disperses; what belongs to earth is turbid and gathers. When spirit departs from form, each returns to its truth—this is called *gui*. *Gui* means 'return,' returning to its true dwelling. The true dwelling is the realm of the Great Void."

The Yellow Emperor said: "When spirit enters its gate and bones return to their root, what remains of me?"
The Most High said: "The Dao is empty yet employed, never filling. Profound, it seems the ancestor of the myriad things. Blunting its sharpness, unraveling its tangles, harmonizing its light, merging with its dust. Vast and deep, it seems to abide—yet I know not whose child it is, as it appears before the Lord of Heaven."

Master Lü said: "Gently warming the lead crucible, light penetrates the curtain."
Xu Shenweng’s commentary: "The gentle warmth is the human body. At the initial union of the lead crucible, the spirit-light overflows—closing the eyes, one sees the curtain."
The eye is the eye itself.
Thus, the Master of Pointing to the Mysterious said: "Concentrating spirit in the grotto palace, closing the eyes and lowering the curtain."
The workings of creation contend in haste—this speaks of humans employing spiritual merit to vie with creation, which is the spirit’s use by humans.

Master Haichan’s ode says:
Gently warming the lead crucible into the middle origin,
releasing the three lights to nurture auspicious lotuses.
When the lotus naturally attains the method of sagehood,
step by step, the spirit-light is before the eyes.

Song Qiqiu said: "What the eye does not see, set up a bright mirror to reflect it; what the ear does not hear, set up empty qi to perceive it. Spirit is within me, seeing and hearing are yonder."
He also said: "The bell in the ear, I myself hear it; the flower in the eye, I myself see it. My day and night are its day and night. Thus, day cannot be called bright, nor night called dark. Only the great person can equalize darkness and light."
He also said: "Water, when utterly clear, congeals into ice that is not clear; spirit, when utterly bright, forms a body that is not bright. When ice melts, it returns to clarity; when form disperses, it returns to brightness. One who knows this death can roam the capital of the Most High."

The Fourth Scroll of *Supreme Clarity and Great Mystery Collection* Concludes
The Fifth Scroll of *Supreme Clarity and Great Mystery Collection*
Composed by Gu Shehou Shanxuan

**Seven-Character Quatrains**

At Kunlun’s peak, the fire-dragon soars asunder,
The jeweled banquet’s celestial radiance illumines the Purple Tenuity.
A single grain of numinous cinnabar fuses in splendor—
Only then does one know the Dao’s power wields divine might.

The Jasper Pool’s feast stirs strife, the sun yields its solitude,
Its light shatters the dusty world—nothing remains.
In the vastness of silent emptiness, who is my companion?
The crystal curtain reflects the night-shining pearl.

Golden brilliance, resplendent, auspicious clouds drift,
Luminous and immaculate, flawless as jade.
The two spirits of purity and simplicity merge as one image—
Such is the wondrous skill of the Azure Micro immortal.

A drop of crimson dew bathes the hibiscus,
Nourishing the numinous sprout to emerge anew.
The tender bud unfolds, smiling in the sun’s glow,
Presenting you with a branch of spring in return.

The marvelous and the putrid are but empty names,
In this troubled world, floating and drifting, honor and disgrace startle.
How much better to shed the mortal coil and return to the unbegun,
Than to be bound by the vulgar gaze that scorns the transcendent.

The three-foot dragon-spring sword rings in the night,
Severing evil, slaying demons, it commands numinous efficacy.
Its radiance untainted by the black serpent’s blood,
It soars to the Jasper Heavens, transformed into jade essence.

The two qi converge in the palace, guarding the true yang,
Yang’s light, jewel-bright, advances the mysterious frost.
Giving birth to heaven, giving birth to earth, returning to the primal ancestor,
Alone in the vastness, it mirrors the realm of the Celestial Emperor.

In the silent, empty hall, the door stands half-ajar,
The spirit-light meanders within, distinctly clear.
Though the moon sinks into the Pool of Sun’s Mouth,
A few stars still gleam in the wintry grove.

A blazing sun rises through the sparse woods,
Its luminous qi fills the eyes, joyfully explored.
Awakening to the great completeness, the Dao is lucidly known,
The image of mystery takes flight to the azure heart of heaven.

Without, the armored dragon embraces the Water Palace,
Within, the metal tiger is driven into the Palace of Flame.
Refined into a single substance, purely essence,
It follows the primordial wind of the Celestial Origin.

Sitting beyond the loom of fate, ten thousand cares forgotten,
Within, the heart settles, instantly cooled and clarified.
Yang congeals, substance solidifies, yin vanishes—
Unawares, the spirit roams the Northern Emperor’s realm.

The resolute man’s will is firm and unyielding,
Ready to ascend as an immortal, he answers the celestial examination.
He grasps Mount Zou, shatters Kunlun’s peak,
Scattering the radiant mystery-pearl to merge with the Jade Yang.

With an empty heart, the mind at ease, he awakens to the subtle and serene,
There is yet a higher mechanism of the Mysterious Origin.
Raindrops of the Valley Spirit fly to the Moon Palace,
A sky of starry splendor moistens the lingzhi brows.

Lead and mercury in the golden crucible, auspicious clouds drift,
Refined to perfection, it shines like a luminous sea-pearl.
A single gleaming grain penetrates the dharma-realm,
The nine heavens’ light scatters into the pure void.

The blue dragon and white tiger mate in the crimson furnace,
The Mysterious Female and cinnabar phoenix freely inhale and exhale.
Flaming brilliance of the samadhi fire,
Lucidly illuminating the old paths of darkness.

The two spirits merge in radiance at the center,
Each drop, cool and clear, blends into the Jade Yang.
The mysterious image, resplendent, veils the Jasper Gate,
The Jade Tower’s deep chambers are locked within azure cloud-chambers.

Leisurely riding a white deer to the Jasper Pool,
Awaiting entry to the Moon Palace to pluck the cassia branch.

The Great Brahma, towering, is but an image,
Yet it shifts the stars’ radiance to moisten the lingzhi brows.
The Treasure-Essence Youth plucks the moonflower,
Flames advance, the flying soul releases purple auroras.

Reversing the current beyond the Milky Way,
No need for misty waves to cradle the numinous elixir.
The virtuous elder’s demeanor is foolish,
Within, bloodless, his flesh becomes ice.
Serenely awakened, he returns to the primal image,
Ascending to the Central Heaven to pay homage at the Purple Tenuity.

Brahma-qi lightly drifts, merging with the Emperor’s origin,
The cinnabar’s light, resplendent, shines through the mystery.
The Jade Dawn requires no thatched-hut effort,
Instantly, the empty hurricane grasps the plain sky.

Vast and boundless, the ten thousand images arise anew,
The Celestial Origin’s single qi blends with the pure void.
The Mysterious Yang’s universal sovereign contains the numinous essence,
All transforms without remainder into five-colored pearls.

Black mercury and red lead transmute into jade essence,
Moistening the brows with golden splendor, illuminating the mysterious essence.
In the wintry grove, the sacred cassia and numinous cinnabar congeal,
Rough jade scatters, scattering auspicious stars.

Grasping firmly, preserving the spirit, entering the wondrous mechanism,
A man’s single-minded resolve never wavers.
Refining the Celestial Crucible, the heart-pearl bursts forth,
The snow-capped youth treads the Jade Stream.

Black waters and crimson auroras illuminate the azure sky,
The blue dragon and white tiger enter the abyss of perception.
They swallow the sea-bottom’s numinous turtle marrow,
Advancing the armor-clad black pearl, round and gleaming.

The arrayed tripods’ souls wander, merging with the Great Azure,
The azure vault crackles, flames soaring.
The Three Origins are securely sealed, returning to the Qian image,
The vast secret, boundless, enters the great square.

Auspicious qi and propitious clouds fill the eyes,
A sky of true refinement transforms the cinnabar infant.
The numinous wind does not follow the willow floss away,
It flies into the Palace of Flame to accompany the morning star.

Emerging from the Yang Pass, he travels the old road,
Listening freely, gazing in all directions.
The essence-jewel is not made to occupy mud and dust,
It pierces the long sky, a single point of clarity.

The primordial current of chaos, Brahma-qi ascends,
The sun of celestial wisdom shines most distinctly.
In stillness, a single mirror—by whose power?
The mysterious pearl descends, dazzling the Great Clarity.

Heavenly wind and sea-sun radiate in splendor,
Above and below, molten gold scatters jewel-crystals.
Knocking on the Dao, vast and luminous,
Shifting the spirit’s radiance, the eyes awaken.

Brahma-qi circulates, blending the hundred rivers,
A single glance from the majestic eyes ripples the numinous mist.
Pillowing on cloudy mountains, dreaming the Huaxu dream,
Not desiring to slumber in the Chang’an marketplace.

The red sun half-embraces the emerald mountains,
A wisp of azure mist lightly veils the water’s gleam.
The brocade-scaled fish are not hooked, returning empty-handed—
What use is a thousand-foot silk line?

Breaking through the sea-gate to seek the formless,
Piercing the empty valley to retrieve the mysterious pearl.
The celestial court’s supreme treasure—who is worthy to receive it?
I tell it to the great men of the world.

A drunken man asks, “Forty springs have passed,”
Suddenly awakened, he finds himself in a dream.
Forgetting form, there is naturally a path through the heavens,
Ascending to the Southern Palace, ranked among the jade stars.

In the silent, empty hall, the door stands half-closed,
Green peaches and red apricots emerge from the sparse fence.
Beyond the southern window, a pillow in the spring breeze—
Not like Zhuang Zhou’s butterfly dream.

The mist at the granary’s corner disperses, the red sun gleams,
The mist at the river’s edge clears, the azure sky shines.
The carefree scholar, his heart unburdened,
The snow-capped transcendent, his eyes bright.

Last night, sitting alone as the night deepened,
Guarding the inner elixir furnace, the four limbs at ease.
No wonder the sparse shadows beyond the curtain are white—
The moonflower visits, illuminating the jade.

The Qian Origin and Great Simplicity wondrously embrace the vast,
Refining the substance, flowing gold, purple qi arises.
At home, the auspicious youth smiles in the sun’s glow,
For whom does the sky’s scenery shine?

The vermilion gate opens to wondrous revelation, the azure grotto unfolds—
Five numinous immortals roam at will.
Dragon smoke coils into a thousand poems,
Amber cups brim with a hundred draughts.

In fleeting trance, the soul wanders the Great One’s abode,
Clouds and mist swirl like flying dragons and serpents.
Since the descent of celestial omens, who in the world has known?
Ten thousand drops of flowing essence merge with the splendor of things.

Far reaching to the Jasper Heavens, yet near as one’s brows,
The image bears celestial substance, wondrously pure and subtle.
Once I traced the traces back to the Primordial Ancestor,
The vast Brahman void transformed into jade and rainbow.

Though the body withers and the heart turns to ash, the will remains steadfast,
Embracing the spirit, guarding the One, one attains distant years.
Longevity need not mean lingering in the world—
Beyond lies a realm of gourd-bound sun and moon.

How can an earthen cauldron boil the golden elixir to froth?
The bottomless stone pool blends the ceaseless flow.
Heaven-shaking waves surge past Ox and Dipper,
Alone I steer a single-leaf skiff through the void.

The deluded, benighted child curls inward,
Yet the sea’s eye gazes outward, bright and clear.
Wandering the cinnabar heavens, the essence glistens,
Azure pupils faintly perceive the pale light’s chill.

Sleeping at night and stirring at dawn, both states forgotten,
Gradually the harmonious qi rises above and below.
The horn of dawn half-contains the gleaming red sun,
A range of brow-like mountains clears the azure sky.

Last night at the third watch, the moonlight was fresh,
The old path to the Jade Empyrean remained unchanged.
Opening wide my gaze across a thousand miles,
All phenomena arise from the single round mirror.

Auspicious cinnabar light scatters, illuminating the azure void,
Lead’s radiance, speck by speck, moistens the lingzhi brows.
The numinous youth, inclined toward the Yang abode,
Yet follows the phoenix carriage to the phoenix tower in flight.

Binding mercury, congealing lead, refining jade and rainbow,
The flesh transforms, bloodless, the countenance star-like.
With a single transcendent leap, ascending to heaven,
The imperial throne relies on the true wind and the Dao’s mighty power.

All gloom before the eyes transforms into Yang,
Within the cinnabar tripod, lead frost emerges.
The black serpent inverts to drink the blue dragon’s blood,
The image, formless, spits forth light in the night.

From time immemorial, all has been guest dust—
What thing constitutes the celestial truth?
Disciples toil in vain with their visits,
Seeking to see the present, yet failing to see the man.

Waves rise on Kun Mountain, stirring the Jasper Pool,
Blowing open jade flowers that scatter everywhere.
The vast void shimmers with auspicious hues,
Essence flows forth, dispersing through the Nine Purities.

Earthly po, heavenly po, sun and moon essence,
True Yang blazes resplendently bright.
Within the swirling divine wind, the Three Qi return,
Thrice reborn, a single star revives.

To refine and preserve, first master the six emotions,
With a start, guard simplicity—thus the Dao is born.
Who knows the flavor of Feather Mountain’s wind?
Clouds depart, heartless, yet the moon shines clear.

The Three Origins’ divine radiance, qi unbroken,
Five-colored jasper blossoms illuminate the Nine Heavens.
Heavenly omens merge into the True One’s image,
The mysterious image soars into the Great Clarity’s abyss.

The fiery furnace blazes, flames soaring,
The seething tripod surges with jade nectar.
The elixir’s fortune fills the eyes with splendor,
Myriad spirits harmonize, naturally pure and cool.

North’s darkness and South’s cinnabar each have their time,
The two spirits swiftly grasp heaven’s mechanism.
Together they devise to repay the chaos of death,
Sevenfold return, perfect communion, transcending old hearsay.

Thick mists and demonic vapors pierce the gall with chill,
In the dark, the black egg emerges from the mud pill.
A divine wind sweeps through the celestial strife,
The shadow-bearing light leaves no bloodstains.

The grotto’s true radiance merges with the pure void,
The resplendent golden elixir shines through the nine thoroughfares.
Having united the fetal spirit into one body,
Within it contains the numinous essence, birthing the mysterious pearl.

Layer upon layer of thin mist clears the cinnabar empyrean,
The cinnabar empyrean’s path is not distant.
Where earth meets heaven amid fragrant grasses,
A divine wind returns, transforming jade and lingzhi sprouts.

The stainless pure void, daily renewed,
Illuminates the heavenly summit, startling the soul.
Suddenly, unawares, form is forgotten,
Far off, striking the numinous Yang, passing the sea gate.

The Dao’s mystery is mystery upon mystery,
Mysteriously pervading, touching the realm before birth.
The cinnabar phoenix blows through the shooting-star eyes,
Flying into the Flourishing Yang and Great Unity’s heaven.

A wisp of rosy mist pierces the purple haze,
Yu’s remnant wind stills, grasses lush.
The sun’s soul foresees the numinous splendor,
Breaking through the cinnabar mound to reveal the sky.

Leaning on a pine, I ascend to gaze at Jade Flower Peak,
Towering, tier upon tier, hundreds of folds.
Moon’s po and sun’s hun inquire of each other,
Between them, above and below, the youthful countenance.

The toad’s radiance, bright and clear, pours into the Silver River,
Illuminating the cosmos with its vast, luminous qi.
Refining the po, enhancing the po, clarifying the Great Simplicity,
Transforming into immortals who ascend heaven’s net.

Northward, the misty waters dark and deep,
Pouring into the fiery palace of the Red Emperor’s realm.
Thus the waves calm, the dragon sleeps soundly,
Black lead wholly transforms into purple gold frost.

The dragon’s abyss in the watery realm reflects the sea pearl,
In the night’s darkness, the world’s mirror gleams like jade lard.
The carefree immortal’s twin pupils shine,
Just as the moon goddess ascends the Azure Capital.

Phoenix marrow and dragon fat perfume the land,
Brilliantly congealing, illuminating the encircling eyes.
Beyond the clear pupils, the spirit’s hues divide,
A single golden elixir shines in the Great Clarity.

Within the profound, deeper mysteries lie,
Beyond the heavens, more heavens arise.
Gazing upward, ever more distant, boundless,
Unawares, the soul flies beyond the Image Lord.

Silent and dim, the Dao incomplete,
Splitting open the chaos to reveal the double mystery.
Naturally mastering the Nine and Five, concealing all functions,
The soul soars, distant, through the eighteen heavens.

The Dao of nature is originally formless,
Clinging to this formlessness is but a borrowed name.
Recognize the single wheel of crystal sun,
Through the mysterious, one begins to perceive the Great Void’s clarity.

The Great Mystery’s vast grotto conceals the numinous treasure,
The Supreme’s emptiness hides the inner truth.
To know what the original truth is—
Not spirit, yet spirit, therefore spirit.

I originally idly chant poems of heaven,
Do not confuse them with inferior methods in wild guesses.
To you, I point directly to the path of cultivating truth—
The Dao connects to the numinous pupils, near as your brows.

Parting the cold mist to reveal the azure vault,
The sea’s moon clears the sky, all phenomena interpenetrate.
Standing alone in the vast, who is my match?
The cinnabar infant wanders, borne by the heavenly wind.

The divine wind, ceaseless, breaks through the cloud blossoms,
Washing the frosty heavens, the atmosphere pure.
Only then does the jade peak’s solitary moon gleam,
Piercing the mysterious tripod, suddenly awakening.

In former years, benighted, the heart’s source was closed,
Today, the Dao’s eye opens, clear and bright.
Delighted to see the azure sky like a jade table,
The twin millstones grind through the white cloud banks.

Turning the mysterious pass, the qi’s aspect returns,
The numinous crow flies past, the azure heavens open.

A single truth suddenly illumines both eyes bright,
Recognize the morning sun’s precious mirror-platform.
One millstone refines the sun’s light through the cosmos,
Two points of primordial essence radiate the valley spirit.

The precious mirror enhances the numinous, Heavenly Water flourishes,
Jade blossoms bloom across the Jade Capital’s spring.
The Jade Clarity, Primordial Beginning, Great Lofty Heaven—
Its majestic qi emerges before the Emperor’s advent.

Within the Purple Tenuity’s golden gates it unfolds,
The cinnabar infant wanders, countenance resplendent.
The sun-essence youth appears luminous,
Feathered canopy and jade blossoms veil the purple mist.

Thereby attaining the mysterious yang to open the precious mirror,
The jade star flies into the Grand Clarity’s abyss.
Twin blades of frost-edged swords gleam on Mount Taihua,
Cleaving the heavens’ crown to admit dragon-sand.

Ten thousand points of cinnabar yang, pure and refined,
All belong to the Primordial Lord’s Purple Mansion.
Vast qi and harmonizing wind penetrate the azure window,
Suddenly worldly traces merge with true yang.

In profound unity, all scheming ceases,
Responsibility and mutual radiance dispel ghosts of themselves.
Golden splendor clear, jade blossoms fly,
Cinnabar flowers flourish, purple clouds return.

Twin lads gather herbs beyond the cold stream,
Whether attained or not—who can know?
Divine work has its method to refine the elixir knife,
The lead crucible gently warmed by subtle fire.

No need for breath or forceful effort,
The flame furnace naturally bears snowflake blossoms.
Washing away worldly dust, ten thousand cares settle,
Shifting spirit into the sea to transform the cinnabar infant.

The Hua-Yuan immortal calls out in greeting,
Laughing, pointing toward the jade capital deep in clouds.
Twin phoenixes welcome the immortal into emerald haze,
Purple mist softly rises, illuminating crimson robes.

Where jade towers stir fragrant winds,
Golden flowers are blown aloft in flight.
Shifting spirit, stepping alone into the pure void,
Luminous purity of the void leaves no speck of dust.

Exchanging the drill for the agate casket, essence refines day by day,
Piercing the heart’s crucible to illumine the ice-pot.
Within, the true nature is clear; without, the mysterious is communicated,
Only when the mysterious illuminates the yang pass does the Dao begin.

Inner and outer awaken, jade-like clarity resplendent,
Intertwined radiance flies upward to Jade Capital Mountain.
Penetrating insight reveals the numinous jade, phenomena dissolve,
The primordial chaos directly flourishes, seizing the heavenly wind.

A single stream from Kunlun’s western waters
Pours into the icy abyss ten thousand fathoms deep.
Releasing a single point of primordial chaos’ essence,
It aids the dark yin and yang, illuminating the unseen.

Were it not the jade infant wandering the Purple Mansion,
How could the numinous palace encounter the Three Stars?
Cleaving open chaos to reveal dragon-light,
Entering and exiting vermilion gates to receive cassia frost.

Thereby attaining the five spirits to clarify the Grand Simplicity,
A single grain of golden elixir seizes heaven’s constancy.
The cinnabar phoenix toils, descending cassia branches,
The Jade Pool’s waters are sipped all day.

Released from the dual gates’ intent,
A single transformation of the mysterious pearl ascends the Great Lofty.
Numinous sound emerges from the distant and obscure,
A waft of fragrant wind enters the dream, clear.

Expounding the twin gates to connect the ancient Dao,
In the Jade Empyrean, one meets the Lesser Micro Star.
Screening away worldly dust, ten thousand affairs vanish,
Only in nothingness is the primordial chaos pearl seen.

Where does the vanished form, altered image return?
Softly, following the wind, it ascends the Jade Capital.
Gazing upward, the mysterious is revealed in the azure realm,
Flowing bells cast fire into the center.

A single point of cavernous origin, the heavenly wind flourishes,
Benefiting my three yin to transform into nine yang.
Cultivation requires exerting deadly effort,
Exchanging substance to retain the true, embodying the Great Nothingness.

The waning soul benefits the spirit in the golden banquet hall,
The cavernous mysterious returns to illumine the Jade Clarity Capital.
Jasper plum blossoms first unfurl with the east wind,
Drifting ethereally, connecting every place in the human realm.

Like the moon goddess departing her precious palace,
Just as the immortal enters the dragon palace.
Who has seen the Jade Pool’s jade-spring rinse,
Where ringing chimes startle the soul, first shocking heaven?

The yang soul pursues the flowing bell-fire to its end,
At night, the Lesser Micro Star awakens the plain mysterious.
Not desiring to scheme in the world of dust,
The carefree crane-nature recalls its eastern journey.

At the Dao’s gate, one realizes few know the tune,
Only the numinous Kunlun remains as before.
Strolling by chance to the Southern Palace to visit the Emperor’s return,
Sword-light flies past, shattering the precious mountain.

Alas for the countless eyes of mortals,
Who do not recognize Penglai’s board or Yuan’s go-between.
Heaven’s concealment, the true wind’s brilliance,
Within, it enfolds dragon-light, flying over the sea.

The golden cavern’s beauty, triple-layered mist,
The jade spirit’s grace, the twofold patterns’ harmony.
A single wheel of bright moon illumines the pure subtle,
The water realm’s divine forest reflects the jade stream.

Bracing air pierces the bones with crystalline clarity,
The Milky Way still bathes its icy flesh.
In the zhi-hall, feathered guests discuss the true mechanism,
Directly pointing to the jade heavens, the path unobscured.

Clear eyes unclouded by veiling mists,
In the Jade Empyrean’s banquet, one’s countenance shines like a star.
Sun and moon revolve, heaven and earth gleam,
Divine light intertwines, the Great Void brightens.

Those who attain this observe its wonders,
Easily meeting the heavenly wind to fill the realm with purity.
Transforming customs, shifting winds to emerge from worldly passions,
A single point of cool constancy, profoundly clear.

Containing light, silently merging with heaven’s substance,
Only then does one trust the divine work, the Dao’s awakening.
Cleaving open chaos to reveal the golden crow’s nest,
Striking through Kunlun’s ridge to the jade hare’s gate.

No need for twin pupils to illumine the dharma-realm,
Thus a single eye suffices to illumine heaven and earth.
The Grand Mystery pure, moon blossoms fly,
The Limitless radiant, moon essence returns.

Orchids and zhi flourish by the jade stream,
Who knows the divine work’s gathering?
Divine skill is reaped—who can know?

**Five-Character Verse**

Shattering Kunlun’s peak,
True essence enters the distant obscure.
A single furnace of phoenix marrow,
Two crucibles of red dragon essence.

Five mountains’ auspicious clouds arise,
Three peaks’ auspicious qi is born.
Opening the heavenly eye to illumine,
The cosmos expands, clear and bright.

Tigers roar, wind stirs the ravine,
Dragons chant, mist fills the horizon.
Auspiciousness floats, the pure realm scatters,
Flames blaze, the azure heavens open.

A single horse enters the gold mine,
Twin wheels grind the jade mounds.
The profound image seeks only me,
Intent remains on Mount Tiantai.

The silver toad emerges from the plain forest,
Descending to cover the Qujiang’s heart.
Bright, bright star river fades,
Clear, clear the sea of awakening deepens.

A single roar of the mighty tiger,
Ten thousand ravines’ female dragons chant.
Startled, the numinous pupils glance,
Intertwined radiance, jade questions gold.

Sitting in solitude, freely roaming,
Ashen, things arise of themselves.
After the ninth of the scorching season,
At noon, striking the third watch.

The wooden horse emerges from fire,
The clay ox treads beneath the water.
Unknowing the inverted intent,
Having eyes, yet blind as can be.

The Grand Supreme’s Mysterious Origin Ancestor,
Born during the vast kalpa’s time.
Heaven and earth’s bright steward,
Sun and moon’s alternating support.

Vastly bestowing benevolent virtue,
Majestically expounding great compassion.

Lord of the Myriad Heavens, Master of All Teachings,
Teacher of Emperors through the ages.
Ascending the Mysterious, feasting in Cassia Groves,
Jade blossoms blanket the Five Shadows.

Moon’s reflection, Azure Lads at play,
Within clouds, the Cinnabar Phoenix chants.
Mists disperse, the Star River pales,
Essence congeals, auspicious radiance deepens.

Where Flying Immortals roam and soar,
Reclining in banquet at the Azure Sky’s heart.
Vast, the Great Luo Heaven,
Within the Mysterious, yet more Mysterious.

Beyond the Three Realms’ dim vastness,
Before the Five Phases’ fleeting blur.
Above and below, all-pervading,
Transcending things, ever foremost.

To seek its end is endless,
Eternally alone, unbroken.
The Primordial Qi unites with the Sage’s mechanism,
The Supreme Dao is beyond thought or conjecture.

Sun’s sea gathers radiant essence,
Star River glows with emerald light.
Dragons soar from jade-green cliffs,
Tigers stride forth from icy streams.

Alchemical cinnabar perfected through transformation,
Together they pay homage to the Purple Tenuity.
Treading the void, entering the Central Lands,
Gracefully feasting on immortal blossoms.

The Northern Emperor veils in mist and haze,
The Southern Darkness unfurls rosy clouds.
Golden Lads uphold the precious mirror,
Jade Maidens scatter blossoms of jade.

Striking the cold moon with sidelong notes,
Numinous sounds pierce the imperial halls.
Awakening within the Ancient Tone Pavilion,
Ashen-hearted, ten thousand cares grow clear.

Wind stirs, the pure dream awakens,
Moonlight illumines the drunken soul’s return.
The Red Emperor departs the golden crucible,
The Azure Lad enters the precious vase.

Twin essences grasp the Great Image,
Together they transform into the Lesser Light stars.
Wind stills, heaven and earth grow quiet,
Clouds withdraw, sky and land grow bright.

Clear, clear the autumn moon’s purity,
Limpid, limpid the pristine waves’ clarity.
Precious cassia preserves the Three Natures,
Jade groves scatter the Five Stars.

Jade constellations surge with snow-white waves,
Roaming feasts in the Crystal City.
The Great One embraces the True Image,
The Numinous Terrace flourishes with jade-like form.

Essence-toad congeals on jade-green cliffs,
Yang unites with the Supreme Frost Orchid.
The Benevolent Sun transforms the Cinnabar Pool,
The Dark Moon waxes in full reflection.

Within the Three Flowers’ vessel, beauty blooms,
Veils part to reveal the mirror’s countenance.
Bathing, the fragrant flesh gleams,
Gathering essence, the Daoist scriptures unfold.

At the sacred altar, jade chimes resound,
In the immortal gardens, void-treading voices rise.
Precious talismans soar to the heavens,
Starlight descends to the Grand Clarity.

Upon the Jade Empyrean’s golden tablets,
Each one bears an immortal’s name.
Seated alone beneath the pine’s shade,
Flowing springs drip upon pendant jades.

Sword-light flashes at the sun’s corner,
Cold mists cascade from the celestial court.
Jade Maidens wander in the imperial gardens,
Golden Lads feast upon Crimson City.

Perfected Ones ride white elephants,
Appearing at dawn before the Purple Tenuity star.
Chaos splits into the Two Modes,
Suddenly revealing the Great Void.

Frosty skies congeal the precious mirror,
Cold dew drips upon lotus blossoms.
The Formless seeks the gleaming pearl,
Essence-jade plucks the choicest red.

Spiritual communion, numinous jade shines,
Light penetrates the Jade Flask’s heart.
The Jade Pivot follows the Dipper’s turn,
Golden Millet circulates divine power.

Sea isles, dragons chant in mist,
Heaven’s origin, tigers roar in wind.
Starry jade, the celestial bones gleam,
Wisdom’s illumination, the sun’s crown glows red.

Blending principles, the Three Pure Ones grow clear,
Intertwined radiance shoots into the Precious Palace.
Blue lotuses float on emerald pools,
Yellow cranes descend to secluded courtyards.

Water valleys, cloud roots grow still,
Jade heavens, the atmosphere grows pure.
Within emptiness, zither notes resound,
Beyond the clear sky, snowflakes shine bright.

Wisdom’s illumination scatters in misty swirls,
Numinous lads ascend the Jade Capital.
The Mysterious Cavern opens the precious mirror,
Jade gates illuminate the golden pool.

Shedding form, roaming the celestial soar,
Nurturing spirit, entering the Grand Tenuity.
Heaven and earth alternate in closure and opening,
Sun and moon naturally follow.

The heart’s crucible blooms with jade flowers,
Numinous light blazes with the sun’s brilliance.
A single awakening to the Supreme Mystery’s mechanism,
Kunlun’s ridge arrays the Two Modes.

The Black Pearl gleams over sea isles,
The Formless illuminates the heavenly pool.
Snow-white waves simmer golden liquid,
Cloudy billows transform jade-like flesh.

Forgetting form, the heart rests beyond,
Roaming and soaring, transforming into dragon and *kui*.
**Six-Character Quatrain**
Mysterious essence emerges from all kinds,
Illusion dissolves, auspiciousness refines the exceptional.
Supreme principles transform customs and shift winds,
Evolving transformations, numinous yang’s celestial omens.

Vast, vast, the Dao’s Ancestor of the Ten Directions,
Majestic, majestic, sole honored one of the Three Realms.
Delivering and guiding souls to receive the ordination,
Revealing this Primordial Beginning’s exhortation.

The Dao of the Grand Clarity, distant and boundless,
Divine power, vast and without limit.
A single point of numinous light appears,
Ascending the Mysterious, roaming the Cinnabar Heaven.

Upon the azure sea, cassia lightly floats,
From the pure source, jade blossoms drift forth.
Flying lads reveal these wondrous principles,
Mysterious numina ascend, mounting rosy clouds.

The Primordial Beginning, Emperor of the One, prior to heaven,
Exhortations receive the mandate of the profound Mystery.
Precious blessings, the cinnabar phoenix’s path smooth,
Within the Jade Constellation Palace, immortals take flight.

Azure screens, the sun’s soul illumines the Mysterious,
Between brows, wisdom’s mirror penetrates essence.
The Three Origins’ Yellow Assistants soar in tandem,
The Pristine Heaven’s singular hue, pure wind.

Sunlight illumines the dark and bright, aiding the cavernous,
Wind blows, splitting the crown, opening heaven.
The entire land, dragon-light advances in splendor,
Divine power, two wings hover and circle.

Last night, clouds gathered, rain ceased,
Revealing jade peaks and the precious moon.
Numinous flight blends into the Middle Origin,
Myriad streams of yang-light shine through.

Kunlun’s mountain, a spring of golden water,
Circulating, rippling forth jade waves.
The original nature fills where emptiness dwells,
The profound Mystery reverses course, ascending the Star River.

Wondrous! The Jade Cavern’s eternal spring,
Within it, immortals roam and soar.
Transforming nature, golden halls’ feathered guests,
Forgetting form, sending off the old, welcoming the new.

The Supreme Dao gives birth to heaven and earth,
Midstream, the sun and moon pass through fullness.
Evolving transformations, the four seasons form images,
Blending into one nature, lofty and bright.

The Dao, vast without boundary or limit,
Spirit roams the expansive desert’s realm.
Gazing afar, celestial light blazes,
Great indeed, the Perfect Power’s true auspice.

**Seven-Character Full Poem**
Returning the two things, washing away deep confusion,
At *mao* and *you*, knocking open the *wu* and *ji* gates.
Beneath the turtle’s base, cold ashes rekindle flame,
Before Kunlun’s ridge, withered trees gradually grow roots.

Within the womb-born crucible, auspicious smoke shrouds,
In the infant’s furnace, auspicious qi surges.
Having attained the myriad spirits’ return to mother and child,
Then offer the one thing to the Primordial Honored One.

With you, I directly reveal the root’s source,
Wondrous transformations, the numinous mechanism lies before your eyes.
Pouring forth pristine waves, piercing the universe’s corners,
Unleashing red flames, filling the entire cosmos.

Pure essence, a singular hue, rivers and mountains flourish,
Vast qi, united with the origin, scenery grows fresh.
The Dao’s power relies on wisdom’s illumination,
Understanding this single method seizes immortals’ authority.

Silent, the yielding feminine guards the Great Male,
The Great Male, bursting forth, emerges from the vaulted sky.
Circulating, sun and moon conceal heaven and earth,
Flowing, essence and flower fill the Great Void.

Laozi awakened to this, becoming the Jade Image,
The Tathāgata attained this, verifying the Golden Countenance.

Since I encountered the Mysterious Origin,
Its transmission has spread everywhere among people.
In tranquil, true joy, far from recklessness,
A single cloud-heart refines the Nine Suns.

From heaven descends the Fire Dragon, roaming the sea’s depths,
From earth rises the black mist, entering the vaulted sky.
Golden Elixir flies forth from the Primordial Ancestor,
The Jade Image returns to the homeland of Dao and virtue.

Should you wish to know the true marvels of the Mysterious Origin,
Within the Five Thousand Words, ponder them in detail.
Rolling forth from Fusang, the sun’s single wheel,
Its radiant, blazing flames illuminate the Void.

Within the Qian-Yuan cauldron, the Fire of Li is added,
In the Taiyi furnace, the Wind of Xun arises.
The refined Golden Elixir soars through the cosmos,
The forged Great Joy emerges from the vaulted sky.

Divine transformations transcend a thousand kalpas,
Ascending Kunlun’s first peak.
Silent and desolate, the myriad forms dissolve into emptiness,
Within the void, dimly discerned, divine powers appear.

The moon in the endless sky is neither round nor incomplete,
The primordial wind neither moves nor sways.
Moonlight shines, yet Li Lou’s eyes lose their sight,
The wind blows, and Shi Kuang’s ears forget their keen hearing.

Through refined thought, the divine and sagely work grows refined,
Greatly revealing the Mysterious Origin’s supreme achievement.
Once parted from homeland and kin, forsaking the six relations,
Heart like cold ashes, form withered, escaping the clamor of dust.

The Azure Youth daily presents treasures within the text,
The Red Child constantly replenishes the cauldron’s precious contents.
Clouds and waters, Mount Jing’s empty appearances,
Post roads and merchant travels weary the spirit in vain.

Spirit roams the eight directions, riding the empty chariot,
In another realm, the Purple Palace blooms with spring.
Beyond the misty forest, the ancient pavilion of echoes,
Gibbons cry in the haze, awakening from drunkenness.

At midnight, through parted curtains, the sparse moon gleams white,
At dawn, beyond the window, the drifting wind is clear.
Pure as the jade zither’s chill beyond the world,
Resonant as the jade pendants’ sound amid the clouds.

Not a speck of dust remains, the starry eyes gleam bright,
The Flying Youth pierces the great Orchid City.
The Immortal of the Northern Darkness pays homage to Fuxi,
The path smooth, the Cinnabar Phoenix enters the Emperor’s realm.

Scattering auspicious jade blossoms, they reach the Sun Palace,
Gathering rosy clouds, the golden mirror shines in the Hall of Light.
Form shifts, shadow turns, transcending the Three Realms,
Things change, stars flow, emerging from the four directions.

Penetrating earth and heaven, yet nothing remains,
Solitary, a single point illuminates the center.
Without fasting rituals or scripture study,
Refining true essence enters the Great Vehicle.

In heaven’s furnace, the Red Phoenix’s marrow,
Between the brows, two cauldrons of Black Tortoise essence.
Yang’s light illuminates, piercing dark valleys,
Vast qi surges into the profound, entering the distant void.

Self and other both forgotten, the whole body manifests,
The work complete, one is ranked among the Nine Celestial Stars.
The solitary peak of Mount Mei, locked in cloudy blossoms,
A single path of mindfulness dissolves the form.

Two streams of pure light pierce the azure vault,
A single wisp of blue mist pours into the cold courtyard.
Osmanthus blossoms push forth, the spirit refreshed,
Luminous qi clears the forms, making them bright.

The twin luminaries’ intersecting light dazzles the heavens,
The Five Spirits’ immortals may ascend.
Worldly affairs and dusty passions, swept away with a single sword,
The divine wind’s mighty power matches the Mysterious Mechanism.

The sun’s essence and moon’s spirit penetrate the hexagrams,
Wood’s fluid and metal’s essence transform Kan and Li.
Riding phoenix wings through the Nine Bends of the river,
Embracing the dragon, soaring above the Three Mountains’ peaks.

Silently paying homage to the Lord of Images, returning to the transformations of Chen,
Swiftly driving the jade heavens, the path never lost.
The Mysterious Pass moves in and out, operating the pivot,
Dividing yin and yang, establishing the Two Modes.

Before the Taiyi Kun, the Jade Hare dashes,
Atop Kunlun’s summit, the Golden Rooster takes wing.
Within the Western River’s waves, red brocade unfurls,
From the Eastern Sea’s billows, the White Tortoise emerges.

Spitting forth auspicious light, the heart-cauldron shines,
The divine elixir advances in splendor, piercing the heavens in flight.
The celestial essence melts, nourishing the Seven Treasures’ body,
At ease, one never loses their true nature.

Two wisps of blue mist return to the Source Sea,
A single streak of light illuminates the Valley Spirit.
Often taking this mechanism to guide the superior person,
Always using the Supreme Dao to refine the stubborn vessel.

Fellow disciples, grasping the poem’s essence,
May also become carefree, idle individuals.

**Inscription of the Three Sages (Two Chapters)**

The Three Sages’ rule begins with the Dao as foremost.
Beyond affairs, how can it be natural?
Opening the *Book of Zhou*, "silent and unmoving,"
Illuminating the hexagrams and images, "stirred, they penetrate the Mysterious."

Delving into Buddhist scriptures, forgetting the finger pointing at the moon,
Awakening to perfect clarity, this may be called Chan.
Perusing the *Dao and Virtue*, "the Valley Spirit does not die,"
The profound Feminine, "entering and exiting, ceaselessly."

Wandering beyond the dust and grime,
Unfettered, before the Great Ultimate.
All streams, when gathered, return to the sea,
The myriad forms, when arrayed, all belong to heaven.

**Another Chapter**

Of old, the two masters opened my sacred text,
Uttering a single truth, unlocking the primordial chaos,
Expounding the Two Modes, splitting open Qian and Kun.

The great sound, why should it be confined to notes?
The great image, not bound by blue and black.
Pursuing Zhuangzi, attaining the formless net,
Measuring Guanzi, approximating the forgotten fish-trap.

Embodying the Tathāgata, awakening to the wondrous essence,
Exalting Laozi, exploring the profound mystery.
Profound! Profound!
Without beginning, without end,
Neither self nor other.
Beyond the images of the Five Phases,
Emerging before the myriad transformations of the primordial heaven.

Is this empty talk? It rests upon true vision.
Returning to the never-beginning,
Eternally enduring.

**Another Ode**

Heaven hangs its round image like an ice wheel,
Luminous and pure, without a speck of dust.
Twelve Jade Lads support the purple decree,
The August Emperor commands me to drink the Elixir of Eternal Spring.

**A Seven-Character Poem with Hidden Meaning**

Unadorned, the yellow-crowned visage, simple and profound,
Pearls strung with branches of red agate’s breath.
By what means is the transformation discerned? A snowflake’s hidden core,
Beneath the clam, beyond the flesh, twin pearls gleam.

A single gourd requires the dragon’s red path,
Upon the ice, mercury congeals, lead refines the golden crucible.
Great Zhang’s immortal queries, twelve odes in four-character verses.

**Supreme Clarity**

Within Supreme Clarity, undivided and whole,
The Primordial Ancestor, revered by all sages.
The Great Mystery, the Way of Great Mystery,
Ascends to the Primordial Palace.
Pure yang and true wisdom,
Wondrous transformations without end.

A single celestial path,
Two routes diverge as one.
The Jade Infant’s divine metamorphosis,
Reveals the visage of the lofty perfected.

The true realm of Penglai,
Where earth flourishes in eternal spring.
Roaming the azure screen in spirit,
One awakens to the celestial truth.

Within purity,
Nurturing the primordial spirit.
The numinous light illumines all,
The truth of the Great Ultimate.

Earthly po and celestial hun,
Above and below merge as one.
Formed into the supreme treasure,
Eternally enduring through kalpas.

The Dao is formless and vast,
Firmly nurturing the divine spirit.
A thousand truths converge,
Ten thousand sages find peace.

Yin po and yang hun,
Sun and moon in pursuit.
Piercing through the earthly gate,
Breaking open the celestial portal.

Sun and moon radiant,
Heaven and earth in harmonious fullness.
Unfurling the Dao-eye,
The whole is perfectly rounded.

Two infants,
Embrace the pure wind.
From the wellspring of awakened sea,
They leap into the Dragon Palace.

A spring of golden water,
Two rivers of silver.
The abyssal flow runs clear,
Rippling with numinous waves.

The crescent moon furnace opens,
Stirring forth jadelike plum blossoms.
Transformed into divine beings,
The immortal embryo takes form.

**Sixteen Five-Character Odes in Response to Marshal Wei’s Queries**

**Celestial Treasure**
A fragment of celestial treasure,
Gathered into the Crimson Palace.
Assembled into the canopy of the mystic moon,
It blankets the winds of my lineage.

**Following the Moment**
Perceiving the true nature in all things,
Without corners, without crookedness or straightness.
Soaring into the Great Void,
Only then does the spirit flourish.

**Utmost Purity**
Utterly pure, silent in purity,
The azure heavens gleam in clarity.
Through the valley, autumn’s waves shimmer,
Profound and deep, entering the ancient capital.

**Utmost Clarity**
Clarity and contention awaken purity,
Within purity, clarity shines.
The primordial Way of the One Heaven,
Unchanging, the Great Void levels all.

**Moon Valley**
Moon Valley illumines the radiant pool,
The silver abyss stretches boundless.
Nine rivers flow full and vast,
A single surge reaches the heavens.

**Auspicious Response**
Virtuous deeds move heaven’s merit,
The spirit roams the Palace of the Northern Emperor.
A pure name resounds across the four seas,
A myriad leagues carry the immortal’s wind.

**Gathering and Dispersing**
Lead and mercury nurture the embryonic immortal,
Soaring in emptiness, standing in vastness.
Parting the summit of the celestial river,
Shattering the crystal heavens.

**Merging Subtleties**
Sun and moon merge in a single bracelet,
The starry river gleams bright and clear.
The Three Primordials shine through to the depths,
A single precious pearl hangs suspended.

**Unfathomable**
The Great Sound is unheard,
The numinous light connects to the Great Subtlety.
Yin and yang cannot exhaust it,
Neither gods nor ghosts can peer into it.

**True Warrior**
The True Warrior visits the Eastern Flower,
The numinous official dwells in his true home.
The black tortoise seeks the watery abode,
Upon its back, a golden serpent coils.

**Application**
Vast and boundless, the Great Void of Dao,
Nurturing my great spiritual power.
Merging and coalescing golden light,
Intertwined as one.

**Concealment and Manifestation**
The Earthly Mansion meets Rāhu,
Straddling the heavens atop a fiery ox.
The sword’s light bears no bloodstain,
Severing the red dragon’s head.

**Heart-Fire**
True fire advances without smoke,
The crucible’s cauldron boils and seethes.
The elixir complete, its radiance outshines the sun,
Crimson flames fill the cosmos.

**Serenity**
In utmost emptiness, the primordial spirit settles,
The numinous brightness reveals the Great Truth.
The light of the Primordial Cavern enters the crucible,
Subtly reflecting the four seasons’ spring.

**Difficulty and Ease**
Entering the Dao is not easy,
Returning to truth is not difficult.
I fear you lack steadfast resolve,
And thus remain distant by a thousand mountains.

**Numinous Brightness**
A single spark of numinous brightness,
Born from the vast kalpa.
Bright as the sun in the heavens,
Radiant as the moon’s blossoming light.

**Marshal Ma’s Queries on Concealment**

**Concealment**
Alone in a thatched hut, concealed,
Silently guarding integrity and purity.
Mercury flows long in the vessel,
Lead sand is replenished in the crucible.

**Forgetting Words**
Attaining meaning as if forgetting words,
Within it, the wondrous mystery is grasped.
Nurturing the spirit, refining the great image,
Cultivating nature, tempering the embryonic immortal.

**The Path of Communication**
The two luminaries illuminate the path,
Preserving the spirit with firm resolve.
A thousand strands of purple mist unfurl,
Ten thousand vibrations of silver radiance spread.

**Ascending as Immortal**
With merit complete, one ascends as immortal,
Soaring beyond the nine heavens.
The simurgh follows to the Purple Palace,
The phoenix leads the way to the Primordial Court.

**Five-Character Full Ode**
**Master He’s Inquiry on Dwelling in the Hermitage**

**Delighting in Forests and Springs**
From youth, I delighted in forests and springs,
In poverty’s dwelling, nurturing vastness.
Nurturing the spirit, preserving unified qi,
Preserving life, cultivating the Three Fields.
Discussing the Dao with friends of true principle,
Conversing on mechanisms, expounding wondrous mystery.
The heart of right and wrong already stilled,
Long have I gazed for the crane soaring to heaven.

**Master Da’s Inquiry on Leaving Home to Enter the Dao**
In years past, lost in wine and lust,
Today I awaken to the Yellow Root.
With intent, I return to the path of truth,
Without longing, I enter my native land.
Jade skies contend in sacred verse,
Golden gates respond to the imperial exam.
Receiving the mandate of celestial immortals,
My spirit roams into the great expanse.

**Han the Second’s Inquiry on Awakening to Return to Truth**
Startled awake from southern branches,
Returning to truth, leaving the river of love.
With empty heart, refining vast qi,
With full belly, tempering harmony.
The crucible lacks lead sand,
The furnace overflows with mercury.
The immortal maiden of the Crimson Palace rages,
Wielding her sword, ascending misty gauze.

**Tian the Immortal Asks of the Great One**
**Mystery’s Origin**
Mystery’s origin births the ancient stem,
The Great One blends with primordial heaven.
Responding to things, a thousand truths arise,
Congealing in emptiness, the power of ten thousand images.
Essence vast, piercing nine paths,
Spirit’s use emerging from three bracelets.
Above, it reaches the realm of no-birth,
Joyfully attaining wondrous mystery.

**For Master Xin of Jigu Valley on Sitting in Meditation**
In a blink, the toad’s eye sits,
Raising brows, the Dao’s eye opens.
Knowing the heart, free from filth,
Recognizing nature, beyond dust.
Moonlight samadhi shines alone,
Lofty, illuminating the eight bounds.
Vast and still, without movement,
Suddenly beholding the Buddha Tathagata.

**Elder Yuan Asks on Sudden Awakening**
Sitting upright, sensing dimness,
Limpid, the Buddha’s eye opens.
Twin forests pierced by the bright moon,
Deer wilds suffused with pure wind.
Auspicious qi coils the golden crucible,
Auspicious smoke inscribes the jeweled palace.
The Great Mystery unfolds the true teaching,
Following transformation, awakening to true emptiness.

**Old Immortal Niu Asks of the Golden Crow’s Descent to Seek Wu and Ji**
The golden crow seeks Wu and Ji,
The jade hare beholds Ren and Geng.
Blending things, the heart-pearl gleams,
Congealing emptiness, the sun of wisdom shines.
Clear and bright, heaven and earth flourish,
Profound and still, the great abyss is pure.
At last perceiving the Qian-Yuan image,
Harmony nurtures the utmost essence.

**Little Immortal Zhang Asks of Yin-Yang’s Creation and Transformation**
Sun and moon soar and descend,
Heaven shakes, turning the Dipper’s stars.
The dragon swallows the golden phoenix’s marrow,
The tiger drinks the jade toad’s essence.
The crucible refines the divine elixir,
The furnace fires the great medicine.
The sick return to unity,
Countless spirits and gods are startled.

**Inscribed for the Hall of Shared Dao**
Gathering together for the purification fast,
Joy fills every heart.
Monks discourse on the path of prajna,
Recluses speak of Penglai.
The great Dao transmits the mind-seal,
The Chan gate reveals dharmata.
Blending all, the bright sun soars,
Its light shining upon the jade terrace.

**In Response to Elder Yu**
Supreme goodness knows no resentment,
Cultivating truth needs no force.
Knowing the heart, harmonizing with vast light,
Attaining the Dao, standing in mystery’s strength.
Illuminating the eye, entering the chamber of spiritual power,
Clarifying emptiness, entering the great azure.
The pearl of doubt contains the moon’s treasure,
In daily use, heaven’s constancy is found.

**Li the Immortal Asks of the Water Crystal Hall in Jing Mountain**
Resplendent, the water crystal hall,
Jade orchids fill the earthen pillars.
White clouds pierce the azure eaves,
Purple mist illumines golden light.
Brilliant, the chamber of congealed spirit,
Radiant, emerging from the grotto.
Had I not traveled to this place,
I would not have awakened to the immortal realm.

**Ten Admonitions for Disciples**
True words are the ultimate secret,
Why fear the judgments of others?
Pointing the way through frozen paths,
Lifting from the pit of karmic fire.
Not seeking the esteem of gentlemen,
Who fears the scorn of petty men?
Silent speech follows heaven’s principle,
Loyal heart transforms all to peace.

To learn the Dao yet cling to home,
Years pass, affairs grow awry.
Mouths boast of purity,
Hearts churn like tangled hemp.
Wine and lust ever increase,
Qi and wealth daily accumulate.
I urge you to awaken early,
Follow me to rest in clouds and mist.

Self and others, too much pride,
In truth, turning to perversity.
Cunning hearts like rhinos and tigers,
Fierce natures like vipers and snakes.
Lust is no path to cultivation,
Greed cannot nurture a family.
These two, how can they be right?
Each step is misaligned.

For years, leaving the sea of desire,
Today, still clinging to splendor.
Inevitably, solitary struggle brings suffering,
Again, entangled in dual bonds.
Unclear about the strange fruit,
Secretly eating winter melon.
Abandoning desire, yet desiring more,
Leaving home, yet entering home.

Lush and enchanting scenery,
Bewitching, the fragrance of jade wrists.
Willow brows, starry eyes like swords,
Tender cheeks, crimson lips like spears.
Brocade curtains become a prison,
Bed curtains erect a execution ground.
Though the head remains unsevered,
Qi is harmed, the hall of essence ruined.

Jealousy breeds resentment,
Lustful lechery lacks benevolence.
All day, lost in wine and lust,
Each day, attached to the red dust.
Guessing dogs ever companions,
Foxes and demons nightly kin.
The heart of lust not yet severed,
How dare one speak of heaven’s truth?

Speaking of soaring dragons,
Walking like limping turtles.
Cultivating mountains, the fruit unripe,
Yet worldly works already accomplished.
Lustful as wild birds,
Lascivious beyond mountain beasts.
Constantly harboring the mind of beasts,
Do not expect heaven and earth’s protection.

Learning the Dao without resolve,
Merely wielding a clever tongue.
Constantly storing the mad mind-horse,
Ever letting the heart-ape falter.
Secretly, the demon of lust,
Publicly, boasting of purity.
Deficient heart, deep karmic retribution,
One day, heaven’s judgment will fall.

Eloquent in expounding wondrous merit,
Yet dwelling amid wine and lust.
Unable to penetrate the sacred teaching,
Establishing one’s own household creed.
Nature stained within the red dust,
Body residing in the fire’s courtyard.
At the brink of danger, a single misstep,
Eternally sinking into the abyss.

Truth, when has it ever been?
Vainly wrestling with vines and creepers.
Knowing oneself a sparrow in the nest,
How can one see the whale or roc?
Short in conduct, boasting of skill,
Failing in merit, parading one’s ability.
Not for excessive flattery and deceit,
Evil karma multiplies ten thousandfold.

All resides in the Primordial Ancestor,
All returns to the Supreme Lord’s school.
Every head receives its mandate,
Every thing connects in mutual resonance.
Encompassing the Qian-Yuan image,
Containing the Great Beginning’s midst.
To exhaustively know the ancient stem,
Inquire at the Palace of Five Clarities.

**Zhang the Sixth of Hezhong Prefecture Asks of Spirit, Qi, and Essence**
Spirit’s light dazzles things to clarity,
Following transformation, revealing true form.
Profound, the azure sky’s moon,
Limpid, the azure vault’s stars.
Fathomless, returning to the Purple Palace,
Vague, entering the Yellow Court.
The utmost sage is unfathomable,
The Dao’s mystery, myriad transformations’ spirit.

At first, the single qi divides,
Following the mechanism, the four seasons flow.

Obscure, heaven and earth enfold,
Silent, the Great Void extends.
Rising and descending divide the pure and turbid,
Floating and sinking determine the ancestral lineage.
All beings endowed with spirit receive their mandate,
No thing is not encompassed.
Chaotic and profound, the essence of darkness,
Intermingling radiance gleams like the sun’s brightness.
The Qian-Yuan knows there is form,
The empty valley reveals the formless.
Pure and concentrated, it congeals in the heart’s crucible,
Yang’s light merges in the precious vase.
Embracing the splendor of heaven and earth,
Resplendent, it illumines Huaqing.

**Presented to Niu, Palace Examination Daoist Name Tonghengzi, Courtesy Name Guoxiang**
Guoxiang presents auspicious splendor,
Virtue and benefit treasure unimpeded passage.
Mist disperses, the golden crow gleams,
Clouds withdraw, the jade hare shines.
The Three Heavens dwell in pure realms,
The Four Seas spread a pristine name.
Virtue and power both complete,
Moving spirit into the imperial capital.

**Ten Poems on Entering Samadhi and Contemplation**

**Utmost Greatness, Pacifying the Heart Contemplation**
Utmost greatness pacifies the heart’s gaze,
Clearly knowing the power of creation.
The sun’s essence pierces through mist,
The moon’s spirit pursues clouds and smoke.
Illuminating the eyes, the heart’s clarity congeals,
Nurturing spirit, blending with things’ essence.
The profound origin’s light gleams brightly,
Comprehending principle, attaining the subtle and mysterious.

**Utmost Vision, Concentrating on Auspicious Contemplation**
Utmost vision concentrates on auspicious sight,
Spirit roams, heaven and earth connect.
The infant departs the moon’s palace,
The maiden enters the celestial palace.
Together they meet within fragrant curtains,
Mutually inviting into brocade canopies.
Seated beneath the crystal screen,
Beholding the jade lotus.

**Awakening to the Primordial Contemplation**
Awakening to the Primordial’s vision,
Bright as the enduring sun and moon.
Subtle and minute, fathomless,
Utmost greatness, wondrous and boundless.
Following transformation, a thousand merits manifest,
Pervading and nourishing the myriad things unfold.
Clearly knowing there is creation,
Who would carefully examine its details?

**Sunrise at Fusang Contemplation**
At sunrise, observing Fusang,
Only then does the Dao’s eye become clear.
Observing heaven, heaven is fundamentally still,
Examining earth, earth is at peace.
Amidst things, there is no lack of form,
Concentrating on emptiness, how could there be shape?
Responding to the moment with correspondence,
The integral whole reveals completion.

**Heart and Eyes Communing with the True Contemplation**
Heart and eyes commune with the true vision,
The true is before one’s eyes.
Two beams of light penetrate the earth,
One thread of purity soars to heaven.
The moon’s illumination, limpid and bright,
The stars’ presence, serene and luminous.
Should one encounter this method,
Instantly they transform into flying immortals.

**Wisdom Sun, Heart-Communing Contemplation**
The wisdom sun’s heart-communing vision,
Light pervades the ten directions.
Good spirits all gather in protection,
Evil ghosts entirely vanish and hide.
Profound, heaven and earth are still,
Limpid, heaven and earth are frozen.
The Great Mystery’s true body appears,
Spiritual awareness penetrates pure light.

**Sudden Awakening, Empty Heart Contemplation**
Suddenly awakening to the empty heart’s vision,
Accord with the true, harmonizing with nature.
Myriad spirits pay homage to the Image Emperor,
One nature attains the immortal’s power.
Facing the Primordial Ancestor,
The heart connects with the beginning of kalpas.
Utterly true, clearly penetrating to the depths,
Returning to nature, ascending to the Jade Heaven.
