**Correct Unity, Void-Soaring Contemplation**
Correct Unity’s void-soaring vision,
Unfurling light, a myriad miles bright.
Throughout heaven, pure auspiciousness descends,
The entire land, purple mist arises.
The mysterious female facilitates coming and going,
Between the brows, taking the path of self-cultivation.
The true person encounters no obstruction,
The Four Seas, freely roaming at will.

**Luminous Fusion, Breath-Uniting Contemplation**
Luminous fusion, breath-uniting vision,
Utmost vision is the celestial truth.
The jeweled palace’s fragrant winds are extraordinary,
The jasper terrace’s emerald hues are fresh.
The flower pool irrigates the valley of wisdom,
Divine beings water the spirit’s root.
Every tree’s blossoms vie to bloom,
Radiance utterly free of dust’s speck.

**Detaching from Desire, Facing the True Contemplation**
Detaching from desire, facing the true vision,
Eternal spring exists in another realm.
Winding, crimson mist glows brilliantly,
Gently, purple light shines freshly.
The red child beyond the clouds,
The blue lad embraces the moon in sleep.
The jade dawn’s cold dew presses close,
Faintly sensing the crystal’s chill.

**Ten Poems on the Superior Practitioner**

The superior practitioner commands ghosts and spirits’ reverence,
Disasters vanish, calamities do not invade.
Myriad evils all keep far away,
All sages’ blessings simultaneously arrive.
Suddenly awakening to the nature yet to come,
Able to know the past mind.
Present before one, constantly undimmed,
In daily use, guarding pure resonance.

The superior practitioner refines the returning elixir,
The returning elixir penetrates the two barriers.
Pure light departs the nine earths,
Crimson flames emerge from the three mountains.
Surging within heaven and earth,
Void and bright, amidst heaven and earth.
Throughout the empty sky, all sages appear,
All are ranks of immortals.

The superior practitioner awakens to the mysterious truth,
Serene, within and without the same.
Within the bag, observing the still realm,
Beyond the body, beholding the clear wind.
Sun and moon communicate with celestial images,
Void and nothingness penetrate the world’s emptiness.
Completely merging into one body,
The utmost Dao forever without end.

The superior practitioner comprehends the Qian-Yuan,
Within it, simmering the small fresh.
Surging, the golden crucible boils,
Seething, the jade furnace refines.
Only then realizing the spirit elixir is complete,
Just knowing the great medicine is whole.
Ingested, ascending to the upper realms,
Eternally dwelling in the Great Luo Heaven.

The superior practitioner attains the subtle and mysterious,
Spiritual light fills the chamber with radiance.
Distinctly revealing the Dao’s essentials,
Unfettered, exposing the heart’s mechanism.
This method is known by few,
The numinous text’s awakening is rare.
Should one grasp this meaning,
Wondrous transformation enters non-action.

The superior practitioner abides in non-contention,
Non-contention surpasses reciting scriptures.
Unfolding, clearly manifesting form,
Withdrawing, silently without shape.
Guarding the One, the five spirits stabilize,
Preserving the Three, the seven po settle.
Refining into the immortal child’s countenance,
Leaping into the Jade Void City.

The superior practitioner refines form and spirit,
Form and spirit observe their true union.
Within fire, jade flies green,
Beneath water, silver leaps red.
The entire earth becomes treasure,
Soaring to heaven, all transforms into preciousness.
The mysterious pearl knows there is form,
Luminous and pure, utterly free of clamor and dust.

The superior practitioner abandons entanglements,
Carefree, entering the grotto-heaven.
Clouds and mist serve as companions,
Pines and cypresses are family ties.
Often reciting the *Huangting* scroll,
Constantly perusing the *Daode* chapter.
Awakening to this true and wondrous principle,
What worry of not attaining immortality?

**Presented to Enlightened One Yang Qing**
The superior practitioner abandons glory and splendor,
Carefree, entering the grotto’s mist.
Lead simmers the pot’s snow,
Mercury refines the crucible’s sand.
The medicine complete, the complexion flourishes,
The elixir formed, the color transforms further.
Primary and secondary divide into five hues,
The utmost principle, wondrous and without flaw.

**Presented to Serene One Xu Ji**
The superior practitioner abandons stubborn rigidity,
Carefree, entering the grotto’s chamber.
Heaven’s emptiness suspends the wondrous body,
The heart’s ground merges with true yang.
The old woman sleeps in the toad’s shadow,
The infant embraces the sun’s light.
The original spirit knows there is a master,
Through myriad ages, attaining pure clarity.

*Shangqing Taixuan Ji*, Scroll Five, Complete
*Shangqing Taixuan Ji*, Scroll Six

**Seven-Character Quatrains by Marquis Gu She Shanyuan, Sixty Poems**

How wondrous—this heart at ease in the great school,
Not drifting midstream but reaching distant shores.
Drunk, I fell from the cart for white wine’s sake;
Sober, I grasp my sandals for pure tea’s grace.

Primal essence surges forth, piercing heaven’s flight,
Wandering winds yield to the Two Modes’ might.
Thus I shed my form to return to the unbegun,
Where the Azure Lad invites me to the Elixir Pool.

Why in youth did I leave my home?
Pondering deeply, I sigh with woe.
Had not the Image-Mystery flowed into the crucible,
I’d still be driving the salt cart to this day.

Dragon’s drool and phoenix candles trace fragrant smoke,
Eyes illumine sparse woods, vast qi serene.
A gust of cold wind startles the crane’s dream—
On the star altar, the *Step-of-Void* chant rings.

The secluded pass’s fading light dissolves form,
Dual luminaries merge their glow in one bright realm.
Self and things both forgotten, the whole body appears,
Fused into a single point of Great Void’s essence.

Brows unfurled like wings, the sky’s vastness gleams,
The radiant sun and numinous wind illumine the Grand Clarity.
Transforming the body leaves no room for wind-fire’s nature—
I know my true self belongs to the Lesser Weave Star.

A furnace of gold and fire emits lead’s splendor,
Dazzling heaven and earth with emerald haze.
Guarding within, no thieving yin-ghosts intrude—
Naturally, the sacred crucible congeals numinous sand.

Nurturing one furnace of red phoenix marrow,
Refining two crucibles of crimson dragon essence,
I open the cosmos-wide Heavenly Eye—
At chaos’ first division, my vision grows clear.

Late at night, sitting alone as autumn’s moon hangs,
Auspicious qi lightly floats through twelve cycles.
Longing to return to Divine Empyrean’s old path,
The ancient fork gleams where azure haze gathers.

The soaring kite outshines cloud-ladders,
Carved wood’s craft plays with cunning mechanisms.
To be useful or not—one must suit oneself;
In the forest, I cast aside the sling and wander home.

Shaking off the dust’s bonds, I part ways,
My brother’s resolve stands firm, unchanging.
Though water and clouds veil us three thousand leagues apart,
I vow not to return unless I become an immortal.

Gazing up and down through a hundred thousand fathoms,
My drunken soul flies into the azure sky’s heart.
A youth guides me to Jade Pool’s mouth—
The toad’s radiance is refined into pure gold.

This illusory body long concealed in deep illness,
Exchanging form and light to illumine the jeweled peak.
Layers of jade-green shadows float on rushing mist,
A fire-dragon emerges from the azure pool’s depths.

In a blink, brows raised, the sun of wisdom dawns,
A river of landscapes unfolds before my eyes.
Jingshan’s peaks split open to reveal the spirit-treasure—
A flawless heap of jade gleams forth.

My heart dwells beyond things, serene and free,
A single lotus leaf floats on the azure sea.
The lotus blooms, its flower born of the sun’s smile,
Drifting with the wind to Jade Capital’s sky.

Standing tall in the empyrean, I survey the world’s splendor,
On Jade Pool’s twin shores, golden flowers bloom.
My drunken soul roams beyond the mundane,
Awakening into the Mysterious Metropolis, the Lord of Images’ abode.

The Mysterious Origin and Great One embrace vast mystery,
Within the misty haze, all sights arise.
Only when the two spirits merge with the twin luminaries
Does yin’s numen transform into a single celestial star.

Gazing into the grotto’s waves of deep green,
A sea-dragon plays with the night’s radiance.
Light blazes from the Great Nonbeing’s vast solar horn—
Myriad spirits converge to bear witness to the True Yang.

Auspicious clouds densely blanket river and sky,
Phoenix plumes and rainbows pierce the sun’s corner.
No wonder fragrant winds fill the hall—
In the jade palace, the jasper trees’ flowers vie in bloom.

The pearl-playing dragon emerges as the sea-gate opens,
Purple mist soars through the ninefold heavens.
Breaching the Bitter Pool to swallow sun and moon,
The immortals of the ten directions all turn in awe.

Rolling up the pearl curtain to gaze outward,
Pine winds and radiant sun penetrate the jade grove.
Seven treasures gather in the tortoiseshell abode—
A dazzling cluster of silver haze and jade.

Roaming and soaring through golden clarity, merged with the Great Void,
Brow Mountain’s moon-valley floats with auspicious clouds.
Without mastering this art, what can one achieve?
In vain does one stand tall in the empyrean as a man.

Before the jade mountain, myriad trees bloom,
Naturally claiming a fine livelihood.
The immortal lad smiles at the western guest—
Recently, the High Yang wine-tasting household.

Returning again to Divine Empyrean’s old path,
I wander at ease within the Jade Clarity Palace.
The starry river gleams, unknown to all—
Two blossoms of jasper bloom in one place.

Clearing the wild to plant jade *zhi* sprouts,
I break open Jade Pool to irrigate them anew.
Dao-qi circulates, surging through the azure sea,
Numinous winds pervade the clear empyrean.

Sun’s essence and moon’s marrow are refined without loss,
Earth’s po and heaven’s hun are tempered without flaw.
Exchanging substance while retaining truth, I endure in the world,
Amid ninefold radiance, I roam at will.

Misty Jiang’s haze scatters, the vast sky clears—
Alone, I face the Crimson Yang’s flying snowflakes.
Golden and jade light streams, illumining the Grand Clarity,
In the cold forest, jasper flowers naturally form.

The world’s net and dust’s passions—already left behind,
The Mysterious Gate’s true secret—what doubt remains?
If a man harbors the will to soar to heaven,
Why wait to become an immortal?

Clinging to illusion, why question the illusory mechanism?
Awakening to the mechanism still leads one astray.
I sigh for the cloud-water wanderer of the east—
In vain he journeyed to Jing Mountain, returning empty-handed.

The hundred-legged *kui* and serpent pass pity in turn,
Wandering winds and spirit transformations—all in vain.
One must first seek the precelestial ancestor—
Only then can one enter my school’s foremost mystery.

Last night at the third watch, the moon shone bright,
Gentle winds and dew dripped in clear spheres.
Who sang that resonant melody?
I suspect it was a jade-inebriated immortal from the jasper palace.

Alone I come and go on Zhongnan’s slopes by the Wei,
Seeking the worthies, I pass through Tong Pass.
Market scholars and rustic elders pay no heed—
Through rain and clouds, I return to my old mountain.

Briefly leaving the immortal isle for the human realm,
The bitter sea’s waves make salvation arduous.
Braving snow and wind, I return to my old retreat—
In the night’s chill, I cross Tong Pass with sword in hand.

Nine years’ work accomplished, the effect is subtle,
Returning home, I contain the jade mechanism’s secret.
Long have I sighed for the empyrean—
Yet in the forest, I am again bound like a tree stump.

Clinging to illusion, Master Wen questions the illusory mechanism,
Further inquiring of Master Yang—only to deepen the maze.
How many gains and losses does the deer discern?
Drunk, I ride the cart, my limbs undone.

Words and wit contend with Hui Ang,
Yet I regret having no master to meet Liang Yang.
Abandoning home and neglecting work to indulge desires—
Thorns await the moment to test Ji Chang.

The wise of this world mock those who leave home,
Knowing their spirit’s vastness has no bounds.
Seeking the fire-mirror, three cups of wine—
Their savor surpasses Lu Tong’s seven bowls of tea.

The rut-bound fish long trapped, awaiting the western river,
For my esteemed guest, I speak of Master Yang.

All say, "Having gained the pearl, why need the Dao?"
Fortunate to meet Master Dongguo, I pour out my heart.

Ten thousand layered emerald peaks lean against the azure haze,
A river of jade-green waters joins the river’s edge.
Where now the sword bestowed in years past?
To whom today is the hidden light entrusted?

Auspicious radiance stirs the celestial glow, illuminating the Great Clarity,
The vermilion court bears the fiery essence of tiger and dragon.
Refined into a treasure-mirror, luminous as the heavens,
Two divine beams converge in one bright place.

Facing the wind, we chant and harmonize a thousand poems,
Beneath the moon, cups brim with a hundred measures of wine.
At ease upon ancient Kunlun, self and other forgotten,
The drunken soul soars into the Palace of Broad Cold.

The ancient Dao was originally divided from the Primordial Beginning,
Vast and boundless, the Three Realms merge as one.
The whale and roc emerge from the sea, their traces stretching far,
Flying to the Jasper Pool in the sixth summer month.

I regret having pursued rare skills and vain pursuits,
For rank and wealth, glory and gate—how hard to attain!
Just now I saw the lord boast of his strength,
Fashioning a single leaf for you to see.

The shallow filth of the salamander and loach becomes their foundation,
Yet to restrain the weak and bind the sturgeon is not fitting.
If only the heavenly wind would lift my wings,
I would ride the whirlwind to the Jasper Pool.

The fiery wheel grinds through the azure beryl,
Two golden beams advance in radiant flight.
Thus the image of the Mysterious flows into the crucible,
Naturally roaming and soaring through the Ninefold Clarity.

Who pities the rut-bound fish, trapped on the road?
Those who flow with the current mock the sickly flesh.
The misty waves of the Northern Sea must part in the end—
Unfurl your wings, chart the southern course, cross the Five Lakes.

Who has seen the divine being, so ethereal in form,
Drinking wind, sipping dew, her skin like snow?
For a moment she leaves the misty caves of Guye,
Steadily riding the flying dragon to the Jade Capital.

What matter of the Primordial Origin is most profound?
The towering treasure-dharma crowns all past and present.
Having gained the jade grove’s soaring white feathers,
A single crimson sun illumines the heart of heaven.

At ease with Mei and Zhang, I chant extemporaneously,
The two masters’ wisdom deepens our bond.
Like wind and moon, clear through all ages,
They illuminate the heart of heaven, ten thousand fathoms deep.

Striking the void, striking things—ghosts and spirits startle,
Leaning into each step, borrowing lightness with ease.
When I ascend the Jade Empyrean to the realm of Jia,
I shall transform you then, carrying you to take dragon form.

A crucible of golden fire blazes in the celestial thoroughfare,
Revealing the flawless pearl that illumines the sea.
Enveloped and suddenly clarified, congealing into jade,
Refined into an immortal—wondrous skill!

Jade springs well forth, flowing into golden wells,
In an instant, the southern cinnabar and northern sea achieve merit.
Splitting the Mysterious Pearl to release radiant clouds,
The Mysterious Pearl soars to Kunlun’s summit.

Perfect clarity—ten thousand dharmas exist within the void,
A single stream of cinnabar surges through the gate of wisdom.
Gazing upon the jade grove’s clustered blossoms,
Two geese tilt the celestial flask, pouring wine from the Gourd Heaven.

The Primordial Great Man’s wind tears asunder,
His brows like the jade toad swallowing the moon over the sea.
The treasure-feast’s celestial light illumines the Five Tombs,
Cinnabar essence scatters, yellow blossoms form.

Staff in hand, I wander to visit the misty vines,
Yet how many desolate paths and wayward inns lie in wait!
No need for the two concubines to know beauty or ugliness—
Alas, I lack the grace to emulate Han E.

Three-colored mists swirl, striking the Crimson Palace,
Vermilion gates half-conceal the true countenance.
The ice-grinding wheel shatters the path of the Mysterious Ridge,
Transforming all under heaven with the wind of primordial antiquity.

To move things, to pluck flowers—all is emptiness,
Where in human relations does one apply effort?
The Tathāgata once spoke of awe-inspiring spiritual power—
I ask the Chan stream: have you grasped it?

Ascending the upper story, the eye’s realm brightens,
I seem to doubt my body has reached Huaqing.
No need for cloud-borne chariots in the central heavens—
I fly into the fiery palace to accompany the morning star.

Gazing all day at the golden crow in the empyrean,
The Vermilion Mound’s fiery domain refines the jade crucible.
The treasure-dharma dissolves form, transcending the material,
The Nine Spirits’ immortals ascend to the Upper Clarity.

The numinous gaze, tempered, enters the vermilion court,
Yellow qi surges, sweeping away impure forms.
Looking up and down, the cavernous void is fully responsive,
The lush radiance of the Empyrean illumines Huaqing.

**Seven-character full verse**
In the Hall of Fungi, verdant hues speak of the Mysterious Subtle,
Directly pointing to the alchemical canon, revealing the jade mechanism.
The ocean’s depths churn with red agate,
The mountain’s heights shatter azure beryl.

The jade hare of the Moon Palace roams the mossy path,
The golden crow of the Sun Palace rests on the cassia branch.
Two segments of light return to one place—
The Peerless Noble ascends to the Jasper Pool.

In years past, I wandered and lost my way, not returning home,
Today, turning my gaze, I return to the emerald clouds.
Golden fire overflows the crucible in five hues,
Cinnabar fills the tripod, emitting triple radiance.

By the river, I seize and break the Black Dragon’s tail,
On the ridge, I strike open the White Tiger’s teeth.
The cave-mirror of Fivefold Clarity penetrates the Great Existence—
Then I ride the crane-chariot, driving the cloud-carriage.

In the cavern-chamber, the night is desolate,
The ape and horse are captured to accompany solitude.
The jade hare pursues the toad at the corner of the heavens,
The golden crow embraces the sun, circling the sky’s waist.

The dragon coils around the medicine tripod, the Three Flowers gather,
The tiger retreats from the elixir furnace, the Five Qi pay homage.
Refining the numinous cinnabar to dwell beyond form,
The Jade Capital’s immortal precincts are not far.

By chance I traverse the long abyss, dwelling temporarily,
Like one waiting for a hare by an empty stump.
Unmet by Bo Le, I ride a salt-laden horse,
Like encountering Zhuangzi’s rut-bound fish.

How could I heed the vain search of years past?
Only now do I know the attainment of the Mysterious Pearl.
In Longxi, we meet again by chance—
I write these heartfelt words to send to you.

Why does Zhan He reel in his fishing line?
The □ carp leaps the waves, snapping the hook.
Delighted to escape the shallow stream, leaving the sea of suffering,
Fortunate to meet the long waters and find ease.

Content to dwell in a thatched hut, welcoming the mountain elder,
Forgetting to visit the vermilion gates of noble lords.
Who will see me home, drunk from the village feast?
A shepherd boy supports me, riding backward on an ox.

Alas, I wander within and without, knowing no path,
Mistakenly entering the cloudy mountains to strike and stay.
The lost Mysterious Pearl must be sought in concealment,
The moon of the mind, once stilled, requires no search.

A single strand of blue mist descends from the heavens,
Two trails of red rainbow roll across the earth.
Having reached the Fiery Palace, mother and child part,
Sideways, the Seven Luminaries circulate through the great expanse.

I send word to the pine-shaped, crane-haired elder:
Search well for the Mysterious Subtle, leap from the mortal cage.
The Three Passes’ qi surges, white as the heavens,
A single golden elixir shoots red into the crucible.

Mercury congeals in the Jade Yang, leaving the Water Palace,
Lead solidifies into golden qi, entering the Fiery Palace.
The flowing pearl ascends Kunlun’s summit—
I behold the vast winds of the Jasper Pool.

To imitate others is not merely to betray kindness,
Concealing evil, obscuring the upright, dimming heaven’s truth.
Relying on spirits, clinging to the Dao for livelihood,
Clasping a child, nestling with a wife, expounding the teachings—

Such is not the way.

The discerning masses despise the lofty adept,
The ignorant demons slander the enlightened one.
Say not that heaven and earth lack judgment—
Far in descendants, near in one’s own person.

**Five-character full poem**

Joy and sorrow stem from a lost horse,
A blemished eye from birthing an ox.
The deer was shared by Duke Xun’s minister,
The butterfly dream awakened Zhuang Zhou.
Gu Ye returned through spiritual transformation,
Hu Qiu resumed his outer wanderings.
Dongmen became my companion,
Nanguo too my fellow.
In youth, my nature inclined toward the sacred,
In middle age, my appearance grew dull as folly.
The gull startled, forgetting its true form,
The dog barked at the exchange of black robes.
Why question the two concubines?
The Three Spirits have their own appointed time.
Ji Jian failed in physiognomy,
Wen Zhi excelled in healing arts.
Who wields the illusions of the owl and rooster?
The ring dance charts its own discord.
Sharp as a mountain-consuming fire,
Proud as a cup set upon the elbow.
A gentleman’s vessel bears no burden,
Yet displays the talent of a petty man.
Recent conduct differs not from wisdom,
Vainly laboring on a thousand-foot terrace.
Why should such as these cross the threshold?
A master craftsman measures before cutting.
Easy to maintain a pure and disciplined mind,
Hard to sustain a daily fast.
The crucible boils root-bound greens,
The furnace burns leaf-laden firewood.
I marvel at the fish trapped in the wheel rut—
A ladle of water brings no disaster.
Disciples’ affections run shallow,
The Daoist abbey grows desolate.
Wild herbs remain year-round,
Household grain nears exhaustion.
My heart has already consented—
What say you, sir?
Liezi journeyed through Wei,
Yet where to find one’s true abode?
In facing affairs, one knows the value of leisure,
In stilling the mind, one perceives the Dao’s majesty.
Ancient masters personally demonstrated ruin,
Temporarily borrowing aid from the Mysterious Gate.
Why boast of flint’s sharpness?
Shang Qiu remains in dullness.
Three years to form a single leaf,
All by grace of heaven’s favor.
The secret of ascending immortality is broken—
Kunlun’s peaks array the Two Modes.
The elixir furnace gathers divine fire,
The precious tripod glows with nocturnal radiance.
Refining the body into golden liquid,
Nourishing the countenance into jade mist.
Mighty spirit shines in great abundance,
The roc’s wings reach the celestial pool.
Having encountered the true immortal’s secret,
I dwell in seclusion to refine the valley spirit.
Through penetrating the mysterious, self and other are forgotten,
Attaining the wondrous, kinship and estrangement dissolve.
Yin Shi transformed into a servant,
The laborer presumptuously played the guest—
No need to distinguish waking from dreaming,
Beyond appearances lies eternal spring.
A long whistle laughs at the unworthy,
Fishing for fools, not for fish.
A needle’s tip dispenses grains of rice,
A standing tree praises the long road.
When singing in harmony, gratitude must be distant,
Those who know the tune keep the Dao close.
Looking down upon my disciples,
Not one shares the same aspiration.
Striking tiles, the child is careless,
Mocking poetry, the vase is but a model.
Inquiring of the dawn, one knows distance,
Pitying creatures, one discerns their arising.
Dispelling illusions, the ring dance ceases,
Welcoming the lord, facing the circular screen.
Refining cinnabar to temper azure jade,
Exchanging bones to ascend Qingcheng.
On the road, startled by the three cloths,
Midway, wary of the five brews.
The inept servant cannot judge a horse,
The neighbor’s son has already lost his sheep.
Why plot to wear Zhang’s seal?
Why imitate Ji Chang?
Not boasting of autumn waters’ arrival,
The heart finds boundless ease.
The Great Dao manifests the Three Bodies,
The Three Bodies all converge in one truth.
The black dragon hides in the depths,
The cinnabar phoenix rises in auspicious clouds.
The two apertures pour forth golden liquid,
The twin passes refine the jade spirit.
Wisdom’s light soars to the purple towers,
Resplendent, it illumines the celestial wheel.
Splitting open the seamless pagoda,
Releasing the primordial essence.
Qi spreads, calming the three rivers,
Clouds withdraw, clarifying the four seas.
The golden serpent roams the water palace,
The jade hare hastens to the fiery city.
Refining the firm and pure nature,
Returning to rest in the Great Clarity.
Ten thousand *yi* given are still too few,
A single hair’s aid is more than enough.
At ease with the three excellences,
Dwelling in leisure for a hundred years.
The Yan capital holds no intent to depart,
The Hua Xu realm beckons with purpose.
Life and death are but momentary realizations,
Forgotten again in an instant.
Hidden illumination pierces the jade grove,
Jasper blossoms scatter from the jeweled peak.
The vermilion court hears the golden phoenix cry,
The lunar palace echoes the jade dragon’s chant.
Refining the body to condense the Three Qi,
Nourishing the spirit to disperse the Nine Yin.
The mysterious image is like a precious mirror,
Ever present in the azure sky’s heart.

**Two five-character quatrains**

Azure pupils cast light to earth,
The red sun’s flames reach heaven.
Within the five-colored clouds,
A single lotus leaf in the Jasper Pool.
Outer and inner are all illusion,
The center is wholly void.
Pointing to the unenlightened—
Where to apply effort?

**Seven-character quatrains**

The true message is clearly revealed,
The celestial eye pierces emptiness through wisdom’s power.
Above and below, perfectly fused—nothing remains,
Majestically revealing the vast and luminous.
Who can recognize the Primordial Dao of Mystery?
Silent and desolate, it enters without seam.
Striking with unyielding might, it shatters the sky,
Congealing emptiness, ten thousand points of streaming stars emerge.
The Primordial Void Sovereign gave birth to the Great Antiquity,
Fitting to be the eternal lord of the mysterious.
Among the four great domains, it alone stands first,
Enduring through kalpas as heaven and earth’s ancestor.
Nourishing the spirit, I knock upon the Dao to clarify mysterious virtue,
Vastly distant from misty vines, still and silent.
Leaping forth as a flying immortal into Great Hua,
Dwelling forever in the serene and sunlit realm.
The heart connects to wondrous subtleties, illuminating true patterns,
Attaining that pure emptiness, delving into profundities.
The supreme Dao is level and easy, taken in due course,
Ascending the mysterious to become a guest of the Great Canopy.
At heaven and earth’s center, like a bellows,
Skillfully harmonizing sound and form through mutual accord.
Within the mysterious, not striking the fine notes,
A single strain of reed pipes pierces the phoenix pavilion.
The Jade Clarity Sage Ancestor left the Three Armors,
Responding to the supremely profound and wondrous Dharma.
Sending forth jasper blossoms to descend from the azure sky,
Red frost flake by flake, pressed by fragrant winds.
Sincerity subdues the corporeal soul, uplifting the ethereal,
Luminous qi, pure and clear, envelops the jeweled jade.
Intent follows the sun’s splendor into emerald peaks,
Jade cliffs stretch into the gaze of empty mountains.
Shaking off the dusty world, not long submerged,
Merging with the Great Beginning, knowing the true origin.
Divine might and qi’s image encompass heaven’s heart,
The Dao spreads the sun’s essence, bright and glistening.
The Dao slays the Three Corpses through the power of attraction,
The numinous yang elixir conceals pure yin.
Suddenly, unaware, the inner form is forgotten,
Seated, one attains the cloudy heavens, the spirit feasts in repose.
Within, the essence is cleansed, the void gleams with jade fragments,
Clear as ice, lustrous as the autumn river’s moon.
The Crimson Palace faintly senses the crystal’s chill,
Jeweled splendor, starlight’s radiance, flying flakes of snow.
A single point of heaven’s light in the Great Void,
Clapping, sealing, surging harmony enters without seam.
Treading upon the ten thousand fathoms’ peak of heaven and earth,
Congealing emptiness, flying stars rush forth.
The jade well’s flowing spring does not burst forth,
The resonant chime echoes against the green mountains.

The jade waves surge through the peaks’ clouds,
Waves batter Kunlun’s stones to powder.
The golden well glows with the sun’s radiance,
Cloud-jades fly forth from the Jasper Pool Isle.

The crystal curtain winds roll, wafting pure fragrance,
Heaven’s lustrous void, dustless, transmits the Six Treasures.
The Dharma-eye unfolds at the brows’ lashes,
Eyes gleam, pupils dazzle, weaving celestial brilliance.

Awe-inspiring wind encircles the earth from the four directions,
Ten thousand streams of numinous light greet the heavens.
The Primordial Beginning dwelt before the vast kalpas,
Opening the Three Realms, establishing the Double Mystery.

Heaven and earth are born from Its transformation,
Through kalpas’ ruin, It endures, ever majestic.
The Dao transforms the Three Palaces in wondrous mystery,
The Primordial Spirit Emperor secretly transmits It.

Fetal radiance flows into the numinous yang body,
Six Caverns’ flying essence descends from the Nine Heavens.
The pilgrim’s staff stirs the sea of Perfect Awakening,
The precept-knife cleaves the Jade Capital Mountain.

The Dragon Palace proffers the resplendent Mystic Pearl,
Subtle flowing light fills heaven and earth.
Jade-like forms ascend the peaks in reverse,
The numinous crow alights by the sea turtle’s edge.

Forms shift, shadows turn, following the wind’s departure,
Things change, stars drift, waves meet the sky.
The divine sword, whetted, startles the mad steed,
The wisdom-blade, brandished, shocks the playful ape.

Heaven and earth stand apart, all demons’ heads severed,
A single surge of awe-inspiring light topples the world.
At night, the sonorous stone is cast into the sea’s depths,
The Water Palace is split open, revealing the Dragon Palace.

All proffer the luminous pearl in offering,
Flames blaze in the cloudy skies, the azure firmament.
The Precept Altar’s sacred beasts exhale fragrant spirals,
Jade pendants chime, harmonizing with the tinkling girdle-ornaments.

True sages descend, returning to their original stations,
Once more wielding the divine sword, ascending the stellar pivot.
I urge you to keep your heart in the realm of Dao and virtue,
I hear the immortal courts have established the examination grounds.

The Divine Empyrean bears wings to transmit the golden register,
The Purple Palace knows no one to present the jade missive.
The dragon soars, roaming the Crimson Emperor’s realm,
The Luo Yuan immortal maiden sits in Flowery Yang.

Two streams of earthly qi traverse the Ox and Dipper,
A single ray of heavenly light anchors the azure vault.
The Crimson Palace just perceives the talismanic smoke’s fragrance,
The wind gently carries the sound of jade pendants.

In the clear night, who presents the memorial?
The perfected one paces the stellar pivot upon the altar.
Cultivation must attain the Valley Spirit’s numinosity,
A single point of perfect clarity illumines the Supreme Clarity.

The frosty sky, profound, hosts the ancient moon,
The limpid sea of awakening bathes the streaming stars.
A single grain of numinous cinnabar glows in the Great Clarity,
Merged with the empty valley, the formless appears.

The Dharma-realm’s boundless truth gleams in a thousandfold purity,
Misty radiance illumines the ten thousand images of heaven and earth.
The ancient Dao, level and smooth, allows progress,
Two branching paths connect to the celestial court.

Riding the dragon, the maiden of alchemy roams the Golden Gates,
Mounting the tiger, the infant traverses the Jade Capital.
Treading Kunlun, piercing the heavens,
Returning to the supreme Dao, restoring the primordial origin.

Tigers leap, mountain peaks turn,
Dragons soar from the abyss, sea waves churn.
Opening the wisdom-eye, beholding the divine light,
A single surge of pure yin wholly transforms into yang.

Vast as the sun rising to illuminate the world,
Bright as the moon casting its glow upon all directions.
Brushing aside the mist, the spirit roams the azure realm,
Two wheels converge, grinding the stellar pivot.

Dragons fly in the sun’s palace, brewing golden liquid,
Phoenixes blaze in the moon’s palace, drinking jade nectar.
Shunning worldly ties, seeking beyond the material,
Head held high, laughing freely, delighting in the joy of song.

Shifting the spirit, step by step, following the wind’s path,
Escorting my light form to ascend the precious peak.
The Dao descends in misty splendor, the scene is sublime,
The wondrous birth of heaven and earth knows no bounds.

Flying essence, refined, pierces the heavens’ summit,
Embracing the sun, approaching the void, transforming Mount Taihua.
Avoiding wind, nestling by the sun, eyes languidly open,
Within, yin and yang unite to nurture the sacred embryo.

Only then does one believe a man’s body can conceive,
Naturally, beyond the material, the immortal fetus dances.
Pairing heaven and earth to serve as the elixir furnace,
The sun and moon, round, encircle the face’s dwelling.

At the sea’s bottom, the true supreme treasure is refined,
The gray-haired one cooks the Primordial Pearl to perfection.
Slaying the ape, taming the horse, transforming the dragon colt,
It bears me, following the wind, into the Great Void.

A single streaming star flies to the moon’s palace,
Two crimson flames ascend to the celestial Wu.
Clad in simplicity, awakened, drinking the true wind,
Emerging from the human realm, affairs are not the same.

Should you ask where the master abides,
Steadily riding the crane’s back, wings upon the turtle palace.
Amidst the seated clouds and mist, the cold stream is locked,
Thunder’s peaks rumble, disturbing the Supreme Subtlety.

Ten thousand silver waves pour into the azure ravine,
A single surge of jade waves cascades into the Jasper Pool.
The sun’s soul and moon’s spirit cast their cold radiance,
The two are captured, held between Kan and Li.

Suddenly, from the sea’s depths, the dragon and tiger roar,
Atop the mountain, the phoenix and luan bird take startled flight.
The layered peaks of Guye cast floating emerald shadows,
Within the grotto, the divine transformation reveals snow-white skin.

By what power does one roam the four seas?
The crane’s chariot, riding the whirlwind, departs the Jade Capital.
Releasing the jade hare to chase the numinous crow,
Catching up to the Gate of Simplicity, entering the Great Beginning.

Ten thousand golden rays illuminate the cosmos,
A thousand silver mists shine upon the void.
To refine the One True, the Three Wonders must be cultivated,
Then employ the Three Wonders to unite the Two Modes.

If the Two Modes are made one body,
The golden elixir will naturally pierce the heavens and fly.
Eyes pure, beholding the celestial signs,
Ears keen, listening to the steps of emptiness.

Great is the Dao that follows all directions,
The most wondrous true constancy merges with the sun’s congealment.
The fiery furnace pours into the tripod, refining red cinnabar,
Three-colored mists swirl, releasing rainbow hues.

Resplendent treasures, intricate, fly through the cosmos,
The Primordial Elixir descends into the Central Land.
The body like withered wood, the nature like ashes,
Silently, in clarity, nurturing the sacred embryo.

Seated in the jade palace, coming to inquire of the Dao,
Head held high, laughing freely, the osmanthus blooms.
Brows arched, eyes bright, the heart’s pearl leaps,
Descending upon the golden plate, five colors unfurl.

Within, dispatching the jade lad to gather the sun’s sea,
To accompany me in returning to the grotto-heaven’s abode.
When lead and mercury are paired, rely on the sun and moon,
When the tripod and furnace are placed, employ heaven and earth.

The Three Yangs’ true fire burns the numinous substance,
A single grain of golden elixir ascends in reverse.
A foot’s distance, yet the sea of suffering is deep,
The mind follows the currents, drifting into the waves’ heart.

Losing the celestial truth, one wanders through a thousand kalpas,
From ancient times until now, endlessly cycling.
Ascending the Mystery, awakening to the Dao’s profundity,
Expanding the numinous source, concealing the illusory heart.

In an instant, traversing all directions,
Only by treading the ancient path can one know the present.
Startled awake, one awakens to the immortal realm,
Only then does one trust the spirit’s congealment in the sun’s beneficent light.

In the child’s furnace, the jade liquid pours,
Within the fetal immortal’s tripod, the jasper nectar blends.

The Dao’s utmost profundity, wondrous and mysterious,
The Supreme Clarity’s true teaching—how could it be vain words?
If you still possess a man’s resolve,
I shall impart the celestial mechanism to your ear alone.

All speak of refining the elixir, yet none speak of the elixir’s duality—
The two golden elixirs lie but a foot’s span from the Great Void.
A single pill, resplendent, illuminates the cosmos,
Yet in daily use, it seems as distant as ten thousand mountains.

Gazing down, one sees Earth’s tranquility in Kun’s softness;
Looking up, one beholds Heaven’s clarity in Qian’s Dao.
Floating and sinking, their positions manifest in the center,
Merging with the Void, sun and moon shine brightly.

Within, purify the mind-ape to nurture the pearl of nature;
Without, subdue the intent-horse to refine the path of darkness.
The numinous light pierces the Golden Crow’s cavern,
Merging into perfect clarity, the body unites with the Great Void.

Gently strike the jade lock, the grotto gate opens,
A pair of divine winds rush through the doorway.
With intent, embrace the simurgh and soar to the Moon Palace,
Beneath the Yinless Tree, wander at leisure.

The four leaky vessels ultimately return to illusion,
Only the perfectly luminous nature is not yet true.
Wait until your name is inscribed in the Jade Empyrean,
Only then shall you truly embody the one who has left the household.

Cloudy mists scatter as dawn’s frost glistens,
In the clear night, dustless, the moon is full.
Seated, one draws near the jasper palace,
Within ninefold radiance, the Golden Immortal is borne aloft.

Kan and Li unite, breaking free from the dusty world’s confines,
Sun and moon exchange their light, illuminating the body.
Water and fire refine the Leakless Child,
The precious vase cradles the Jade Flower Infant.

Golden crystals rain through the jade window,
The Hua Yang Immortal enters the Central August.
The Lesser Weaving Star falls to the clear river’s depths,
The crane presses the treetops, snow dusts the frost.

The waters are pure, fishless, waves touch the sky,
The numinous spirit flies away, entering the Essence Abyss.
Hua Yang does not follow the red dust’s path,
For the divine wind naturally merges with the Great Mystery.

*Supreme Clarity and Great Mystery Collection, Scroll Six Concludes*
*Supreme Clarity and Great Mystery Collection, Scroll Seven*

**Seven-Character Verses by Gu Shehou Shanyuan**

Kan and Li intertwine, merging the sacred mechanism,
Two paths sever the way, linking to Heaven’s frontier.
The celestial cycle ten thousand times returns, the dragon assumes its stance,
The earth a thousand fathoms deep, the tiger displays its might.

Driving back external demons, eradicating the six harms,
Seizing the retreating yin ghosts and the Three Worms.
From between the brows, the toad sword is drawn,
With a single slash, floating clouds mend the leaky pond.

Carefree and untroubled, delighting in pure leisure,
Leading cranes, bearing staffs, wandering water and mountain.
Wind rolls emerald mist across verdant peaks,
Moonlight and gentle haze reach the blue ridges.

Before the grotto, water bursts forth like a thousand pearls,
Beneath the ravine, clouds congeal into a ball of snow.
Luminous and crystalline, the Dao-eye shines,
Divinely clear and refreshing, chilling all who approach.

In the primal chaos, the Two Modes first parted,
The Three Powers transformed, root of creation.
Ascending and descending, sun and moon soar,
Floating and sinking, Qian and Kun stand firm.

Jade fragments drift down from the void,
Golden elixir grains surge upward in reverse.
Two azure lads roam the green peaks,
Embracing the simurgh, they fly into the Gate of the Great Mystery.

Suddenly, the nature awakens to the true source,
Instantly, the heart-pearl connects everywhere.
Unfettered and pure, returning to refined delight,
Mighty and spiritually refined, washing away dust and delusion.

Clouds withdraw, revealing the moon in the deep pool,
Mists disperse, and the primordial wind arises.
Supremely all-knowing, pervading the ten directions,
Perfectly luminous, the solitary body illumines the void.

Splitting open chaos to reveal Heaven’s heart,
The essence of sun and moon fills the Great Yin.
The Dipper’s handle turns, heaven and earth rain,
The Dharma wheel revolves, the Great Void deepens.

Intermingling light emits a thousand pearls,
Chaotic things welcome ten thousand specks of gold.
The supreme treasure needs no search beyond,
Nurturing spirit and awareness, the Dao takes its course.

Embracing constancy, knowing contentment, the primordial spirit is restored,
Delighting in ease and tranquility, the utmost truth is cultivated.
Eradicating sharpness, eliminating greed, the Dao is fully realized,
Dispelling the blade, gazing into the mystery, the eternal body is renewed.

Externally seeking jade and pearls brings no true worth,
Internally cleansing the sacred casket is never impoverished.
Where does the crane’s chariot, borne on the whirlwind, alight?
Within the grotto, only the four seasons renew.

Ever preserve the will, severing false splendor,
Returning to reflect on the Dragon Realm, the Purple Mansion.
In the indistinct, the primordial spirit surges through vast qi,
In the profound darkness, true breath radiates crimson mist.

The Jade Pool’s waves are pure, golden pistils float,
The Azure Sea’s ripples are clear, jade blossoms drift.
Fragrance unfurls, heaven and earth gleam,
From the congealed void, night-bright sand flies.

Divine fire blazes fiercely on Mount Gen,
With a single thrust from the tail gate, the Three Passes open.
The colossal image of heaven circles the void,
The sea-blending flood dragons coil beyond all things.

Congealing in one crucible, the marrow of heaven and earth,
Fusing in two cauldrons, the liver of the Great Yang.
Those who awaken to this ascend as immortals,
Riding the Yi, mounting the true, straddling the colored simurgh.

Turning the Dipper’s handle, moving the numinous pivot,
The Great Being’s gate opens—nothing remains.
Externally embracing the primordial Dao of Heaven,
Internally concealing two scrolls of life-giving scripture.

From nothingness, a thousand layers of jade are built,
In emptiness, ten thousand pearls are adorned.
With merit and practice both complete, transcending the world,
Riding the whale, stepping steadily toward Yingdu.

Vastly opening the wisdom eye, revealing the clear gaze,
The two wings of divine wind chase the sun’s head.
In the Ren-Wu clouds, riding the jade elephant,
In the Ding-Gong sea, straddling the golden ox.

Crimson mist curls around the Dragon Pavilion,
Purple haze swirls thickly around the Phoenix Tower.
Should one ask what blessed land this is,
The azure lad respectfully reports: it is Yingzhou.

Curbing desire, removing passion, the will stands firm,
The barren wilderness of the quail transforms into fields of lingzhi.
The heart like the azure Han, probing the moon in the deep pool,
The nature like the red furnace, a lotus within the flame.

Roaming and feasting beyond the true realms of Supreme Clarity,
Lingering in the primordial Great Luo Heaven of Yuanshi.
The Central August names me the Double Mystery Child,
The Gu She immortal dwells as the Primordial Transcendent.

Reversing yin and yang is true cultivation,
A single torrent of the Yellow River flows backward.
Ten thousand strands of white light pierce the corners of the universe,
A thousand threads of crimson flame emerge from mountain peaks.

The sun’s soul gleams brightly, manifesting everywhere,
The moon’s spirit radiates brilliantly, circling all directions.
Greatly unfolding the majestic wind, opening the ancient Dao,
Riding the simurgh, wielding the sword, roaming the nine heavens.

**Ode to Nurturing Spirit**
In true emptiness, the child-mother mechanism is complete,
Ghosts and spirits intermingle, penetrating the mud pill.
The Two Modes and the Great Beginning must return to one—
The Dao of the Three Essentials.

The six directions share a single path—
The mechanism of the six harmonies.
The nine qi, profoundly mysterious, are the body beyond—
The Dao of the nine yang.

The celestial flow and heavenly water are the central symbol—
The mechanism of the upper pivot.
One must rely on the essentials, the master’s clear teaching,
The most profound explanation of the Double Mystery.

**Ode to the Mysterious Image**
Vaguely, the divine transforms, the Jade Pass opens,
A single point of fetal light descends upon the wisdom terrace.
Naturally, the brilliance of Li and Yang shines,
Returning the light to the origin, the flame glows white.

The Double Mystery’s wondrous pointer is hard to fathom,
The gate of all wonders—fools cannot guess.
Serene, it may exist, approaching the morning audience with the Emperor,
Embracing the heart-moon, hastening to Penglai.

**Ode to Cultivating Nature**
In the indistinct, departing for the Toad Palace to nurture the nature-embryo,
The hidden dragon bathes the cinnabar embryo beneath the waters.
One must know that guarding the dark is the root,
Naturally, the numinous radiance illuminates the nature-terrace.

Within chaos, the Great One is revealed,
In the profound darkness, the heart’s brilliance is unfathomable.
One should follow where the wisdom-soul and yang arise,
The resplendent mystery-pearl moves of itself.

**Ode to Heavenly Auspices**
The Heavenly Treasure is naturally so, without contrivance,
Abandoning wisdom, leaving form, preceding the ten thousand transformations.
Leaving nature to accompany emptiness, light pervades all,
Moving spirit, gazing into the mystery, the Jade Heaven gleams.

Allowing things and self to become illusory,
Naturally, starry radiance shines before the eyes.
The sea-moon contains brilliance, light in ten thousand strands,
Transforming into the Heavenly Auspicious Jade Pot Immortal.

Qian’s origin, benefit, and harmony reveal my spirit,
The five qi ascend to the origin, employing the utmost truth.
The *Zhouyi*’s opening and closing clarify movement and change,
The ten thousand mechanisms converge, emerging from the dust.

Following the mechanism, responding to all, observing the mysterious image,
All day, diligently, drawing near to the Dao.
Internally and externally crystalline, penetrating inside and out,
The numinous radiance adorns me, hastening to Pengying.

**Hidden-Head Poems**
Qi intermingles, the ten thousand things flourish—know this,
The eye’s qi refines the true, the yin soul scatters—awareness.
The Yellow Palace’s chambers, the Dao is complete within the Great—
The four enter the numinous emperor, images gather in the void.

Opening, returning to the hour, awakening the drunken soul—treasure bright,
The grotto’s gate gleams, the three mountains gather mist—clear.

**Again**
Dwelling in solitude near the forest springs, the jade stream,
A thousand years of bitter practice rely on the heart’s deep rectitude.

The Three Perfections’ wondrous form—vainly slight in record’s light,
In primordial chaos, immortals soar, transformations fill the vast expanse.
Things refine within, naturally merging with Heaven’s diligence—
Luminous brilliance shines on both, yet formless is the Way.

**Lyrics to "Fragrant Incense"**
Heaven and earth, dark and yellow, follow transformations, unforced.
The Great Void’s heights—sun and moon take flight.
Dragon musk and starry Dipper, phoenix ignites the Mysterious Net.
Behold the sea’s divine tides, the river’s spirit convenes, the valley’s power unfurls.

Resplendent, radiant, illuminating the ten directions.
Merging the Three Palaces, with one shake, yang currents flow.
Not apart from daily use, here and now, receive and uphold.
Gradually return to true emptiness, revert to true correctness, attain true constancy.

**To the Tune of "Lesser Layered Mountains"**
Yin and yang inverted—a single thunderclap.
Suddenly startled from sleep, awakened within the dream.
Deluded clouds brushed away, wisdom’s light unfolds.
Following the wind, embracing the sun’s orb, I come.

Tempering nurtures the immortal embryo.
In emptiness, clearly manifest, surpassing the numinous terrace.
Gazing all around—above and below—at Penglai.
Worthy to return to the jade grotto as immortal talent.

**To the Tune of "Intertwined Branches"**
Blunting sharpness, no shame; encountering favor, no joy.

Amidst gentle softness and ordinary ease, flow with conditions and pass by—unfettered and at peace.
Strolling through forests and springs, deep into emerald clouds,
I delight in a lifetime of pure leisure.
Should one wish to transcend birth and death,
to grasp that truth of eternal constancy:
Refine qi into spirit, spirit soars beyond the azure vault,
one with the Great Void.
Roam boundless heaven and earth, forever free from care—
attain longevity and enduring vision.

**Two Poems to the Tune of "A Sprig of Plum Blossoms"**
One in worldly toil, one in ceaseless haste.
Since parting, one attains true constancy.
One day of radiant essence, one day of cool clarity—
a single gleam of pure light,
a single band of congealed yang.
One qi intermingles, one qi expands.
One binds the elixir of spirit, one extends life’s span.
One numinous spark enters one cloud-chamber—
a pair of golden youths,
one guides to the immortal realm.

Again:
Lightly breaking from the world, tender green branches grow.
Unlike the pine and bamboo, they alone endure frost and wind.
A heart steadfast through winter’s cold—auspicious sign.
Tiny buds first bloom,
outshining all other fragrances.
Let not the graceful one overstep the powdered wall.
Let Huan Yi play his flute—
what harm in his artful strains?
Nature’s beauty unfolds in golden splendor.
Peerless charm, pure and rare—
the fragrance of a single sprig of plum.

**Two Poems to the Tune of "Voicing Hidden Feelings"**
Yin and yang cycle—let no deviation arise.
Hold to correctness, let not the heart stray.

Perpetual tending of the alchemical furnace and crucible,
Dragon and Tiger stir the Three Carts.
Gather the divine water, refine the essence’s splendor,
congeal the numinous cinnabar.
Within the crystal palace,
jade hare and golden rooster
spit forth blossoms of jade radiance.

Again:
One day’s autumn hues, emerald as if painted.
The wild goose trills its high song.
Mountains resplendent, waters bright—mirroring each other,
mist-laden trees reflecting on the brook’s bridge.
White waves surge,
cloud-waves billow,
brushing the light robe.
Returning, deep in intoxication,
until dusk descends,
moonlight cresting the pine boughs.

**To the Tune of "Tang Duoling"**
Cease this bitter striving for silks,
how long does a human life endure?
Alas—these hundred years,
but a dream of Nanke.
Wealth and honor, fame and achievement—all as one desires,
yet none escape the grindstone of death and life.
*Ye luo.*

Follow your portion, nurture harmony with heaven,
yang flourishes, the crucible brims full.
Within, simmer and seethe,
congealing the numinous waves.
Refine the golden elixir until its light suffuses the body,
merge into one qi,
pervading the sahā world.
*Ye luo.*

**Four Returning Songs**
The Way of long life,
in daily practice abides in emptiness.
One qi first divides, clearly moving and still,
the Three Powers transform, revealing sinking and floating.
The jade hare pursues the spirit crow.

Rumbling through the cosmos,
a single strike shatters the dark thoroughfare.
Light pierces the White Tiger’s brow on Three Mountains,
flames fly from the twin strands of the Red Dragon’s whiskers,
illuminating the night-shining pearl.

Again:
The work of cultivation—
sever love, cut off entanglements.
Body purified, heart cleansed, the Dao-eye bright,
within, uphold the untainted, qi and spirit whole.
True mercury refines true lead.

Set the furnace and crucible,
proceed with fire, let it simmer and boil.
Gently ladled, hammered into flakes,
round and round, congealed into a precious pearl.
Beyond the body, transform into a flying immortal.

The True Constant Dao,
in daily practice pervades the three thousand worlds.
Vast, it encompasses beyond heaven and earth;
small, it circles even a grain of sand or mustard seed.
In every thing, the Mystery is fully known.

Mighty spiritual power,
within the undifferentiated, moves in ceaseless return.
Shattering empty space into seven or eight fragments,
a luminous pearl rolls forth from the sea turtle’s edge.
Its light joins the flaming demon-heaven.

Again:
Forsake worldly thoughts,
all the ten thousand kinds are utterly empty.
Singing by the pillow, sleeping at night, dreams of wandering cease;
half a window’s bright moon, a curtain’s breeze.
Gently, one awakens in a hazy drowse.

Donning robes, sitting,
at once beholding the original countenance.
In the quiet chamber, radiance arises, vast qi surging;
in the empty hall, auspicious signs reveal divine work.
Light shines within the jade flask.

*Jiangshenzi*
The cinnabar flower vainly clings to a false frame,
long buried, inviting misfortune and calamity.
Tiny mayflies, all are pressed by death and life.
Suddenly awakening, knowing self and other perish,
letting form and emptiness come before the eyes.

The golden crow beneath the sea first appears,
the azure sky opens, free of the slightest dust.
Light densely spreads across the heavens,
brilliant light returns before the face.
Intertwined splendor—jade-like youths outshine jade,
like snow reflecting a single plum branch.

*Shengshengman (Seven Poems)*
The human heart is hard and stubborn,
unwilling to turn back.
Deeply submerged in the bitter sea, lingering.
Wine, sex, wealth, and qi—never forsaken,
when will it ever end?
Hearing early, seek the path of return,
joyfully drifting like clouds and water.
No entanglements, no vexations, no sorrows,
no joys, no cares.

Gradually entering the cool, living practice,
embracing heaven’s true purity, a single qi harmonious and gentle.
Matching frost-like lead, repeatedly gathering transformations within the crucible.
Gently, the golden elixir gradually congeals;
later, the work complete, seizing immortality’s companions.
Worthy of returning,
riding the phoenix and crane, ascending to
the Purple Court and Penglai Isles.

Again:
The heart floats, easily moved,
familiar scenes hard to forget.
Hurried all day long, restless.
Already past middle age,
like the fading light of dusk.
Just as a dying lamp fears dawn,
like wind-blown withered leaves turning yellow.
Most bitter is the sigh—
as stars shift and things change,
one is seized by impermanence.

Seeing through, seek the path of return,
knocking earnestly at the Mystery Gate,
discussing the immortal’s recipe.
Entrusted with intimate transmission,
calm the heart, in the quiet chamber ponder deeply.
Polish the ice-like platform until it gleams,
revealing divine light, merging into the numinous yang.
Perfectly bright and manifest,
attaining long life and enduring vision,
eternal peace and well-being.

Again:
Time swiftly passes,
like ants in an endless cycle.
Back and forth, unbroken in succession.
A year gone by,
unaware, another year has already come.
Suddenly, the limit of impermanence arrives—
what can one delay in the journey ahead?
The work of cultivation:
others may have a share,
but oneself has no fate for it.

If one turns back in awakening,
forsaking fame, wealth, and honor,
detached beyond the world.
Preserve the original essence,
in the jade furnace, simmer flakes of snow.
Vaguely, heaven and earth become radiant and clear,
brilliant and translucent, the sun’s light dazzling.
The Three Lights shine,
blending the one numinous true nature,
escorting it to the Jade Heaven.

Again:
The busy fool, burdened and dull,
unaware of others’ praise.
Wildly chasing absurdities, acting recklessly.
Stubborn and witless,
vainly seeking, wildly guessing.
Hasty words, empty quarrels,
battling ignorance, galloping in strange perversities.
Forcing ruin,
blocking others, burying oneself.

If one awakens to the celestial mechanism’s secret,
knocking once at the Mystery Pass,
the jeweled cavern’s gate opens.
The jade maiden and golden youth,
entering and exiting, nestling side by side.
Naturally, yin and yang unite,
in the void, giving birth to an immortal embryo.
The True Person appears,
leaping over the turtle palace and sun hall,
roaming freely at will.

Again:
Hard and soft, strong and weak,
good and evil clearly distinguished.

The responses of Heaven and Earth differ:
Those who muddy the Way to flaunt prosperity,
while the steadfast and virtuous languish in poverty.
The wondrous Dao of purity and non-action
is slandered by fools as a heretical gate.
How can they understand?
To those true cultivators who refine themselves,
they appear as enemies.
The lofty Dao is suspected as theft and banditry,
while the vicious and stubborn are deemed worthy.
Adorned in fine robes and sashes,
versed in etiquette, yet blind to rank.
The masses learn only to brawl,
heedlessly debating human ethics.
All is swept aside—
cloud-patterned robes and hairpins exchanged
for a simple headscarf.

Again:
Wisdom and folly intermingle,
right and wrong entangled in the thicket,
clear and turbid matters urgently confused.
How many, in ignorance,
speak recklessly, indulging in absurdities?
The phoenix chick is called a sparrow,
the sacred *chun* tree mistaken for a morning mushroom.
Even if one were as eloquent as Sui He or Lu Jia,
there would be no door for reasoned debate.
Niu Que feigns benevolence and righteousness,
while Xiang Wu, eyes locked, obscures his celestial truth.
Blind men groping an elephant,
day and night, unaware of light or dark.
The jade chime is used as cooking fuel,
the sacred *hulian* vessel treated as a mere mortar.
Most grievous of all—
jade zithers burned, phoenix plumes boiled,
the qilin and unicorn slain in error.

Again:
Time flies swiftly,
summer departs, winter arrives,
suddenly announcing another new year.
Forms shift, appearances change,
all silently worn away in obscurity.
Who realizes that each person grows older,
youthful verdancy replaced by silver hair and aged countenance?
Wasted away,
like fallen blossoms and drifting catkins,
gone with the flowing water, never to return.
Yet if one turns the light inward,
stirring the spiritual pivot with a single strike,
shattering the twin barriers,
the luminous pearl of the sea shines,
its radiant flame connecting with Kunlun’s peak.
The jewel of inherent nature illuminates the body,
transforming the mortal frame,
nurturing the immortal elixir.
The Jade Dawn appears,
soaring through the central heavens,
transcendent and free beyond the worldly.

**Nan Ke Zi**
A thousand things exist before awakening,
the heart opens to nothingness.
In the struggle between being and non-being,
awareness suddenly clarifies the void.
Within the chaos, yang pours forth,
a single point piercing the celestial crow.
Auspicious vapors coil in the golden crucible,
auspicious smoke plays in the jade vessel.
In the jade vessel and golden crucible,
the spirit pearl is refined.
Its light, resplendent as flowing clouds,
slowly ascends to the celestial Wu.

**Tian Zi Cai Sang Zi**
Withdraw early from the thicket of fame and profit,
I urge you to turn your heart,
cutting off all dissipation.
When stirred, the demon hordes are instantly subdued—
do not let them encroach.
The nine worms slain, the three corpses destroyed,
entrusting yourself to the Dao,
who then is your confidant?
On a clear night, dustless, the moon climbs the peak,
gazing toward the grove of *qian* trees.

**Jian Zi Cai Sang Zi**
Alas, this bodily form—
a hundred deceptions,
twisted into wild perversities.
Now awakened, I seek the path of return,
pure as ice, flawless as jade,
soaring to towering heights,
why cling to the vulgar cliff?
The heart, still as an ice terrace,
its spiritual light lustrous,
untouched by the slightest dust.
Suddenly, another wondrous truth emerges—
□ and *sheng* unite as one,
ascending through the mysterious, feather-transformed,
shedding the mortal husk.

**Ta Suo Xing (Two Poems)**
Within primordial chaos,
traces vanish into the boundless.
From the vast expanse of *hongmeng* and *mingxing*,
the universe first unfolds.
In the hollow void, a single sun-star,
its divine wind and qi expanding in majesty.
Graceful as ice-formed flesh,
jade cliffs stretch across the azure.

A crane startles heaven and earth—
a single bird soaring.
Not merely traversing the Great Void,
it shatters a thousand walls of Mount Jing.
Moreover, nurturing *qi* and preserving spirit,
its essence grows firm and unyielding.
How could the muddled vessel of mortal form comprehend?
The pearl of the heart leaps into the Great Void,
the Jade Infant’s divine transformations unlocking the gates of mystery.
Chasing away the Golden Crow,
pursuing the Jade Hare’s return,
congealed yang refines and ascends in immortal flight.
Pure tones and fragrant breezes escort its farewell from the Jasper Terrace,
as the Perfected One, drunk, reclines in Penglai’s affairs.

**The Oxherd**
Essence depleted, soul scattered, spirit adrift.
Heavenly truth warped into delusion.
Chasing appearances, the nature dims,
adrift in the bitter sea, rushing and wandering.
The path ahead—how treacherous to navigate.
I urge you all: cultivate the Supreme Dao early.
The Supreme Dao pervades all knowledge, luminous,
its radiance outshining Li Lou and Huan the Master.

**Yu Meiren**
Within the Cavern Origin, a single point of celestial light,
luminous and pure as a thousand suns.
Silver rosy clouds shimmer, threading through the earthly realm.
Myriad spirits gather in awe,
suddenly, boundlessly bright.
From the void emerges an embryonic immortal,
graceful as the wind’s drift.
It strikes open the heavens’ vault, ascending through clouded jade,
where jeweled towers and jasper pavilions
inscribe its name upon the Jade Register.

**Dao Lian Zi (Two Poems)**
Speak of the Golden Elder,
discourse on the Yellow Matriarch—
naturally paired, they refine harmony.
Molten cinnabar fills the crucible,
abundant and overflowing.
Divine light manifests,
illuminating the Celestial River.
A single point of fetal radiance emerges from the vast waves,
revealing the Three Clarities,
ascending to the Great Luo.

**True Lead and Mercury,**
Kan and Li in harmony.
Two reversed, yet naturally fitting.
Refining the golden elixir,
radiant as the sun’s brilliance.
Penetrating the profound mystery,
attaining the subtle and hidden.
The Crimson Maiden and Infant ever ride dragon and tiger.
Ascending to the Immortal Capital,
uniting with the sacred mechanism.

**Four Jade Tablets (Two Poems)**
A single point, luminous and pure,
like ice and jade, unsullied.
Through kalpas unborn, undying,
transcending ancient and present without pause.
Gazing boundlessly,
true emptiness gathers all.
Only then is the wondrous key understood—
the profound principle few discern.
Two paths diverge at Caoxi’s node,
mirrored in water, the moon in empty sky.

Again,
Within the false, the true is sought—yet the true essence differs.
Wisdom’s illumination pierces the vast heavens.
The sun gleams, the void crystalline,
spirit-light enfolding all.
Sealed in azure vastness,
congealed in emerald hue.
Attaining this, the heart opens to the wondrous key,
self and other both dissolve.
Beyond birth and death, in endless clarity,
there is yet another—
the eternal moon in boundless sky.

**Willow Branches (Seven Poems)**
Reclining, coiled in stillness, gazing into the precious mirror,
eyes without flaw.
Purified vision, like an infant’s,
upright in bearing.
Ask where this night leads—
to the immortal’s tryst.
A boat laden with emptiness returns by moonlight,
ascending to the Jasper Pool.

Again,
Within, the compass and square reveal the root of the lineage,
the Dao flows through.
In solitude, abiding in the Primordial Palace,
awakening to true emptiness.
Gazing above and below—nothing remains,
with whom to share?
Roaming freely, seated alone in moonlight,
accompanied by the pure wind.

Again,
Suddenly perceiving the round and bright, the image of ease,
mystery without end.
Auspicious mist drifts into the Jade Clarity Palace,
the moon hangs in the void.
Nature’s essence, naturally pure, the ancient Dao—
with whom to share?
Willow branches set in a precious vase,
a fine family tradition.

Again,
Precious nature perfected, rising and descending in harmony,
inwardly probed to its depths.
Threefold misty radiance illumines the Jade Palace,
flames soaring into the void.
The Jade Yang’s clarity refines the precious sign,
naturally harmonized.
The Valley Spirit soars within the Primordial,
playing in the immortal’s wind.

Again,
Who has seen the western dawn’s brocade adornments,
a scene beyond compare?
Mist-wreathed willow banks reflect the slanting sun,
a realm of water and clouds.
The home mountain lies near, yet none approach—
what wondrous scenery!
Stepping into emptiness, ascending to the azure chamber,
the grotto-heaven endures.

Again,
The crane’s nature, lofty and far-reaching, climbs beyond,
passing Tong Pass.
Deep autumn, rain cleared, robes suddenly thin,
water and clouds chill.
How could one bear the taint of fame and profit in years past?
Better to return early.
In the twilight, villages fade into the mist,
gazing toward home.

Again,
In the year of Mao, a tumbleweed drifting to distant mountains,
water and clouds at leisure.
Know that a thousand ages weary of the human realm—
longing to return.
Exchanging bones, shedding the fetal husk, retracing the old path,
restoring youthful countenance.
Stepping into emptiness, ascending to the ancient Star Altar,
riding the cloud-phoenix.

**Farewell to a Hundred Masters (Willow Branches)**
Wild cranes and solitary clouds depart and return,
hard to detain.
Heart-rending, the bond of love’s two passions,
tears like scattered beads.
After autumn, the homeward path is desolate and distant—
hasten the climb.
By Luoyang’s misty shores, willow-fringed banks,
gazing toward home.

**Crossing the Mountain Stream**
A man’s single resolve—
never let the initial aspiration wane.
In decisive rectitude, hold fast to integrity,
casting aside all reckless impulses.
Following conditions, letting fate take its course,
clouds and water as livelihood.
Beneath green pines, amid emerald bamboo,
lies a true and savory taste.

Serene and empty, tranquil and still—
this is the plan for the remainder of life.
Qi settled, spirit naturally harmonized,
advancing the mysterious pearl, emerging from Kan’s position.
Glowing crimson, faintly entering Li’s palace,
connecting above and below,
illuminating the ten directions,
gathering all realms into the heart’s ground.

**Nocturne (Four Poems)**
Earth, water, fire, wind—the four great elements,
for you, a hundred harms arise.
Let each depart in its own way,
and my Dharma-body becomes light and free.
At ease, at ease—
transcending the three realms in wondrous transformation.

Again,

Old friends—no word from any,
alone I sit by ancient cliffs, who shares my silence?
Turning my head toward the river homeland,
scattered auspices drift like duckweed, nearly touching.

Grief and resentment,
grief and resentment—
a single leaf of wind-sail carries me lightly away.

Again,

Facing the southern bank of the green stream,
endless flowing water and falling blossoms.
Turning my head through the mist of fine weather,
my Dao-companions fade from sight.

A long sigh,
a long sigh—
a single leaf of wind-boat gently drifts.

Again,

A man of integrity, resolute and pure,
beyond this, no distinction remains.
The solitary moon stands ever-round,
merging into the jade-green pool, limpid and clear.

Congealing, congealing—
purer than ice and snow in a jade vessel.

**Night Travel Boat (Two Poems)**

Tiger far, Heavenly Stem swallows Phoenix Tail.
The fire-wheel turns, Mount Gen begins to rise.
Pouring into the cauldron, flames blaze,
boiling the divine water—
the union of earth’s essence and heaven’s marrow.

Refining the pure yang elixir to suffuse the body,
exchanging the mortal frame to depart the dusty world.
Hastening the crane-chariot,
following immortal companions,
we ascend at dawn to Jade Purity’s Primordial Beginning.

Again,

Vows declared, heartfelt words spoken,
all things and sentiments cast aside in haste.
Heart and mouth at odds,
unable to discern truth from falsehood—
undoing the return to the mysterious gate’s achievement.

Indulging the will in wrongdoing, hard to admonish,
karma deep and transgressions boundless.
In the cold night’s wind-knives,
ghosts and spirits tug and provoke—
how can you not tremble with fear?

**Welcoming Immortals**

The Dao is not distant,
though Kunlun stands between.

**In Meditative Repose**

In silent sitting, the spirit probes the profound.
Within this cultivation—no schemes, no strategies.
A single gleaming speck of gold,
its jewel-bright radiance blazing in the furnace.
Plucked, the sacred lingzhi;
harvested, the coiled peach.
Auspicious qi flows, filling the purple paths.
Jade lads chant,
golden youths clap.
White cranes and azure simurghs,
clustered in welcome for the immortal guest.

**Two Poems of Grotto-Heaven Spring**

The Dao’s essential immortal mechanism—
sudden awakening alone reveals it,
all things cast aside without remainder.
Behold the original, single nature,
piercing the vastness of heaven’s expanse,
lucid as autumn’s moon,
pure as a cold spring.
Deep and limpid, utterly still,
not a mote of dust clings—
entering and exiting the Dragon Realm,
the Purple Palace of Heaven.
At the return to the origin,
it answers to the Boundless, the Great Beginning,
before the vast kalpas of time.

The Primordial One’s qi stretches unbroken,
heedless of summer’s heat or winter’s cold,
unchanging through all shifts.
Like the great void—
subtle, dense, flawless—
though the three disasters and kalpas crumble,
it remains serene as ever.
Thus in emptiness there is no birth or death,
from the most ancient past,
eternally enduring, ageless.
The true and constant Dao—
this is the Mysterious Origin’s Sage Ancestor,
transmitted through ten thousand generations.

**Again**

At the first division of creation,
a single transformation: the hidden dragon,
the undifferentiated splits into the Two Modes.
Behold the sun’s essence, the moon’s marrow,
congealing lead, binding mercury,
yin and yang in reversal,
tiger leaping, dragon soaring.
The hexagrams of Pi and Tai alternate,
Zhun and Meng return—
the *Yi*’s images emerge from Kan and Li.
Pure and refined,
it illumines the ignorant and the fledgling,
transmuting them into radiant clarity.

How vast and wondrous, the supreme Dao!
Yet who would turn their heart back to the old gate?
The earth’s great turtle bears aloft the vault of heaven,
where towering peaks stand proud,
a solitary moon casts its limpid glow.
Seas stilled, skies empty,
no flying dust intrudes—
the crisp qi, the spirit’s clarity, the marvelous mechanism.
The path to the true opens,
the mortal frame exchanged for one resplendent,
riding the wind to return.

**Three Poems to "Court of Blossoms"**

Among the ten thousand things,
humankind is most noble,
holding within a single spark of the subtle and refined.
Most numinous, most sagely—
who in daily use perceives it?
Hidden or manifest, born or extinguished, flowing with change,
square or round, bending or straight—all meet the moment.
From its transformations,
whether walking, dwelling, sitting, or lying,
movement and stillness ever attend.

Suddenly,
light suffuses the body—
the True Person appears,
clad in a different majesty.
Jade hairpins and vermilion slippers,
sashes of jade pendants and brocade tassels.
A jeweled canopy, a phoenix chariot,
clouds of jade trailing,
the graceful True Consort.
Immortal music plays,
golden lads bear the goblets—
drunk as mud, they revel.

**Again**

Shedding the gross for the splendid,
returning to simplicity, restoring antiquity,
the root-source, once turbid, slowly clears.

Humble and modest, dwelling in depth,
what is worn need not be new to endure.
Contentment knows neither glory nor shame,
serene in mastery—neither hasty nor light.
Do you yet understand?
Existence and extinction, gain and loss,
advance and retreat—all like waxing and waning.
Thus,
wholly may the Dao be preserved:
from the heart, dross is cast out;
from the eyes, nails are drawn.
Dim pupils brighten like feathers in flight,
the empty valley shines in vast clarity.
Three qi intermingle in dense harmony—
pure yang descends,
illuminating form, liberating mind.
Condensing, returning to the source,
wind stills, waves settle,
bright moon gilds the earth and seas.

**Again**

Jade dust and numinous frost,
cloud essence in secluded purity—
the Three Treasures of primal chaos hold fullness.
Fullness, then return—
sun and moon pierce Kunming’s depths.
□ grasps the realm of round penetration,
qi descends in misty profusion,
heavenly treasures bloom as sacred infants.
Within this mystery,
five peaks send flying snow,
one dwells in the crystal city.
Divine jade opens the ancient path,
spirit winds shift with ease—
who guards the distant years?
I ponder my long flow, enduring vision,
the profound verses ever sincere.
Secretly transmitted elixir must transform the body;
from this, ascend to wander Huaqing’s halls.
Golden lads summon—
in the Jade Dawn Palace,
the self belongs to the Lesser Weaving Star.

---

**Four Western River Moons**

Still and solitary, the thatched hut stands free,
steep peaks seal mist and rosy clouds.
Beyond the sunlit pavilion, a single branch slants—
awaiting guests with clear tea and quiet words.
Silent sitting, effortless in purity,
not a speck of dust or sand clings.
The heart’s terrace, white as the lotus,
ever abides beneath the Western River Moon.

**Again**

To pore over a thousand scriptures is still too little;
to awaken to a single word is yet too much.

Within the cauldron of Great Void, refine the harmonious and tranquil.
Nurtured thus, a myriad of dark pearls coalesce.
Following principle, roam directly through the jeweled realm;
on the path of profound emptiness, traverse the starry river.
Ten thousand spirits gather, piercing the misty veil—
in oneness, no division of self and other.

---

**Again**
The Lesser Reclusion admits not a speck of dust;
the Great Permeation fills all directions.
Merged with the numinous expanse, boundless and vast—
one nature grasps the great image.
Within fire, white snow is forged;
in water, the crimson sun is nurtured.
The jade infant, wondrously transformed, rides phoenix and simurgh,
soaring into the moon above the Western River.

---

**Again**
Unwilling to seek within the self,
stubbornly grasping outward in ceaseless pursuit.
Clinging to lesser arts of side doors, long mired in delusion—
such folk are hard to save.
Like one who guards a tree awaiting a hare,
how much better to brave the snow astride an ox.
In the land of Hua Xu, roam at will—
at midnight, turn night back to day.

---

**Three Long Thoughts on Immortality**

Subtle within the profound—
mercury and lead.
Advance the fire, laboring as the cauldron seethes and boils.
Spirit-sand, round in every grain.
Inner work complete,
outer ascent to immortality.
Divine water flows deep, reversing course to ascend the heavens—
lightly borne on a single lotus leaf.

---

**Again**
The Dao is level and smooth.

**Nature’s Subtle Dependence**

Nature leans on the elusive—
water and fire conjoin, the low and the high.
Yin and yang meet in their own time.
Use the Flowery Pond,
bathe the jade-like flesh.
A radiant child soars beyond the heavens—
divine light illumines the Purple Tenuity.

**Again**

Moonlight Pool,
bathe the sacred tortoise.
From its mouth, auspicious clouds transform to jade rainbows—
spiritual radiance gleams in the Purple Tenuity.

Crimson robes gleam,
veiling skin like ice.
Graceful, it drifts on the wind beyond the heavens—
the Jasper Palace awaits its destined hour.

**Two Boating Songs**

Sharp as refined essence at night’s end,
yang’s flame and luminous splendor dispel evil.
The jeweled *Brahmā* crystal pierces the void with its gaze.
The cinnabar phoenix flourishes—
ten thousand spirits bow in submission.
The wondrous work of non-action unfolds naturally.
Weave the horned net without error.
Where are my companions?
None remain.
I speak to the clear wind and bright moon—
they are mine.

**Again**

From the primal depths, the mind refines to its end.
The boundless *wangxiang* governs good and evil.
Its dark scrutiny is impartial, never missing or erring.
Truth and falsehood—
all

**Ten Odes on the Skull by Gu Shehou Shanyuan**

**The Skull Is Not**
The skull is not, the skull is not—
a heap of white bones lies on the sandbank.
Where now are glory, wealth, and honor?
Only the white poplar and the ancient stele remain.

**The Skull’s Greed**
The skull was greedy, the skull was greedy,
well-versed in fame, profit, wealth, and desire.
Shattering worldly toil beyond the dust,
a single spirit’s true nature emerges from the clouded hermitage.

**The Skull’s Wrath**
The skull was wrathful, the skull was wrathful,
quelling the fire, stilling the heart, severing self and others.
Nurturing divine radiance to pierce the azure vault,
a day of emptiness cleanses the red dust.

**The Skull’s Delusion**
The skull was deluded, the skull was deluded,
seeing through all yet knowing nothing.
Embracing the one true awakened nature,
auspicious light softly rises in crimson robes.

**The Skull’s Sorrow**
The skull was sorrowful, the skull was sorrowful,
leaping free from fleeting splendor—all things cease.
Gazing upon the primordial Dao of heaven,
the moon of the empty heart illumines clear autumn.

**The Skull Knows**
The skull knows, the skull knows,
turning light inward in ineffable reflection.
Recognizing the original true face,
a single flash of spirit reaches the heavens.

**The Skull Laughs**
The skull laughs, the skull laughs,
shattering the mountain of attachment to seek the wondrous.
Surveying all beneath heaven, embracing the void,
round clarity endures through kalpas without depletion.

**The Skull Speaks**
The skull speaks, the skull speaks,
comprehending the subtle and formless with ease.
Nurturing the nameless in emptiness,
dim and distant, it merges with the cold radiance.

**The Skull Declares**
The skull declares, the skull declares,
a jade pillar pierces the heavens.
Ten thousand rays of rosy dawn lean on the firmament—
only then does the true heart awaken to its natural distinction.

**The Skull Rests**
The skull rests, the skull rests,
carefree and at ease, joy without sorrow.
Shedding its shell, it roams the celestial river,
