riding the phoenix and crane to the Isles of Yingzhou.

---

**Following the Ancient Rhyme**

Earth’s *qi* billows and gradually congeals,
chaos spreads across the Milky Way, the heavens unlit.
Swept away by me, I raise my hairpin to gaze—
alone, the high void reveals the radiant sun’s clarity.

A sweep clears the azure sky, the universe stills,
brilliant, the Three Realms emerge from evening clouds.
From my embrace, I bring forth the full moon,
ten thousand forms arrayed without a single blemish.

Deluded clouds brushed away, the Three Mountains gleam,
worldly mists dispersed, the four horizons clear.
Beneath, the restless borders settle at last—
raising my head, the vast void shines in its entirety.

The sea of awakening, limpid as autumn waters,
the boundless void, serene as undisturbed waves.
The spirit youth presents flawless jade—
its radiance shines boundlessly, illuminating all.

Long concealed in gloom, heaven and earth darkened,
clouds gathered, mists amassed—suddenly, clarity.
Following the wind, I bring down the moon from the sky’s edge,
amidst the throng of ten thousand forms, it shines alone.

Extending my hand, I part the summit of the Milky Way,
the distant void expands, the great emptiness brightens.
The Primordial Qian grants me vast spiritual power—
flashing yang’s light, a thousand miles gleam.

---

**Following the Ancient Rhyme Again**

Suddenly, a single point grasps the true mechanism,
seizing the mysterious pearl, rare in the world.
Luminous and pure, unstained by dust,
incense burns in the golden tripod as coiled smoke ascends.

In the zither hall, silently pondering the mystery,
outside the gate, moss grows thick where few tread.
The Daoist abode is desolate, free of worldly things—
pine winds scatter fallen petals in disarray.

Comprehending the true essence, the highest mechanism,
in emptiness, faintly discerned, beyond the dust’s reach.
A single point of yang light pierces the void—
steadily riding the fragrant wind, cranes take flight in chaos.

I preserve one method to seize heaven’s mechanism,
mastering divine skill, unmatched in the world.
Spirit youths attend at the Jade Palace,
riding dragons over the Miluo River in flight.

Attaining the wondrous mystery beyond mysteries,
my family’s supreme Dao is exceedingly rare.
From emptiness, the nameless simplicity stirs—
a single spirit’s light soars beyond the heavens.

The golden gate turns the pivot of mechanism,
a few streaking stars emerge, rare in the world.
Divine power forces open the Qian and Kan positions,
shaking the vast sea, soaring to the heavens.

---

**Pervading All**
Pervading the ten directions, filling all with misty *qi*,
drifting down to the human realm, connecting everywhere.
Spirit harmonizes with the Dao’s depth, the blazing sun gleams,
nature aligns with the round sea, moon’s radiance like wind.

**Primordial Beginning**
The Heavenly Worthy establishes teachings throughout *Saha*,
universally saving sentient beings with the Dao’s harmonious *qi*.
Reflecting back to the origin, casting off the snowy waves,
returning light, jade dew scatters upon the starry river.

**Communing with the True**
Seeing through the illusory body of the skin-sack,
searching deeply for the mystery, leaping beyond the mortal cage.
Kan and Li ascend and descend, divine light flashes—
sun and moon conjoin, piercing the cauldron’s red.

**Substance and Function**
The Dao’s power and spiritual might pervade the great thousand,
formless and traceless, penetrating mountains and rivers.
At Caoxi’s waves, clear fish play—
the celestial shore’s waves pure, the sea of awakening profound.

**Turning from Awareness**
Sentient beings, unaware, waste their youth,
obscuring the luminous clarity of kalpas’ truth.
Restless, fierce, and stubborn, clinging fast,
the fire of ignorance ignites, indulging greed and wrath.

**Deluded from the True**
Before the eyes, sun and moon lie beyond the heavens,
the clear void obscured by veiling membranes.
Washing away the clamor of dust, returning to clarity,
the jade infant’s divine transformation pierces clouds and mist.

**Transformation**
A single *qi* in the primal void of the Great Beginning,
the high emptiness ablaze with dawn’s rosy glow.
Encompassing the cosmos without the slightest obstruction,
illuminating heaven and earth, wisdom’s power flows.

**Harmonious Fusion**
Auspicious smoke fills the gate, nurturing the golden pass,
the bellows and key of emptiness allow free passage.
Flowing mercury fills the cauldron to its brim—
cloudy waves surge high upon Jade Capital Mountain.

**Opening the Origin**
First issuing the primordial Dao’s *qi*,
within the pot, a single flavor simmers like snowflakes.
Flowing through, it irrigates the cauldron, the Jade Pool pure—
swallowing it whole, the body becomes utterly clear.

**Union**
Lead and mercury devour each other in the cauldron,
refining sun and moon, forging the void.
Kunlun’s fire blazes without smoke or flame—
nurturing the divine elixir, it shoots into the jade pot.

**Spiritual Abyss**
Vast and distant, the immortal source, deep as the sea’s eye,
twin springs gently ripple with water’s gold.
Dragons hidden in the pool’s depths, wind and waves stilled,
tigers crouch by the stream, ancient tones resonate.

**Gathering Transformation**
All become the great Dao’s transforming spiritual work,
gathering the mystery into the cauldron.
Refining the golden elixir to radiant purity,
a single pill seals the Five Luminous Palaces.

**Seizing the Mystery**
By the river, seizing the Black Dragon’s tail,
on the summit, overturning the White Tiger’s head.
Snatching a single night-shining pearl,
a thousand beams of light stream to the heavens.

**Dual Passes**
Spirit and demon commune, each with their own intent,
naturally, the heart settles, revealing true spirit.
Enabling the Crimson Maiden to play at Fusang,
allowing the Infant to frolic in the moon’s radiance.

**Ascent and Descent**
The Three Palaces ascend and descend, sprouting the spirit-sprout,
the crucible and tripod fly with frost, spitting emerald sand.
Radiance scatters, filling the heavens with blooming red pistils,
heaven and earth are sown with the fair golden flower.

**Illumination**
The Dao-eye gazes upon the sky—all is clarity,
the precious tripod levels the mercury within.
Red frost flakes drift past the golden gate,
white snow clusters descend upon the Jade Capital.

**Generation and Completion**
Yin and yang exchange by nature’s decree,
the myriad transformations arise from a single principle.
Attaining the One, unbound and truly free,
carefree and joyous in the mystery’s core.

**Perfected One**
The Perfected One of the Numinous Treasure holds a revered rank,
often ascending the lunar palace, leaping through the divine grove.
In the Three Clarities’ realm, roaming the vast expanse,
the jade pendants’ chime resounds across the four seas.

**Divine Transformation**
The Perfected One sits alone, hidden in the cloudy void,
condensing emerald mists to greet the distant court.
In stillness, the eyes gather moonlight’s glow,
jade lotuses array in two or three shoots.

**Fetal Radiance**
A single point of the celestial sphere—a shooting star falls,
illuminating the flask’s interior with flickering light.
Having refined the fetal immortal to return home,
eternally dwelling in the Three Clarities’ pavilion.

**Luminous Perception**
The fire-screen is parted, opening the Dharma-eye,
ignorance swept away, revealing the starry net.
The high heavens push forth a thousand heaps of jade,
the level earth surges with ten-thousand-zhang waves.

**Vast Embodiment**
Nameless, selfless, and formless,
as one body, gazing upon the ancient imperial capital.
Shallow wisdom and dull roots breed clinging views—
how could they know the light arrayed in the eye’s abyss?

**True Essentials**
The great mystery’s true awakening transcends worldly toil,
suddenly enlightened, the empty heart raises the Dao-eye high.
Naturally, jade lads attend the Purple Court,
in the lush heavens, riding a golden-furred steed.

**Mighty Spirit**
I embrace the celestial wind’s true primordial bones,
transformed by my master’s touch into immortal talent.
In the world, none match the copper-headed man,
dancing with the sword, its light cleaving the jeweled terrace.

**Immortal Cassia**
In the lunar palace, the cassia remains unpicked,
in the Purple Court, the peach blooms toward the sun.
These two treasures gathered and placed in the tripod,
their fragrance alike, perfuming the immortal steps.

**Blending of Things**
Congealed perfection densely reaches the azure heavens,
vast and lush, it hangs in the void, locking the emerald mist.
High above, the azure clouds roll back, opening the lunar palace—
the two barbarian gates’ feathered transformations array as golden immortals.

**Divine Sword**
Honed to three feet, sharp as frost and snow,
its sunlight rivals brilliance, flashing like lightning.
Last night at the third watch, it repaid vengeance,
the blue blade stained with the blood of apes.

**Seeing Through**
Wealth, fame, riches, and desire—do not rigidly seek,
when will the fiery household ever reach its end?
How much better to be a carefree cloud-and-water wanderer,
in the boundless void beyond, attaining true cultivation.

**Exiting the Pass**
A staff slung across the shoulder, bearing a giant alchemical gourd,
a cloud robe borne by the wind, crossing the floating bridge.
A sleeve conceals a three-foot blue-bladed sword,
severing hundreds of black dragons.

**Subtlety and Refinement**
Essence gathers in the subtle mystery, the Dao supremely bright,
shifting spirit through the mortal realm, delighting in purity.
A single yang enters the Three Flowers’ tripod,
two qi are gathered into the Seven Treasures’ vase.

**Water and Fire**
From the eastern sea, rolling flames scorch the sky,
from the western sea, settling waves congeal to crimson.
These two things blend to form heaven and earth’s splendor,
their essence shining throughout, harmoniously fused.

**Vast Wisdom**
The sword hews the golden mountain—spark and fire flow,
the Three Corpses perish together, the ten thousand ties dissolve.
I cast the boundless net into the sky,
scooping up the void, vast as the sun.

**Being and Nonbeing**
Within emptiness, seeking emptiness, recognizing emptiness,
suddenly, within emptiness, the divine power is seen.
From now on, red dust affairs are no longer questioned—
naturally, jade flowers fill the grotto.

**Autumn Night**
A single qi coils, floating beyond the Milky Way’s clarity,
the rustling night rain scatters autumn’s sound.
Ordinary people do not see the Moon Goddess’ cassia,
only I wander alone in the lunar palace.

**Mighty Radiance**
The ten thousand ties severed, all karma dissolved,
suddenly perceiving the wondrous mystery of the formless.
Several patches of dark clouds banished beyond the isles,
a heart-moon fills the empty sky.

**Primordial Harmony**
A single qi first divided, heaven and earth parted,
the Three Powers established forms, transforming the numinous mechanism.
Shifting the heart back into the golden chamber,
it produces a luminous pearl to illuminate the curtains.

**Correct Formula**
The *Dao and Virtue*, the *Yin Talisman*, the *Great Beginning*’s chapters—
students who do not comprehend vainly seek immortality.
Golden script and jade tablets are lightly cast aside—
how can they discern my master’s profound mystery?

**Tranquil Application**
Who in the mystery establishes the still mechanism?
Serene and constant, guarding the Great Abyss’ pool.
The sun’s wheel turns, opening the heart’s path,
heaven and earth are ever observed in minute detail.

**Extinguishing Thought**
Body still, heart clear, intent also clear,
within, constantly guarding the qi and spirit’s tranquility.
Dredging open the treasure trove, the mysterious pearl gleams,
its light illuminating Penglai’s myriad forms.

**Subduing the Dragon**
Rending open the heaven’s crown, roaming at will,
just then seeing the flood dragons frolic in the vast boat.
A great shout shatters mountains and seas—
the sword’s tip pursues the red dragon’s head.

**Divine Elixir**
A single flying elixir guards the upper realm,
the primordial spirit’s essence rivals the sun’s brilliance.
Fiery congealing flames burn the empty expanse,
frightening away the host of yin, all transformed to yang.

**Divine Power**
Pressing the sword, divine might surpasses Huayin,
gnashing teeth in fury, galloping with chest bared.
Piercing the brows, the myriad demons’ courage is shattered,
opening the eyes, the hundred monsters’ hearts are terrified.

**Penetrating the Mystery**
Detached from desire, the empty heart opens the wisdom-eye,
congealing the void, leaning on flawless jade.
The delicate emerald hue releases its splendor,
illuminating the ten directions—who knows contentment?

**Blending and Union**
Descending, the celestial soul; ascending, the earthly soul,
in harmony above and below, without flaw or blame.
The great square encompasses all, without corners,
jade walks and gold flies, interspersed and distinct.

**Lofty Merit**
The Dao and virtue’s pure name spreads to the sea’s edge,
the celestial kitchen bestows blessings, adding to good merit.
One day, soaring and ascending through the Milky Way,
rising into the cloud-deep, playing amidst the emerald mists.

**Divine Might**
By chance, bearing the sword to ascend the celestial net,
slaying a million hosts of yin spirits.
The jade hare startled, retreats to seek its burrow,
the golden crow flies up to the cassia branch.

**Numinous Power**
Seated, the flying sword gallops with divine might,
toppling the celestial net, leveling Mount Taihua.
Pulling down the lunar palace to seize the jade hare,
overturning the solar palace to capture the golden rooster.

**Departing and Descending the Sacred View**
Having become one with the enlightened, discerning truth from falsehood,
not aligning with the deluded, debating right and wrong.
One day, the elixir complete, flying through the cosmos,
the vast void’s boundless body is my return.

**Chen the Immortal Asks: Is the Empty Not Empty?**
The supreme Dao is formless, like the great void,
shifting spirit to blend with things, all bodies become one.
Though rivers and mountains reach their utmost number, they endure here,
heaven and earth’s boundlessness resides within.

**Jia the Immortal Asks: Is It Neither Empty Nor Existing?**

**Jia the Immortal Asks: Is It Neither Empty Nor Existing?**
Neither empty nor existing is perfect completion,
yet clinging to this perfection is but a provisional name.
Having realized the Supreme Mystery, true reality arises—
within appearances, no thing abides, serene and clear.

**Guo the Immortal Asks: The Mystery Within Mystery**
Inquiring the mystery within the mystery,
a mechanism stands beyond heaven, another heaven beyond.
From primordial chaos to the utmost bounds, no trace of obstruction,
the wondrous transformation pervades, the Great Awakened Immortal.

**Jue the Immortal Asks: The Profound and Obscure**
Profound, obscure, the essence in subtle vagueness,
spiritual might shatters heaven’s sinews and bones.
Congealing emptiness, vast and luminous,
standing alone between heaven and earth, not a single thing remains.

**Elder Liu Asks of Body and Function: Unaware of the Immortal Path**
The immortal’s function wields the celestial mechanism, its body vast and square,
congealed yang unfolds, radiating auspicious light.
The elder has already found the path of returning to truth,
unaware, he follows the wind into the imperial realm.

**Jiao the Young Immortal Asks of Renouncing the World**
Shaking off worldly passions, the karmic fire’s pull,
fame and fortune, wealth and honor—all swept away.
A man’s resolve stands firm, soaring to the heavens,
seizing the name to hang among the ranks of immortals.

**Elder Liu Asks of the Wondrous Function of True Emptiness**
True emptiness, the supreme Dao, leaves no trace,
its wondrous function nurtures the spirit, all phenomena as one.
Within the Great One’s flask, the bright moon is gathered,
in the Palace of Broad Cold, the pure wind plays.

**Dong the Immortal Asks of Unyielding Until Death**
Maintaining the original resolve to the very end,
until death, no path leads into the forest of transgression.
Ever guarding the elixir furnace, the three tripods of jade,
ever preserving the cinnabar crucible, the single flask of gold.

**Li the Immortal Asks of Neither Within Nor Without**
Externally, no form; internally, no cultivation,
the middle path departs from subtlety, abandoning all seeking.
All dharmas are swept away as one,
no idle matters strike the heart’s core.

**Elder Qi Asks of the Great Dao**
Suddenly awakened, the mind’s pearl shines,
illuminating the dusty world—nothing remains.
The Daoist attains the essence as the true teaching,
the Chan monk calls this thusness.

**Chen the Immortal Asks of Tortoise Hair and Rabbit Horns**
The wooden horse howls to the heavens, grinding rabbit horns,
the clay ox roars to the earth, scraping tortoise hairs.
Capturing these two, they return to the Yellow Dao,
eternally stabilizing heaven and earth, unshaken.

**Liang the Immortal Asks of Entering the Dao and Returning to Truth**
From youth, pure and steadfast as ice,
endowed with immortal winds and a spirit of wisdom.
Awakened from sleep, the Dao’s eye opens,
startled in dreams, sudden perfect completion.

**[Answers to Questions]**
**Great Zhang the Immortal Asks: Not Dwelling in Mountains, Not Abiding in Hermitages—How to Suddenly Release?**
Thus I compose two verses in response.

Unbound to green mountains, not dwelling in hermitages,
the spirit soars beyond the heavens, emerging from mist and haze.
The crane follows the Purple Palace to pay homage to the Immortal Lord,
the phoenix leads the way to the distant sun to visit the Old Master.

Leaping beyond the thatched hut, not hiding in mountains,
carefree, trusting in the joy of tranquility.
Forever dwelling within heaven and earth,
embracing the moon, ever abiding between sky and land.

**Zhang the Immortal Asks of Not Observing False Appearances to Recognize the True Form**
A heap of foul decay is ultimately false,
the two points of light in the eyes are not worth pride.
To recognize the original source, the true Dharma-body,
observe beyond appearances as if a shooting star.

**[Answers to Questions]**
**Elder Qi Asks: The Goose in the Jar—Growing Large and Flying Out, Neither Harmed**
Born in seclusion, entering the jar,
undaunted, soaring like a phoenix with bold intent.
To ask how both are preserved, both attain sagehood—
the goose flies beyond the heavens, the precious jar remains full.

**Guo the Immortal Asks of Coolness Within Fire**
Flaming fire, blazing like sunlight,
form and spirit both wondrous, attaining coolness.
Eternally one with the Great Beginning, without increase or decrease,
having attained the Mystery’s origin, standing enduringly.

**Li the Immortal Asks of Realizing the Dao**
Meeting with a glance, the Dao is known and understood,
seeing through the emptiness of a thousand sutras and myriad dharmas.
Not dwelling in famous mountains, repeatedly bowing in inquiry,
spared the suffering of wandering clouds and waters in bitter practice.

**Guo the Immortal Asks of Unconfused Until Death**
The great Dao is a single, level, and stable path,
yet veiled by self-delusion, one does not know the return.
Now I point out the celestial thoroughfare for you,
ascending into the Jade Palace to discern the subtle.

**Dong the Immortal Asks of Caoxi**
Recognizing the two paths invading Caoxi,
Jingshan’s shadows intertwine with the Twin Groves.
Though a small stream flows into tiny drops,
it penetrates the spiritual source, the ocean of awakened mind.

**Dang the Immortal Asks of the Ladder to Heaven**
Would you know the ladder to heaven?
Stand jade, cross gold, leaning against the emerald haze.
If you reach the Moon Palace to behold this scene,
it will awaken your clarity to grasp the elixir’s mechanism.

**Lei the Immortal Asks of the Spirit Merging with the Dao**
The Dao’s law has long pervaded the Three Powers,
its spiritual penetration most wondrous, awakening cool clarity.
Merged into one qi, returning to the primordial origin,
standing alone in the precelestial realm of virtue and Dao.

**Guo the Immortal Asks of Being Spirit Without Seeking Spirit**
Ordinary men all worship false spirits,
who would turn inward to recognize their original truth?
If you resolve this within the heart’s core,
on the path of cool clarity, you will laugh at the red dust.

**Yan the Immortal Asks of Internal and External Communion**
Closing the eyes, settling emptiness to reach the wondrous mystery,
opening the light, responding to things, blending with the precelestial.
The harmonious Dao stirs auspicious radiance,
penetrating the distant sun, appearing before the Celestial Emperor.

**Elder Zhang Asks of the State’s Treasured Weapon**
The supreme virtue of the Middle Prime illumines the Golden Kingdom,
the Three Treasures overflow, gleaming like fine jade.
Its benefits constantly nourish the hundred offices,
Heaven bestows upon me true and pure blessings.

**Wang the Immortal Asks of Rare Words as Natural**
Rare words, the supreme Dao, naturally distinct,
unlike the fleeting winds that briefly cease.
Virtue and Dao are ever one with joy,
penetrating the mystery without loss, wondrously pure and absolute.

**Zhang the Immortal Asks of Knowing the White and Guarding the Black**
Unfurling the sun of wisdom, illuminating a thousand rays,
above and below, all is receptive and bright, transformed into yang.
In the quiet of night, embracing the origin, ever silent,
still and unmoving, responding in due time.

**Great Yan the Immortal Asks of the Wondrous Dharma**
The great purity’s wondrous form pierces the empty mystery,
the enlightened open their hearts, boarding the Dharma-boat.
Crossing the vast waves to reach the other shore,
the primordial spirit penetrates the flaming sun’s heaven.

**Elder Liu the Immortal Asks of the Three Teachings Returning as One**
The Tathāgata’s wondrous Dharma speaks of true nature,
the Supreme Master’s mystery expounds the great elixir.
Confucius’ five constants illuminate daily practice,
the three vehicles merge as one in the great void.

Laozi, the Tathāgata, and the Sage Confucius are the same,
yet worldly people do not understand, clashing like winds.
The provisional names of the three teachings—how are they different?
All return to the vast, azure emptiness.

**Young Zhang the Immortal Asks of Giving Life and Nurturing**
The Dao triggers the mechanism of life, virtue nurtures it,
yin and yang’s transformations unfold in their own time.
If you turn this principle to reflect the light,
gaze upward at the Moon Palace to behold the osmanthus branch.

**Lord Dong Asks of Emptiness Giving Birth to Existence**

The Dao’s law arises from emptiness, its root in spontaneity,
giving birth to the great earth and covering the three heavens.
Within, the sun and moon illumine the celestial forms,
the unfolding of yin and yang passed down through ages.

**Elder Zhang Asks Which Gate Is the Path of Cultivation**
Within the gate of purity, recognize the truth,
lest worldly affairs gather in the heart.
If in the forest one points to the path of Caoxi,
sit and watch the Tathāgata enter nirvāṇa.

**Immortal Zhang Asks of Heavenly Nature and Human Nature**
Heavenly nature, dark and profound, connects to the ancestral Dao,
the enlightened call it by this name.
Nurture the heart’s secret mechanism to merge with the primordial,
this is the true mystery of immortals.

**Master Wang Asks of Daily Virtue and Power**
Compassion, kindness, loyalty, and integrity—will pure and clear,
the valley spirit emerges from emptiness.
Grasp the great image to dwell in peace,
everywhere encountering the source, delighting in the Jade Capital.

**Immortal Chen Asks of No Obstruction, No Closure**
The gate of the Great Beginning opens the eye of wisdom,
spiritual light shines through, illuminating the empty valley.
The valley spirit never dies, forever at peace,
embracing all directions without hindrance.

**Great Immortal Yan Asks of the Retribution of Good and Evil**
Evil deeds bring calamity and misfortune,
good works invite heavenly blessings to follow.
Fortune and misfortune are both shaped by people,
each determined by their actions in the moment.

**Immortal Wang Asks of the Three Essentials Merging as One**
Stir the celestial crucible’s aperture,
essence-light blazes like the sun, brightly illuminating.
The primordial mechanism of life and death is established,
the three and one merge into true subtlety.

**Immortal Zhang Asks of the Sun and Moon Within**
The sun and moon exchange their light, great and small distinct,
only then can the elixir be fired in the crucible.
Gradually the sacred work awakens the spirit’s brilliance,
riding the phoenix, congealing yang to meet the Lord of Heaven.

**Lord Zhang Asks of Rising, Falling, Floating, Sinking**
The sun’s essence and moon’s spirit determine floating and sinking,
above and below fuse, great and small intermingle.
Sacred wisdom cleaves open the jade of the celestial well,
divine power presses forth gold filling the pit.

**Great Immortal Yan Asks of the Three and One Undivided**
At the surging bottom of the numinous wave, the three lights shine,
spiritual water flows full, the one Dharma equal.
Standing alone in the vastness, one knows there is form,
silent and solitary, merging with the primordial.

**Exhorting Daoists to Study the Furnace Fire**
People today all study the forging of gold,
who is willing to cast aside greed and refine the original heart?
Those who attain the Dao are unstained by wealth or desire,
what need has the cultivator of true reality for profit or fame?

**Immortal Chen Asks of the Absolute Study**
The absolute study, free of care, penetrates the wondrous principle,
wayward indolence and sloth cannot achieve truth.
If one takes ignorance for the immortal’s path,
foolish maidens and busy men all depart the dust.

**Great Master Zhang Asks of Nature and Life**
Seeing without substance, hearing without sound,
even seeing and hearing are but provisional names.
This original thing admits no comparison,
like wind and moon illuminating the celestial court.

Cherish qi, preserve essence, nurture the mechanism of life,
the spirit-fire in Kan rekindles Li.
As the first yang arises, the Qian’s primordial image appears,
the elixir complete, ascend as an immortal to visit the Purple Tenuity.

**Brother Chen Asks of No Doubt**
Awakening beyond perception, free of knowing,
the spirit contracts with the Dao, both mechanisms forgotten.
If no ignorance arises in the heart,
wondrous transformation ascends into the Great Subtlety.

**Lord Chen Asks of the Northern Dipper**
The seven origins traverse the sea, turning the pivot,
the celestial axle revolves, myriad forms follow.
The Dipper’s handle points back, opening the upper aperture,
all stars bow in reception to the utmost mystery.

**Young Immortal Chen Asks of the Great State Cooking the Small Fry**
The great state, wu-wei, embodies the sovereign’s authority,
the people secure in their work, like cooking a small fish.
Ghosts and spirits meet at the central yellow position,
sun and moon support the true, uniting with spontaneity.

**Exhorting Disciples: Good and Evil Are Not Fixed, the Heart Has Two Uses**
The heavenly net, vast and encompassing, spans all,
discerning people’s good and evil within.
Best to align will and qi with the true and upright,
lest all efforts and diligence come to nothing.

**Immortal Xu Asks of Standing Alone and Unchanging**
The supreme clarity of the Dao stands alone as foremost,
merged as one, unborn, the great image complete.
Still and solitary, unchanging,
from the beginning it abides, establishing the profound mystery.

**Immortal Xu Asks of Merging Things Without End**
A single spark of spiritual light shoots into the great void,
merged and independent, pervading without end.
Unchanged from ancient times to the present,
it embraces heaven and earth as one body.

**Immortal Zhang Asks of Returning to the True and Illuminating Things**
The Kaiyuan era’s awakening illuminates true things,
the wise and sagely attain the same virtue.
Within, embrace the numinous source, distant and refined,
without, preserve the spirit’s knowing, dim and silent.

**Immortal Jue Asks of Heaven and Earth as Substance, Emptiness as Function**
Heaven’s image is Qian’s primordial, earth’s image is Kun,
yin and yang, closure and opening, mutually engulf.
Hard and soft already fixed in floating and sinking positions,
the central Dao, empty of heart, the sun of wisdom rushes forth.

**Immortals Zhang and Guo Ask of Cultivating at Home**
Dwelling at home without defilement, good in the world,
in desire yet without selfishness, apart from worldly splendor.
Not like Zhang Qian, who transcended the sea of suffering,
or Zhang He, who was granted a numinous raft by heaven.

**Elder Liu Asks of Buddhist Karma**
The golden immortal of great awakening speaks of all-knowing,
transforming beings, the Buddha-eye awakens bodhi.
Throughout heaven and earth, there is no karma,
it is only that sentient beings each delude themselves.

**Fellow Daoists Ask**
Those who stray take illusion as calamity and inevitably suffer misfortune.
Clinging to illusion, applying effort, nurturing a calamitous body,
is like filth defiling the heart’s pearl.
Joining the dust, turning from awakening, a thousand truths distant,
abandoning the Dao, departing from the subtle, the myriad things confine.

**They Further Ask of the Upright, Who Take Guidance as the Dao and Inevitably Gain Blessing**
Nurture nature, preserve essence, the supreme Dao becomes clear,
the profound and subtle faintly transform the spirit-infant.
Congealing yang, the great unfolding shines with auspicious light,
in application, flying mystery ascends directly.

**Immortal You Asks of Emerging from Nonbeing into Being**
Emerging from nonbeing, penetrating and revealing the vast image,
entering being, returning to the source, uniting with the original mechanism.
These two inversions are both correct in their secrets,
do not generate distinctions of right and wrong.

**Immortal Xu Asks of Emerging from Being into Nonbeing**
Emerging from being, the abyss of emptiness illumines creation,
entering nonbeing, suddenly awakening to the primordial beginning.
Within emptiness, there are the heaven’s precious treasures,
revealing themselves, exquisitely bright, like pearls in the sea.

**Answering Questions**
One asks of emerging from being into nonbeing, another of emerging from nonbeing into being—how to proceed in practice?
Emerging from nonbeing, see the formless spirit-image,
entering being, awaken to the pearl of nature.
Being and nonbeing, both can be pursued,
illuminating the great antiquity, establishing the primordial beginning.

**Immortal Zhao Asks of the Human Heart Merging with the Heavenly Heart**
The human heart must merge with the heavenly heart,
within and without, clearly knowing to explore the sea of nature.
Recognize the true Dharma-body, not form and appearance,
the numinous light, lofty and distant, illumines the pure sound.

**Immortal Qiu Asks of the Heavenly and Human Merging in Emergence**
Heaven and human merge in emergence, establishing its mechanism,
amidst ten thousand transformations, settling the most subtle.
Left and right, meeting the source, the bright mirror is revealed,
filling the sky with dazzling, pristine radiance.

**Immortal Dong Asks of the Root of All Things’ Nature**
The root of all things’ nature arises from above—
the teeming myriad things return to the root,
flowers bloom and flourish, abiding in the highest.
Reverting to destiny, knowing the ancient stem,
nurturing the spirit, knocking at the Dao, one enters the Mystery Gate.

**Immortal Liao Addresses the Assembly Without Asking a Question**
Why does Immortal Liao not seek a question?
Vastly penetrating the mysterious vision, skillfully searching the mechanism.
Preserving the Three in silent speech, the true awakening is clear,
guarding the One, forgetting words, cutting off perception and knowledge.

**Gifting to Elder Ru and Elder Liu: Discourse on the Tathāgata’s Awakened Nature**
Skillfully penetrating the heavenly eye, awakening to the Tathāgata,
suddenly beholding the numinous sound, the sun of wisdom unfolds.
From the Anavatapta Pool, five leaves arise,
the Blue Lad moves them into the fire to be planted.

**Immortal Zhao Asks of the Valley Spirit Not Dying**
The valley spirit does not die, establishing the heavenly root,
the mysterious female endures eternally through ancient ages.
The northern sea, dark and vast, swells with earth’s vigor,
the southern ocean, blazing bright, descends with heaven’s soul.

**Master Zhao Asks of the Primordial Spirit in the Empty Valley**
The supreme empty valley, still and without dust,
ten thousand streams of yang light strike the eye anew.
Benefiting beings, one source reveals the awakened nature,
skillfully giving rise to the three essentials, suddenly the primordial spirit.

**Immortal Wang Asks of Yin Nature and Yang Spirit**
Yin and yang return and reverse, settling at the center,
within and without, interconnected, virtue and power endure.
Closing the eyes, quietly contemplating the bedrock tiger’s nature,
opening the eyes, the light of the jade dragon shines forth.

**Lord Zhao Asks of the Highest Good Being Like Water**
Ten thousand droplets of numinous waves pierce the cosmos,
a thousand abysses of divine water irrigate heaven and earth.
Stirring the mixed source once gives birth to heaven and earth,
watering the yellow sprout, the stem and root grow long.

**Immortal Li Asks of Returning the Primordial Qi to Heaven**
The nine-five soul flies straight upward,
returning the primordial qi to the heavenly gate.
The Cavern Mystery’s numinous treasure forms the body,
the great transformation’s empty sovereign is the first honored one.

**Master Qiu Asks of the Dao-Eye**
The Dao-eye clearly knows the ultimate true origin,
responding to the mechanism, transforming, skillfully penetrating the divine.
Opening heaven and dividing earth, returning to the primordial beginning,
the upright vision, majestic and wondrous, is the Dharma-body.

**Fellow Official Li Asks of the Supreme Clarity’s Dao**
The Supreme Clarity’s primordial head is the Dao’s honored one,
heaven’s mandate governs the spirits, the ten thousand transformations abide.
The hundred sources of things’ benefit surge through the Kan gate,
the mixed completion of one qi leaps through the Li gate.

**Master Jiao Asks of Non-Obstruction**
The numinous brightness penetrates transformation beyond the body,
unfettered and solitary, utterly free of dust.
If the heart congeals like a pearl, unstained and unpolluted,
what thing could obstruct the true?

**Elder Xiang the Immortal Asks of the Dao’s Harmony with Its Principle**
The Great Mystery merges in emergence, settling its mechanism,
firmly rooted, preserving the true, the will does not waver.
The medicine perfected, one returns to youth, the bones purified,
the elixir completed, one reverts to age, forever without decline.

**Layman Liu Asks of Diligence**
In the six periods, diligently reciting Amitābha,
compassion and kindness boundless, bestowing benefit upon others.
Two converging pure winds gather the earth’s paths,
one wheel of bright moonlight ascends the heavenly river.

**Elder Liu Asks of the Prajñā Boat**
In the Prajñā boat, not a single thing remains,
the moon bright, it sails empty from the dim thoroughfare.
Beneath the twin śāla trees, the heart’s treasure unfolds,
in the Deer Park, the pearl of nature is awakened.

**Elder Xiang the Immortal Asks of the Great Mystery**
The Great Mystery’s true awakening transcends worldly emotions,
a single dewdrop congeals into a pearl, illuminating the sea’s clarity.
The dragon leaps, waves surge, lighting up the cosmos,
shooting open the heavenly tripod, vast and bright.

**Immortal Liu Asks of the Elixir Medicine**
One gourd of immortal medicine, one pot of elixir,
sold in the mortal realm, entering the marketplace.
Several times not encountering a true resolute knight,
it is taken back to the Jade Heaven.

**Immortal Liu the Second Asks of the Empty Vastness**
The numinous source, empty and vast, utterly without remainder,
revealing the heavenly crystal, illuminating the eye’s pearl.
Since the primordial beginning, it has been called the ancestral Dao,
to this day, thereby is the true suchness invoked.

**Gifting to Lords Zhang and Li: The Iron Crucible**
The moth-eaten key fans the blazing fire’s light,
within the crucible, flickering, the true yang gathers.
The steel hammer forges the flying spirit-sword,
its double-edged blue blade gleams in the great azure.

**Master Liu Asks of the Yin-Yang Reversal Method**
Yin and yang return and reverse, giving rise to the Qian position,
dragon and tiger mutually devour, entering the Dui direction.
Two jade lads support the precious mirror,
brilliantly the light shines into the crystal hall.

**Master Luo Asks of the Great Dao Nurturing the Spirit**
Heaven and earth’s harmonious balance nurtures the utmost essence,
the mixed completion of one qi, the valley spirit’s numinosity.
Releasing the vast moon to its thousand-fathom depth,
the fetal light leaps forth, bright for ten thousand miles.

**Master Chang Asks of Guest and Host**
The utmost Dao’s essence, vast and pure, cannot be established,
its movement the great image of heaven’s empty sun.
The settled light eternally anchors the middle origin,
refining the yang spirit, the work may be completed.

**Zhang Mouke Asks of the Six Caverns’ Flying Mystery Qi**
The Dao practices the three essentials, the natural mechanism,
the spirit moves the essence’s brilliance, the qi’s image follows.
Virtue’s transformation, the still light, the toad’s vigor leaps,
the Dao’s nurturance, the clear freshness, the sun’s soul flies.

**Master Zhang Asks of the Ten Thousand Transformations Settling the Mechanism**
The ten thousand transformations’ numinous pivot, self and others follow,
the majestic light compliantly transforms, responding to its mechanism.
Heaven and human mutually give rise to the positions of generation and completion,
embracing the pure wind, forever without delusion.

**Young Master Liu Asks of the Yang Spirit**
The primordial essence, once stirred, envelops the heavenly heart,
blazing bright, congealing auspiciousness, concealing illusory yin.
Wholly like a shooting star soaring through the ancient moon,
as if jade were moving amidst flying gold.

**Marshal Ma Asks of Fleeing the False and Returning to the True—Where Does the True Go?**
The mortal fetus and turbid bones are not the true body,
the jade countenance and pure flesh are the Dharma-body.
Entering and exiting the Yi Gate, the wind is companion,
in the cloud hall, reclining high, the moon is neighbor.

**Immortal Zhang Asks of the Exquisite Mechanism**
Wishing to transmit the profound mystery’s exquisite mechanism,
I fear you would not believe, turning to doubt.
One day leaping free from the net of worldly toil,
I will tap your ear and earnestly explain the subtle.

**Immortal Li Asks of Sitting Alone on the Lotus Throne**
Sitting alone on the lotus throne, guarding the natural,
gazing at the jeweled pool, the moon’s brilliance is fresh.
Several times I have personally been to the toad palace,
daring to face the eternal maiden and speak of the wondrous mystery.

**Marshal Kang Asks of the Great Mystery**
The Great Mystery’s true awakening transcends worldly busyness,
girding the sword, carrying the staff, entering the great square.
Wild cranes and solitary clouds are companions,
forest springs and wind-moon are homeland.

**Master Wang Asks of First Attaining the Wondrous Sound**
Illuminating it is called attaining the wondrous sound,
unfolding the clear eye, cutting off depravity.
One numinous true nature penetrates the primordial image,
responding and employing, moving with the ancient and modern.

**Master Liu Asks of the Heavenly Oneness Without Division**
The supreme emptiness transforms, blending without division,
gathering and absorbing the yang light, achieving the Dharma-body.

**Perpetual Union with the Dao’s Mechanism Has No Separate Form**
The transformation into immortal bones makes one naturally human.

**Marshal Chen Asks of the True Wind and Flowers**
The true wind blows open emerald mists and rosy clouds,
scattering jeweled blossoms across the Sun Palace and Moon Palace.
One crucible refines the essence of heaven and earth,
two cauldrons gather the luminous sands of night.

**Practitioner Yin Asks of the Source**
The awakened sea’s numinous source is the ancient Buddha-hall,
where the golden gate opens and closes with perfect ease.
On the bodhi path, the pure heart gleams,
in the prajñā pool, the radiance of nature shines.

**Abbot Master Liu Asks of the Gourd-Heaven**
One gourd, refined and radiant—one gourd-heaven,
within the indistinct and subtle, the wondrous mystery is attained.
Illusory dreams are suddenly cast off, soaring through the cosmos,
worldly attachments severed, transformed into cloud immortals.

**Old Immortal Niu Asks of Heart-Incense**
A wisp of pure incense rises from the jade gourd,
forming a floral canopy that ascends into the crimson dawn.
The moon’s sacred script is simmered without escape,
the sun’s golden essence is refined without withering.

**Immortal Niu Asks of the Turning Mechanism**
The celestial wheel turns, flipping the mare of the north,
the earth’s gate is pushed open, setting the ox of the west in motion.
The Scarlet Child of the Li Palace seizes the stars and moon,
the Azure Lad of the Kan Palace captures the sun’s head.

**Old Immortal Niu Asks if Two Words Can Comprehend All Dharmas**
Ever since the eyebrows and lashes were plucked into awareness,
the gates of the ten thousand dharmas have opened, all gathered in.
Samādhi and prajñā, perfectly luminous, fill the vast emptiness,
the numinous light illumines all kalpas like grains of sand.

**Immortal Zhao the Second Asks of the Treasure Within the Body**
Carving open the thorny valley reveals the heart of heaven,
unveiling the flawless seven-jeweled forest.
Amidst the tortoiseshell groves, the fine jade is observed,
within the lapis piles, the refined gold is seen.

**Old Immortal Zhang Asks of Seeing and Hearing**
The ears are cleansed to hear the jade chime’s strike,
the eyes are purified to see the golden bell’s toll.
The reclusive one, wishing to grasp the Chan adept’s intent,
laughs and points to the ancient pine in the courtyard.

**Daoist Leader Niu Asks of the Wish-Fulfilling Jewel**
The wish-fulfilling mechanism gathers like a treasure vase,
coral and agate foundations gleam with radiant blossoms.
Within the eight-hued lapis channels, it is present,
each luminous pearl ascending in reverse.

**Old Immortal Tian Asks of Self and Other**
The Gate of the Great One opens, without self or other,
the cool breeze extinguishes the fire that burns the body.
Ignorance transforms into the purple mystery’s frost,
becoming the divine cinnabar—a single elixir pellet.

**Immortal Tan Asks What Is the Treasure**
At the moment the numinous treasure of the Cavernous Mystery stirs the brows,
the wondrous countenance of the Tathāgata appears in the blink of an eye.
The red phoenix’s wings return to the valley of metal and water,
the green luan soars to the Jade Capital Mountain.

**Old Immortal Liu Asks of the Heart-Moon**
Brushing aside the clouds and haze reveals the heart of heaven,
releasing the autumn toad ten thousand leagues wide.
Filling the vast emptiness with a thousand pieces of jade,
overflowing the Dao-eye with two coins of gold.

**Immortal Wang the Second Asks of Penetrating the Origin**
Penetrating the origin’s wondrous awakening leaves nothing behind,
suddenly the numinous sound illuminates the eye’s pupil.
Throughout the body, crimson mists swirl and rise,
the entire being presses forth, releasing a serene light.

**Great Immortal Tian Asks of the Double Pass**
In the Sun Palace, the dragon coils around the golden tripod, still,
in the Moon Palace, the tiger prowls by the jade furnace, cold.
A pair of jade maidens ride the cinnabar phoenix,
two lads drive the multicolored luan.

**Immortal Gao Asks of the Primordial Suspended Pearl**
The Primordial suspends the millet-grain pearl in emptiness,
the assembled immortals rejoice in their tranquil abode.
It encompasses heaven and earth with abundance to spare,
embracing the cosmos with more than enough to contain.

**Immortal Wei Asks of Inner and Outer—Neither Clinging to Emptiness nor Seeing**
Intermingling inner and outer, originally without form,
the pure essence merges, harmonizing with profit and integrity.
Not clinging to being or non-being—what is the self?
The azure sky’s stars gleam, illuminating the world.

**Immortal Zhang of Huayin Asks of Lead and Mercury**
Lead and mercury are gathered and concealed within fire,
refined into a single cauldron of purple golden frost.
Round and round, they coalesce into the image of the divine elixir,
brilliant and flowing, they radiate with the sun’s light.

**[Answers to Questions]**
**Old Immortal Meng Asks:**
*If one recognizes the numinous, numinous thing,*
*ten hundred origins are but one thousand.*
The Primordial awakens to the numinous, numinous thing,
the Perfect Sage penetrates the mystery’s essence in the indistinct.
Only through skillful reckoning is the great thousand known,
not apart from the divine pattern—luminous and empty valley.

**Marshal Huo Asks of Manifesting Nature in Emptiness**
The great sound is without thing—all things are empty,
leaping forth, the mysterious pearl is one with the primordial.
The spirit enters the emerald mist to seize the bright moon,
the nature roams the misty waves to grasp the clear wind.

**Immortal Feng Asks of Dwelling at Home While Transcending the Worldly**
With purity, integrity, and chastity, one dwells at home,
wielding the numinous light to emerge from the illusory body.
The sea’s dragons and serpents swallow the sun and moon,
the mountain’s rhinoceros and tigers play with luminous pearls.

**Immortal Wang Asks of Leaving Home**
Wealth, honor, and fame—swept away with a single sword,
worldly attachments discarded like mud.
The leviathan and roc emerge from the sea, wings brushing the sky,
the phoenix departs the nest, soaring toward the sun.

**Immortal Liu Asks of the Dharma-Body’s Eternal Youth While the Physical Body Ages**
Only by relying on the wondrous body is the illusory form known,
like a thatched hut dwelling in emptiness.
Two casements—bright moon, radiant yang essence,
one door—pure wind, surging vital breath.

**In Memory of Wang the Fourth’s Deceased Mother—Cease Your Tears**
Do not say deep affection binds distant emotions,
in the end, all is but an empty name.
Only by gathering the gaze does the clear eye gleam,
only by restraining tears is the Dao-eye’s brightness known.

**Young Immortal Zhang Asks of Spiritual Transformation**
Graceful and ethereal, the divine wind emerges from the cavern-heaven,
jade cliffs stretch across the azure, sweeping away the empty mist.
Piercing the mystery, responding to images—all is truly luminous,
the essence of the supreme Dao is vast, a single thing resplendent.

**Dharma Master Shan Requests a Four-Character Poem on "Cease"**
**Cease**
Let thoughts follow clouds and water, cease the pursuit of fame,
relying on the sword, roam freely through the world.
Upon encountering mountain peaks, seize the rhinoceros and tiger,
at every sea’s depths, slay the dragons and serpents.

**Gather**
The sun and moon are gathered within the round cauldron,
wisdom advances, fiery condensation flows like molten flame.
The Azure Lad stokes the flames, riding the mare of the north,
the Scarlet Child parts the mist, straddling the ox of the west.

**Worry**
With perfect communion in the numinous awakening, there is no worry,
the boundless yang light pervades all directions.
The phoenix blazes, the sun-wheel returns to the sea’s peaks,
the dragon stretches, the moon’s horns emerge from the mountain’s head.

**Cultivate**
Gradually entering the mystery’s gate, cultivation is attained,
pointing open the heavenly eye, the azure pupil is awakened.
The mighty spirit tears off the black dragon’s tail,
the vast benevolence overturns the white tiger’s head.

**A Quatrain Taking All Four Characters**
Worldly burdens and dusty passions—desire ceases,
the celestial treasure overflows, gathered in the Cavernous Mystery.
Within the furnace, the great medicine—worry it may not form,
within the tripod, the golden elixir—joy in its cultivation.

**Abbot Master Liu Asks of the Great Mystery**
The Great Mystery’s true awakening emerges from the dust of ignorance,
the wisdom-sun’s auspicious light renews the gaze.
The Buddhist disciple, awakening to it, illuminates the nature of awareness,
the Daoist, knowing this, suddenly attains the primordial spirit.

**Immortal Liang the Second Asks of Blending with the World While Radiating Light**

Though dwelling in the dust, the will remains unyielding,
with resolute purity, the true constant is preserved.
In leisure, subtly one perceives the vastness of heaven and earth,
in stillness, clearly one knows the length of sun and moon.

**Immortal An Asks of the Use of Emptiness and Nothingness**
Emptiness and nothingness bear no form, beyond all knowing,
profound silence forgets the body, reaching the farthest depths.
The dragon’s tail coils around the eye of heaven and sea,
from the turtle’s head flies forth the heart of the winding river.

**Immortal Cui Asks of the Original Face**
The wisdom-sun overflows, aiding beings without limit,
beings devoid of selfhood—suddenly all is pure and void.
A torrent of yang fire blazes through the heavens,
the chaos-piercing pair illumines the sea’s pearl.

**Minister Duan Inquires of the Purple Court and Yellow Court**
The spirit roams the Purple Court—what doubt remains?
The nature enters the Yellow Court, naturally fitting the mechanism.
One golden elixir shines bright and clear,
two immortal pellets gleam radiant and luminous.

**Immortal Yan Asks of the Singular Body’s Perfect Clarity**
Split open, the numinous awareness illuminates perfect penetration,
the dust of toil is shattered—all things become empty.
Great awakening to the Mystery’s gate knows no inside or out,
the perfectly realized supreme Dao stands alone as the宗.

*Upper Clarity’s Great Mystery Collection, Scroll Eight—Concluded*
*Upper Clarity’s Great Mystery Collection, Scroll Nine*

**Lyrics by Marquis Guye Shanyuan: "Su Zhongqing" (Ten Poems)**

**I**
The golden empire of the Central Court shines bright,
blessed with pure peace and harmony.
The celestial cycle turns to *jiazi*—
now is the time for cultivation.
Return to truth in stillness,
embody purity in clarity.
Qi and spirit, numinous and divine.
The Mystery’s gate unfolds transformation,
the true wind of the Most High,
drawing all beings upward.

**II**
Jade crucible, golden tripod—tiger and dragon coil,
crimson flames fill the heavens.
Water and fire, warm and cool, arise naturally,
day and night the alchemy turns.
Essence thick as mist,
qi flowing endlessly.
Nurturing the immortal embryo.
When merit is complete, one ascends,
borne by jeweled chariots and fragrant carriages,
up to the Jade Heaven.

**III**
In the depths of the River of Love, best to withdraw,
for fame and profit strike like sorrow’s blows.
Turn your head—gone to roam the river,
mist-locked, a lone boat.
A tune on the qin,
three cups of wine.
Delighting in seclusion.
Wind as neighbor, moon as companion,
drunk beneath the jade grove,
dreaming of entering Penglai.

**IV**
At first light, the river moon pierces the twin groves,
veiled in the deep, pale waves.
Wind still, serene, and crystalline,
in the clear night—true knowing.
White wine,
poured naturally.
Singing in time.
No entanglements, no blows,
the heart opens wide,
floating or sinking—let it be.

**V**
Carefree, unbound, joy in leisure,
strolling where fate leads.
If asked where I return,
I point afar to the winding riverbank.
Willow-lined shore,
half-shrouded in mist.
A sky newly clear.
The night hushed and pure,
no one about,
moonlight filling the empty boat.

**VI**
A sky of pure beauty, a stream of clouds,
wind and moon as near neighbors.
Qin, sword, wine, chess, calligraphy, painting—
as they come, delight in nature’s truth.
Bamboo fence gleams,
the thatched hall renewed.
Still, without dust.
Morning mushrooms unseen,
all around jade blossoms,
separated by the divine *chun* tree.

**VII**
How many through the ages have chased fame and gain,
discarding life to vie for merit?
Where have all the heroes gone?
All have sunk into emptiness.
Better than they—
I, in Dongting’s midst,
send my servant forth.
Lightly skimming the golden goblet,
drunk beneath the eaves,
one pillow of pure wind.

**VIII**
Beings of meager fortune delight in the *shravaka*,
diligently upholding merit.
Fasting, seated meditation, rites, and chanting—
all end in stubborn emptiness.
The true mark,
within being and nonbeing.
A fine family tradition.
Ancestor of the Mystery’s origin,
the gate of the Great Beginning opens,
embodying perfect clarity.

**IX**
Lord Ying, pure and aloof from worldly ties,
unshaken by fame and profit’s pull.
Carefree, dwelling wherever clouds and water lead,
knowing fate, delighting in nature.
Mastering the profound,
awakening to the subtle.
Diligently cultivating immortality.
When merit is complete, return,
leading you to audience at the Origin,
steadily treading the golden lotus.

**X**
The divine immortals’ wondrous art has been passed down,
but who grasps this subtle mystery?
Tortoise and snake breathe naturally,
the Mysterious Female’s qi flows endlessly.
Lead within mercury,
mercury within lead—
both complete.
Withdrawing and adding, increasing and decreasing,
advancing the fire’s work,
refining the immortal embryo.

---

**Ten Poems: "Magnolia Flower"**

**I**
The heartless sea of suffering,
where dust-choked beings drown in craving.
How unlike my home—
the silent grove and spring, apart from worldly splendor.

**II**
Nurturing truth, fostering vastness,
flesh and bone as ice-clear as jade.
Entering and exiting without gap,
graceful, drifting with the wind to ascend the heavens.

**III**
Deep roots, firm stem,
heavenly treasure, flowing rosy clouds—light fills the ford.
Reflected radiance stretches to the sky,
gently, step by step—profound, ever profound.
No birth, no death,
serene, solitary, bright and pure.
Dawn scatters the sparse clouds,
piercing the clear void to reach the ninth heaven.

**IV**
Autumn wind vast,
gazing afar—rosy clouds gleam, auspicious and bright.
Across the shore, reed blossoms,
veiled in mist, two or three homes.

**V**
Heavenly truth, lush and flourishing,
exiled to the world—light fills the chamber.
Preserving and protecting a thousand springs,
crimson-crested, green pine—longevity shared.

**VI**
At first devotion to the Dao,
strictly guarding essence, light returns in reflection.
The Primordial aids truth,
true things arise in the midst of vagueness.
Congealing in the empty vast,
bright moon and clear wind lean upon each other.
Attaining that carefree state,
turning back to wander beyond the mist and clouds.

**VII**
Five phases, four images,
*wu* and *ji* amassed—what form do they take?
Black water, red clouds,
white horse, green ox—divided in two.
Golden chariot, jeweled carriage,
the great Dao level, refining the jade thread.
The path like silver,
bearing the infant beyond the world’s dust.

**VIII**
Fame and wealth,
leading to sinking and drowning—empty-handed departure.
Turn your face, return—
one loss of human form, eternal kalpas of ruin.
Return to purity, revert to simplicity,
turning from the world, cleansing dust—true awakening.
One orb of radiant light,
shining brilliantly into the great square.

**IX**
If not awakened in this life,
where to turn in the next?
The six paths intersect,
one misstep—eternal peril.
If you see through it,
cast aside all in this dusty world.
Clouds and water, carefree,
steadily drifting the empty boat beyond things.

**X**
Floating life’s sorrows,
the dusty world’s busyness—when will it end?
One day, impermanence comes,
fortune passes to others, karma is your own.
If you awaken,
abandon foes and kin to seek the way out.
All things cease—
search carefully within life and destiny.
Staying home to study the Dao,
two matters unachieved—delayed and hindered.
If you wish to cultivate truth,
do not cling to the slightest speck of worldly dust.
Empty the heart, fill the belly—
this alone is the true path to ascending immortality.
When merit is complete, audience at the Origin,
the golden palace’s dawn transforms you into a feathered immortal.

---

**Ten Poems: "Longing for Immortality"**

**I**
Those who leave home
seek truth.
Through all calculations, the vast sky is without a speck of dust.
Knowing the empty valley’s spirit.

**II**
The sun as neighbor,
the moon as kin.
Within heaven and earth, the Dharma-body turns.
Only then do you know the person beyond things.

**III**
Silent and still,
serene and clear.
Day and night, the three lights—nature fills itself.
In every thing, clarity.

**IV**
The Dao has no form,
nurturing the numinous spirit.
Piercing the sea, penetrating mountains—merged in the profound.
The true person’s path of emergence.

**V**
Roaming freely,
delighting in the clear autumn.
Veiled, Cao Creek’s gentle waters flow.
Jade blossoms on both banks.

**VI**
Floating bubbles,
drinking, forgetting sorrow.

**X. "South Branch Melody" (Ten Poems)**

**I**
Sun sets, stars sparse, moon ascends the tower.
Deep in drunken jade isles.
Behold the pure sound, witness rise and fall.
Dharma-eye and star-gaze span ancient and modern.
Crimson wheels encroach between the two.

**II**
Forests of fire-pearls, water’s true gold.
No need to seek afar in other realms.
Inherit and recognize the original heart.
Tiger and dragon harmonize, Kan and Li unite.
Divine water trickles into the jade ladle.
Cloud-waves and snow-surges drift.

**III**
Treasure-pool’s irrigation,
nurturing the numinous sprout.
First blooms the jade plum, tender jade sways.
Fragrance beyond things wafts.

**IV**
The Dao is boundless,
nature’s light is perfect.
Recognize the tortoise and serpent entwined below.
Yin and yang unite heaven and earth.
Mercury and lead, qi and spirit complete.
Radiance streams forth, rosy clouds dazzling bright.
Only then do you know the profound within the profound.

**V**
Do not exert effort,
lest the spirit weary.
In clarity and stillness, recognize the original truth.
Harmonizing light, unstained by dust.
Cast the self aside,
become the natural person.
Leisurely roam heaven’s edge, play with the solar wheel.
Cloud-wander through jade grottoes in spring.

**VI**
Gather frost of the profound,
steep jade nectar.
Two substances blend, swallowed in fire.
After refining, the tripod brims with fragrance.
Flavor extraordinary,
hue clear and luminous.
After swallowing, pure coolness permeates the body.
Intoxicated, the Jade Emperor appears.

**VII**
As a human being,
do not follow blindly.
How many decades of light remain?
In vain, you tarnish yourself with worldly dust.
Diligently cultivate the true,
nurture the original spirit.
The two luminaries’ light grinds the jade wheel.
A single drop of yin essence, pure.

**VIII**
Guard essence closely,
brimming full.
Silently seal the golden pass, ascend in reverse.
Pearls of the profound pour forth.
Within, numinous;
without, bright.
Inner and outer merge—one point of light.
Soaring upward to the jade radiance.

**IX**
Refine the body, the monkey-mind retreats,
burn the true, the horse of intent grows sparse.
One numinous, perfect awakening—suddenly true thusness.
Penetrating profound mystery,
light mirrors the primordial beginning.
Kan’s tiger, jade-like in form;
Li’s dragon, pearl-like in hue.
Clouds surge, lightning flashes—piercing the void.
Thunderous and towering,
playfully brandishing the profound pearl.

**X**
The great Dao, though near, feels distant;
profound mechanism, though receding, not yet sparse.
The vast emptiness congeals in elegance, naturally thus.
One stream of numinous source,
lustrous from the very beginning.
Northern sea’s simurgh bathed in black,
Southern mountain’s phoenix dyed in crimson.
Soaring beyond clouds, emerging from the void.
Sun and moon exchange light,
seizing the night-shining pearl.

**XI**
Matching the principle of yin and yang,
the infant lord accompanies the slender waist.
Harmonizing lead and mercury, requiring the whole day.
Gold essence from the water’s depths,
transferred into fire to burn.
Refine into a sword that communicates with spirits,
forge into a blade of wisdom.
Subduing dragons and tigers, slaying demons and fiends.
At night, it emits radiance—
who dares raise their voice?

**XII**
Phoenix flies far, yet returns;
crane follows wings to the marsh.
Within stone, jade is concealed; clams hold pearls.
Wood grows sunken *ding*,
grasses flourish with purple lingzhi sprouts.
Beasts transform into lions and scaled elephants,
serpents bathe and become sea-dragons.
Fish divide in water-valleys, changing into whales and giant turtles.
The human Dao connects—
cloud-steps ascend the cinnabar heavens.

Rain passes, spring nears its end;
wind arrives, autumn comes too soon.
A hundred years of light and shadow—gone in a turn of the head.
Wealth and honor, glory and splendor,
all like bubbles on water.

I urge you to cultivate yourself early,
search the depths of the Mystery Gate’s intent.
Let not worldly affairs strike your heart.
Guard the secret breath of the Three Fields,
lest thieves steal it away.

**XIII**
The Supreme Mysterious Origin Ancestor,
born before the vast kalpas began.
First transmitted the Five Thousand Words of the Dao,
expounding the orthodox without doubt—
who comprehends this profound mystery?
All consume the drug of delusion,
but who feasts on the elixir of life extension?
Crooked teachings of heterodox paths entangle the self.
Death casts one into the prison of darkness,
eternally bound in the Yellow Springs.

**XIV**
Trample the net of worldly toil,
resolute and steadfast in soaring ambition.
Sword in hand, eyes whirling like rings.
Sunlight vies in brilliance,
flashing and dazzling, illuminating the heavens.
The depths of the sea of awakening,
spirit-waves surging for ten thousand miles.
Demons disperse in terror, gods tremble.
Transforming into pure yang,
forever dwelling in Penglai and Yingzhou.

**XV**
If you ask of the principles of cultivating truth,
do you yet comprehend?
The whale and roc emerge from the sea, piercing the starry canopy.
At night, they lodge in the Moon Palace,
soaring to the branches of the osmanthus tree.
Auspicious and virtuous spirit-birds are few,
ominous and perverse monstrous birds abound.
In flocks and herds, they idly wander.
Thorns become their nests—
where is the phoenix’s abode to be seen?

**XVI**
Sitting, I behold the scenes of Huaxu,
my spirit roams, playing in the treasure realm.
A pair of youths cradle dragon-light,
radiant and resplendent,
gathering it into the center.
A spirit-immortal child is born,
and upon achieving merit, enters the imperial realm.
On the Jade Empyrean’s register, one’s name appears for the celestial examination.
Seizing the immortal’s banner,
holding the jade tablet, one enters the treasure cave.

**XVII**
Unknowing of the treasure within the body,
how can one understand the chapters beyond the material world?
Without the true teaching, one raves in madness.
Gazing toward Penglai,
lying supine, groping for the blue heavens.
To recognize mercury within lead,
one must know lead within mercury.
These two, inverted, become naturally harmonious.
Releasing the spirit in flight,
the embryonic immortal dances beyond the void.

**Three *Xianxiangzi***

Hark! This ugly frame,
reeking, filled with maggots.
Earth, water, fire, wind—hollowly amassed,
buried deep.
Like me, they invite calamity all my life.
To escape the催 of life and death,
cling not to the mortal body as the sacred embryo.
Preserve and refine the numinous ointment until it congeals,
forming the embryo.
Bathe the infant, seated on the treasure dais.

In the ancient courtyard of carefree melody,
alone I sit, composed, contemplating the Daoist scriptures.
The mysterious mirror washes away the clutter of worldly affairs,
bringing peace.
With one cleansing, the machinations of the heart awaken—ears and eyes grow clear.

Serene and tranquil, cool and pure,
a stick of incense fills the courtyard with fragrance.
Beyond the gate, I know not who has arrived—
the jingle of jade pendants,
a gentle breeze carries the faint sound of jade ornaments.

Alone I sit, contemplating the *Huangting*,
beginning to perceive the brightness within and without.
Luminous and still, untroubled by worldly vexations,
the heart grows clear.
Nurturing the spirit-source to its deepest purity.

Lightly steeping snowflake tea,
the universe floats in auspicious qi.
Clouds part, the frosty sky reveals the bright moon—
welcoming me.
A grain of spirit-cinnabar ascends in reverse.

**Ten *Yiye Zhou***

Shaking off worldly passions and karmic debts,
here lies the end of profit and fame.
In purity and solemn dignity,
feast in the Jade Pool.
Waters still and limpid as ice,
revealing the autumn moon in the emerald pond.
Within the moon, awakening to the cinnabar branch—
the radiance of innate nature shines.

Unaware the body ages and withers,
enduring countless entanglements.
Who would cease before death,
mired in bitter craving?
Seeing through early, cultivate diligently,
recognize your own treasure.
A treasure beyond price,
eternally preserved.

The Dao harmonizes with the subtle and indistinct,
discerning that within lies something.
Each thing naturally flows,
all is encompassed.
Moonlit and wind-clear, filling the eyes,
precious talismans exquisitely fragrant.
Vast and empty, pervading the realm of essence—
within the realm of being and non-being.

Donning a bamboo hat, clad in straw,
gradually entering the depths of reed flowers.
By the green shore, mooring the fishing boat,
reeling in the line.
Lightly brewing the single flavor within the gourd,
wild cranes and solitary clouds in harmony.
The horizontal flute’s melody, pure and secluded,
joy without sorrow.

The Great Dao is originally without a single thing,
yet embraces the ten directions, empty and full.
No beyond, nor heart—
not even a needle’s space.
To see clearly, open the eyes of purity,
recognize the original void of the valley.
Neither shallow nor deep,
the golden elixir fills the crucible.

The Great Dao stands alone and independent,
skillfully employing the original traces.
Roaming the vast seas,
delighting in the clear autumn.
Moonlight supports the empty sky, auspicious and clear,
faintly revealing the red osmanthus and light verdure.
A splendid scene most wondrous and secluded,
rivaling Penglai Isle.

Moving the first yang as it emerges,
illuminating the subtle mysteries of the great void.
All phenomena vanish in concealment,
brilliantly radiant.
Congealing the numinous essence within the crucible,
the elixir is perfected in an instant.
The immortal ascends on cloudy blossoms,
playing in Penglai’s paradise.

Pearls congeal at the ocean’s depths, fresh and pure,
in the heavens, flawlessly clear.
At the center, the Great Void is vast—
the divine elixir rolls forth.
Outshining the autumn moon’s full wheel,
illuminating the original absence of wax and wane.
Cool and refreshing, chilling to the touch,
piercing the luminous jade.

The sea’s light congeals into a gleaming pearl,
noble or base—no distinction, like slingshots at sparrows.
What a pity, the original treasure,
soiled in the mire of the ford.
Recognize it, lest error arise,
polishing the bright and pure, free from entanglements.
Emerging from the clamor of dust,
delighting in eternal spring.

The first yang arises in inversion,
myriad transformations merge as one with the primordial.
Light dazzles, shooting toward the Jade Palace—
the hall is filled with crimson.
Clarity and roundness open in awakening,
above and below, penetrating without end.
Heaven and earth are utterly empty—
within the Great Mystery.

**Ten *Leijiang Yue***

Chasing wealth and lust, entangled in profit and fame,
when will the ceaseless strife end?
Day after day, frantically lost in dreams,
the heart’s monkey and horse run wild.
Deceiving earth and heaven, boasting many skills,
turning cleverness into folly.
All is vanity,
accumulating lifetimes of karmic debt.

I urge you to awaken and turn back,
abandon attachments, become a carefree wanderer.
Seek the Dao, pursue truth, find the wondrous finger—
early vow to transcend birth and death.
Failing to grasp the mystery,
clearing the ear’s obstructions,
receive the direct transmission.
The scene of the gourd-heaven appears—
the bright autumn moon before you.

Subtle and refined, the essence of the primordial,
a single point of deep red, flawlessly pure.
Above and below harmonize, opening the eye of wisdom—
leaping forth, the heart-pearl congeals.
Manifesting numinous clarity,
the spirit’s light shines,
inner and outer fully connected.
Floating clouds disperse,
revealing the moon of the heart beyond the heavens.

Empty and formless, turning in solitude,
round and bright, silently illuminating—
through the ages, without the slightest flaw.
With the Dao, originally one, embracing all phenomena,
each thing, each head, all is gathered.
Pervading all directions,
boundless and primal,
merged as one, without distinction.
Sages and worthies of ancient and present,
all find rest here.

The primordial Dao-body,
vast and boundless,
without corners, form, or thing.
Moist transformations and womb births all receive qi,
resonating through the mysterious and hidden.
Encompassing heaven and earth,
containing the cosmos,
sun and moon all embraced.
Returning the light, reflecting inward,
vastly capturing the transformations before the eyes.

Clearly perceiving the heart-pearl,
empty and luminous,
brilliantly opening the valley of spirit.
Nurturing the fetal immortal, skin like snow,
entering and exiting with the wind’s fragrance.
At dusk, inhaling the magic mushroom,
at dawn, feasting on the osmanthus,
at night, lodging in the Moon Palace.
Joyful and content,
seeking the true blessings of the ancient sages.

The Yangtze flows, serene and still,
night whispers, the sky like a jade table, ice-pure.
Lush colors, misty and vast,
the gaze encompasses the radiant jade’s glow.
Sitting alone, nurturing the spirit,
the curtain’s light shines through,
revealing exquisite snow.
Still and limpid,
a single point connects the Great Void.

The spirit soars on two wings,
resting in the Moon Palace’s halls,
lodging for the night on jade branches.
Encountering the true sign, without gain or loss,
forever guided by the perfected.
Achieving both merit and practice,
golden lads and jade decrees,
receiving the mandate at the Liao Yang Gate.
Within the Jade Dawn Palace,
eternally arrayed in immortal ranks.

A thatched hut, carefree and secluded,
still and dustless,
sitting alone behind lowered curtains.
Day after day, leisurely and tranquil,
possessing a serene livelihood.
Grasping firmly to preserve the true,
the heart free from杂念,
forgetting self and world.
The jade infant transforms,
naturally harmonizing with the Dao.

Light illuminates the ten directions,
congealing in the void, resplendent—
greatly manifesting, not a trifling matter.
Embracing the boundless, connecting with creation,
each thing, each head, all is aided.
Holding heaven and earth,
perfecting the Dharma-body,
jade countenance, truly pure and beautiful.
Transcending the mundane, leaving the world,
ascending to pay homage to the Three Clarities’ divine emperors.

Floating life like a dream,
alas, a hundred years of time—
how much can one truly grasp?
Wealth and honor, glory and splendor, fleeting,
why cling so tightly?
All for children and grandchildren,
a beloved wife and son-in-law—
who can replace you in life and death?
Turning back to reflect,
in an instant, free from the dust’s shadow.

Carefree beyond the world, unrestrained,
wind as neighbor, moon as companion—
this is the plan for the remainder of life.
By the rock, by the stream, monkeys offer fruit,
wine fills the ten directions, verses composed.
Drunk amidst mist and rosy clouds,
awakening this night—
where shall the heart return?
Within the Jade Dawn Palace,
plucking the osmanthus in the moon.

Once more—
the sky emerald-clear,
primordial yang harmonious and subtly dense,
emptiness vast, nothing abiding.
Attaining stillness, the heart’s aperture opens upward,
communing with the numinous radiance of the hollow valley.
Nurturing the original spirit,
the Perfected One appears,
unfettered and unbounded.
The Heavenly Dao-Father
bestows upon me boundless pure blessing.

The celestial mind’s orthodox Dharma,
the Alliance of Might,
the Purple Void’s virtue,
the supreme register of the Three Vehicles.
The golden tally, the mysterious canon,
the sealing of the wisdom-sword—
the heart-seal’s luminous clarity, desireless.
First, one’s own ailments vanish;
the heart’s perversities are subdued,
all specters lie concealed.
No need for elaborate faith—
naturally, one dons coarse cloth while holding jade within.

Again—
the formless Dao-body,
circulating yang’s light, densely woven,
pervading the subtle and vast.
Through the dim crossroads of the nebulous,
the vast qi is refined,
brimming with effulgent splendor.
A thousand fathoms of sunlit brilliance,
ten thousand miles of pure wind—
the divine radiance blazes forth.
At the Gate of Yi, feather-transformation,
the Great Mystery’s lineage, spiritually expansive.

Solitary, untrammeled, peerless,
within, immaculate purity—
not a speck of dust allowed to cling.
The embryo-immortal’s snowy visage is nurtured,
entering and exiting without hindrance or constraint.
Roaming the Purple Palace,
feasting in the Jasper Court,
the gift of carefree joy is mine.
Golden lads bear the goblet,
exquisite melodies guide me to the Dragon Tower.

Once more—
in the beginning, vowing to serve the Dao,
hoping for merit lofty enough to ascend as an immortal,
soaring beyond the azure vault.
Years pass, time deepens,
the heart wavers, unnoticed—
emotions entangle, bonds ensnare.
The copper rope tames the tiger,
the iron chain subdues the dragon,
shackling the cloud-treading feet.
No path of escape—
forever sunk in the thousand-fathom abyss.

Facing peril, suffering—who to blame?
No resolve, no decision,
regret for past mistakes.
Intent on cultivating the real,
yet vexed by fame and profit,
ensnared by wine, lust, wealth, and qi.
Household affairs unravel,
practice falters and regresses—
even at death, nothing to grasp.
I urge you to awaken,
spare yourself the burden of delay on both sides.

The Orthodox Teaching of the Great Mystery,
shuns the flourishing, refines the true—pure and still.
Within purity and stillness, the Dao-eye opens,
silver clouds unfurl, streaming from the well.
Essence overflows into emptiness,
qi surges through the Dharma-realm,
brimming to fill the golden crucible.
Sun and moon simmer and blend,
merging with heaven and earth in eternal harmony.

Alone in solitude, peerless,
unchanging in solitude,
the mind comprehends the myriad dharmas.
Transforming and ascending to pay homage to the Supreme Emperor,
returning to the true realm of pure yang.
No night, eternal spring,
immortals gather in assembly,
the divine youth is summoned to receive the mandate.
The Jade Infant chants in farewell,
a cup of everlasting intoxication.

---

*Ten Melodies of the Courtyard Full of Fragrance*

In the quiet chamber, nourish the spirit,
calm the heart, silently circulate—
inwardly observe the single point of true yang.
The cavernous void becomes luminous,
radiantly illuminating the Hall of Light.
It illumines the emptiness of the Dharma-realm,
primordial, standing alone before heaven and earth.
The three luminaries shine,
perfect clarity reveals true form,
enduring through kalpas, everlasting.

Turn back—who questions the self?
Before your eyes, suddenly awakened,
no need for deliberation.
Naturally in accord with the Dao,
both self and things forgotten.
Only the clear wind and bright moon,
communing with the divine, the light of the boundless.
Ascend the path of the Mysterious,
the primordial qi of Hunyuan,
pervading all directions.

---

The ancestral Dao requires no cultivation,
eternally wondrous in function—
awakened, inner and outer become one.
Where the numinous light appears,
it illumines the profound and obscure.
Resplendent, vast, and boundless,
unobstructed, pervading and harmonizing.
The subtle and formless,
the original face from the beginning,
returns to the root, reverts to emptiness.

True emptiness, bright and pure,
solemn, vast,
unfathomable, inexhaustible.
The Dao of heaven,
serene and profound, transcends the mundane cage.
Wondrous transformation arises from the true ancestor,
communing with the origin, returning to the source.
Beyond the three realms,
the spirit shifts, the shell is shed,
beyond the world, the yang-trace appears.

---

The subtlety of the Great Ultimate,
the celestial true in lush abundance,
primordial qi overflows the eyes without bound.
The mysterious pearl ascends and descends,
radiance scattering like sparks.
Gathered into the alchemical crucible,
returning to true essence,
unstained by the clamor of the world.
Turning inward, reflect—
the wondrous body of pure emptiness,
reflects the luminous sprout of the spirit.

Mercury and lead,
gradually congealing, coalescing,
the pure yang elixir is perfected,
eternal, without flaw.
A gourd of spring wine,
a three-foot blade to slay demons.
With confident steps, freely roaming,
tortoise and crane guide,
deep into mist and rosy clouds.
In the realm of carefree wandering,
within the Grotto of Eternal Spring,
time and again, the immortal blossoms are admired.

---

To the ends of the sea and sky,
seeking friends, visiting companions,
yet not a single kindred soul.
Strife over self and others,
wealth, lust, fame, and profit encroach.
Hearing of depravity, lewdness, and false speech,
they exhaust body and life,
unceasingly pursuing.
The true and constant teaching—
my words are direct admonition,
yet in return, resentment runs deep.

Enough, enough—
how can this be endured?
In clarity and silence, circulate,
nurture the true heart.
The primordial qi of Hunyuan,
ascends and descends, settles and floats.
Gradually gathered into the precious crucible,
pure yang is perfected,
touching iron to turn it to gold.
The wondrous mystery revealed,
all demons disperse,
only then do ghosts and spirits revere.

---

Fleeting, the radiant light,
suddenly passed—
reckoning the toil, what has truly been gained?
Youthful complexion withers,
raven locks thin and brittle.
All for the sake of contending for fame and profit,
heedless that life and death cannot be escaped.
At the point of defeat,
like ants on a wheel,
coming and going, thousands of times.

You—awaken the heart,
illuminate the symbols of Zhou,
discern the broken and unbroken lines.
Heaven and earth commune in harmony,
Kan and Li naturally unite.
Yin returns, yang arises in transformation,
pure essence refined,
clear qi soars to the heavens.
The fetal light appears,
the divine wind graceful,
stepping lightly to play amidst jade and jasper.

---

When winter’s breath meets the first month,
jade plum blossoms first unfurl,
waters cold, ice pure in severe chill.
Sparrows alight on lofty trees,
fish dive into the azure depths.
Sea cleansed, sky vast and boundless,
the mysterious pearl descends,
glittering with auspicious radiance.
The fetal star appears,
