a pure name spreads through the world,
virtue naturally shines forth.

Immortals gather in joy,
before the altar, reverent,
offering birthday wishes to the Mysterious Yang.
Golden dragons refine the elixir,
jade beasts swirl, spraying fragrance.
Only wishing for distant years, a life fulfilled,
with heaven and earth,
eternally enduring.
At the ascent to immortality,
phoenixes lead, simurghs welcome,
cloud-steps reveal the August Emperor of the Void.

---

Standing alone at the star altar,
gazing up at the lofty vault,
sincerely cultivating solemn rites.
Incense frequently kindled,
reverently presenting the blue-green memorial.
Only wishing that all beings aspire to the Dao,
hearts opened, understanding—
without attachment, without delusion.
Returning to true essence,
the mysterious gate concealed,
a single resolve, forever unshaken.

All because the heart wavers,
wild schemes, strange fabrications,
what is the purpose of such entanglements?
Lust and passion grow,
virtue gradually wanes.
Like this, dragging through mud and water,
heedless of the ancestral roots of the sages.
As the scriptures say—
if one can be pure and still,
heaven and earth all return.

---

Night departs, dawn arrives,
time swift and urgent,
the four luminaries hasten, urging haste.
This floating life is brief—
who will carefully examine and ponder?
Ceaselessly, deluded heart and vain thoughts,
pursuing karmic debts,
unaware of impermanence.
The form returns to earth,
the three hun and seven po,
chasing scenes, freely wandering.

Who is without
birth and death?
Each person, each one,
difficult to evade, difficult to conceal.
Suddenly awakened,
thus becoming like the wind, wild.
What care for front streets or back alleys?
Singing and dancing,
unfettered, with a broad heart.
In the realm of carefree wandering,
la-li-lo, la-li—
what harm in falling into disrepute?

---

Born with joy, dying with sorrow,
vainly toiling in the dusty world—
how many years of peril?
Success and failure, right and wrong,
honor and disgrace, both wane.
Wealth and nobility—great calamities to the body,
poverty and hardship—
leaving me cold and hungry.
How much better—
neither coming nor going,
the time before father and mother were born.

In emptiness, a symbol appears,
divine wind resplendent,
things dazzle like stars in radiance.
In harmony with heaven’s clarity,
in accord with earth’s subtlety.
The supreme Dao encompasses the Dharma-realm,
returning to the origin,
eternally unchanging.
Beyond birth, beyond increase,
neither growing nor diminishing,
ever equal to the Great Void.

---

The true wind of the primordial era,
the Mysterious Origin, ancestral founder,
propagating the numinous treasure talismans.

Golden chapters and jade scriptures,
words concise yet meaning radiant and new.
Expounding the Dao’s essence, vast and boundless,
pervading heaven and earth, subtle as motes of dust.
To cultivate family and state—
ministers loyal, children filial,
the people’s livelihood naturally pure and tranquil.

Disciples,
do you yet understand?
The wondrous pointer of fortune and adversity,
turning things back to the real.
Washing away the mirror of mystery,
illuminating what lies beyond the body.
In the azure realm, cloud-jewels for companions,
soaring through the void, the sun and moon as neighbors.
With wings upholding heaven,
through the golden gate one ascends in transcendence,
the radiant spirit manifesting in the imperial precincts.

*Ten "Spring in the Garden of Bliss"*

Within primordial chaos,
vague and indistinct, remembering and forgetting—
what agency is there to act?
Since the first division of heaven and earth,
the Three Powers respond in transformation,
mountains and rivers resplendent,
wilds lush with orchids and irises.
Sun and moon shining bright,
the spirit shifts and gleams,
penetrating the mysteries of yin and yang to grasp the sage’s mechanism.
Through the hexagrams’ images,
the lofty dragon and the tiger of Kan appear,
the two beasts locked in contest.

At the mountain’s peak, mist veils the cold stream.
Thunder crashes, jagged and clamorous in the Great Tenuity.
A torrent of the Silver River pours forth,
thousands of pearls,
rippling in cool waves, shimmering,
their light illuminating the Flowery Pond.
Gathering and returning to the source,
drawn back into the crucible,
the fire-tending refined through the hours of Zi and Wu.
When the cinnabar is complete,
it transmutes form and spirit to eternal solidity,
preserving life without decay.

Again,
nurturing the vast and sustaining the spirit,
detaching from desire to clarify emptiness,
observing serenely beyond the world of things.
Behold the Jade Pass crumbling,
a thousand frost-flakes gathering,
the azure cliffs drifting in vastness,
snow descending in clusters.
Within the chaos, suddenly lucid,
in emptiness, a symbol appears,
heaven and earth intermingling as the Four Beasts converge.
Before, the Crimson leads,
behind, the Mysterious follows left and right,
the tiger encircling, the dragon coiling.

From the Yellow Palace, the divine elixir is borne forth.
Encountering this,
the blind and ailing body is healed.
Let the snake swallow one pellet—
it transforms into a dragon with wings;
let the owl or quail grasp it—
instantly they become auspicious simurghs.
Turning iron to gold,
reviving the dead from their bones,
the monstrous *Taowu* upon meeting it reverts to sandalwood.
Do you know?
Ascending as an immortal, entering sagehood—
nothing is too difficult.

Again,
how lamentable this floating life,
so driven by scenes and emotions,
bound by every thing.
To cast aside body and life,
pursuing wealth and honor,
granaries and storehouses filled—
yet in the end, what does it amount to?
Fame like a snail’s horn,
profit like a fly’s head,
stirring mad cravings that ever delude.
Pitiable indeed—
like dust in the eye or a sparrow coveting jewels.
The true is buried in wasteland,
desire’s tassels blind and obscure the Dao.

Turning from truth to delusion,
living in inversion,
the path ahead treacherous,
each step awry.
I urge you to turn back,
cutting resolutely like iron,
to become a steadfast and unyielding man of courage.
Wield the spirit-sword,
shattering the mountain of attachment to dust,
and recognize the words of Kun.

Again,
the *Dao and Its Virtue*, the *Yin Convergence*,
the treasure-store of numinous scriptures—
sages and worthies all revere them.
Discoursing on the dim and indistinct,
the subtle and profound Dao,
the ascent and descent of being and non-being,
the movement and stillness of floating and sinking.
The Six Caverns’ soaring mystery,
the Three Palaces’ wondrous transformations,
the twin gates of meditation and dual cultivation encroaching upon both realms.
The luminous valley of emptiness,
vast, boundless, unfathomable,
neither shallow nor deep.

The numinous light illumines the pure tone,
uniting the qi to comprehend the union of past and present.
Alas, the deluded do not understand—
how many can truly grasp it?
Pursuing peripheral, lesser methods,
they seek blindly and erratically.
Turning from awakening to dust,
changing morning’s resolve by evening,
like a stubborn horse or a frantic ape—hard to seize.
Cease your anger,
lest your efforts show no sign,
corrupting your original resolve.

Again,
the Great One of Prior Heaven,
the Azure Sovereign of the Void,
the Supreme and Unsurpassed.

Within the Jade Firmament’s palaces and halls,
the host of immortals gathers in assembly,
fragrant clouds arrayed in ranks,
their radiance casting crimson hues.
Jade beasts and golden unicorns,
white cranes leading the chariot,
jeweled canopies and jasper blossoms scattering through the void.
The immortal maidens play their instruments,
releasing the True Consort’s graceful form—
her song and dance, her bearing refined.

The immortal melodies resound in endless wonder,
all manifesting before the Three Clarities’ thrones.
Hearken to the Cavern of Primordial Numinosity,
the ascendant mystery of the Supreme Dao,
the revelation of the Three Essentials,
the manifestation of numinous penetration.
Weary of stillness, they unfurl their scriptures,
turning the phoenix-drawn chariot,
the Five Elders escorting the Perfected into the Crimson Palace.
The host of immortals withdraws,
toward Penglai and the Jasper Gardens,
embracing the pure wind.

---

Again,
the Great Dao’s subtle mystery,
abiding since time immemorial,
ever steadfast and unchanged.
Yet the deluded heart, lost in ignorance,
sinks into the cycle of birth and death,
turning back to transform its countenance—
piling bones like mountains.
Only now do they realize
their original form,
casting off the false to return to the true,
gazing beyond the realm of things.
Departing from birth and extinction,
instantly, the true nature without residue
moves in and out of the muddy pellet.
Between the brows, the golden cicada dances,
freely flying forth and returning,
piercing the jade ring.
Gathering the sun’s essence and moon’s marrow,
drawing them into the crucible’s work,
the celestial cycle of fire and timing,
forging the elixir.
Transmuting form and spirit, free from decay,
gradually restoring vigor,
regaining youth to preserve the countenance forever.
When the work is complete,
amidst the depths of rosy clouds,
they ride the auspicious simurgh in stability.

---

Again,
worldly burdens and dusty passions,
daylong stupor—
when will it ever end?
Ensnared by profit, fame, wealth, and desire,
they obscure their celestial truth,
persisting in folly.
Fair maidens and darling sons,
golden fetters and jade shackles,
binding them in unyielding entanglement.
O foolish ones,
accumulating boundless evil karma—
when the reckoning comes, who will bear it?
Summoned to Fengdu, questioned without recourse,
alas, the transgressions of former days
bring retribution in their wake.
Enduring the knife mountains and sword trees,
the biting cold of icy winds,
the boiling cauldrons and pounding pestles,
the torment of ghostly tortures upon the corpse.
A thousand deaths, ten thousand rebirths,
yet no path of escape—
eternally cast into the dark abyss.
In the realm of rebirth,
they take on human form,
wearing horns, tails, fur, and hide.

---

Again,
the Primordial Beginning’s ancestral way,
permeating things before Heaven,
its essence harmonizing with the Great Subtlety.
Within the ninefold yang crucible,
the dragon chants and tiger roars,
thunder rumbles and lightning flashes,
purple mists soar and swirl.
Playfully toying with the black pearl,
boundless and ethereal,
its light bursts forth in streaming radiance,
illuminating Kan and Li.
Penetrating the wondrous mystery,
behold the mastery of this lineage—
a power divine and apart.
Naturally grasping the celestial mechanism,
moving and turning,
following the handle of the Dipper’s array.
With a shout, the Dragon Spring’s sacred sword
sends its light piercing the azure vault,
terrifying the host of demons,
toppling the hundred specters.
Enriching the nation, pacifying the people,
bringing purity, peace, and joy—
the advent of the Formless Perfected.
By the cinnabar script’s decree,
they ascend to Penglai and the Jasper Gardens,
the immortal return beyond the realm of things.

---

Again,
within the golden towers and jasper pavilions,
the fragrant clouds of the jeweled halls
manifest at dawn in the Jade Void.
The phoenix-drawn chariot arrives,
rainbow pendants chiming,
the Heavenly Perfected descending in exile,
long concealed in mortal form.
Suddenly, stillness is realized,
the numinous light penetrating the body,
merging with the Primordial Mystery to emerge from being and nonbeing.
The flying spirit-sword
plunges into the Dragon Palace’s sea-vault,
seizing the luminous pearl.
Streaming radiance blazes from the beginning,
myriad golden rays
enveloping the crucible and furnace.
Refining the pure yang elixir to completion,
piercing Heaven and Earth,
the cosmos in flux—
rising, descending, sinking, floating.
When the work is fulfilled and the origin is returned to,
golden lads and jade maidens,
crane-drawn chariots and fragrant winds
emerge from the cavern lake.
Contending for primacy,
they receive the mantle of the immortals’ leader,
eternally presiding over the sacred isles.

---

Again,
kindness, humility, and gentleness,
relieving suffering and pitying the poor,
adapting to circumstances with flexibility.
Skillfully governing the household and enriching the nation,
cultivating the body and nurturing life,
profoundly plumbing the workings of creation,
shouldering the legacy of Zhuang and Lie.
Embracing and guarding the mysterious yang,
the numinous source firmly secured,
within, the twin gates nurture the vast and unconstrained.
The path of the mysterious penetrates,
releasing the wondrous hue between the brows,
its light connecting with the clouds and mist.
Vast and boundless, obscure and distant,
revolving the sun and moon,
their essence blending with things, ever fresh.
Illuminating the Cavern of Primordial Vacuity,
congealing the void in radiant splendor,
the fetal star’s single point
emerges to transform the prior Heaven.
Responding universally to all directions,
pervading the Dharma-realm,
filling all gaps with flawless virtue and power.
The might of their spiritual force
displays their lifelong mastery,
seizing the immortal’s domain.

---

*Golden Flower of Longevity, Twenty-Nine Stanzas*

The cinnabar field’s root is firm,
the numinous spring drawn in ceaseless irrigation.
Gradually, the yellow sprout grows,
the wind sways the solitary root along its narrow path.
The golden flower blooms in beauty,
its fragrant petals unfurling, breaking through the husk.
Cut and arranged in a silver vase,
paired with dragon’s incense, offered to the Supreme Clarity.

Nurturing life from death,
escaping death to return to life, ever cycling.
Abandoning the false to seek the true,
the true nature clearly knows the body beyond the body.
From nonbeing, being arises,
within being, nonbeing returns—hard to express.
Silently guarding the divine work,
when the work is fulfilled, ascending to the azure sky.
Truly pure, truly still,
in stillness, purity perfects nature and life.
The life-root holds the spirit,
the spirit flourishes in the Yellow Court and Purple Palace’s spring.
The spring’s light gleams bright,
its vast brilliance filling the ancient Dao.
The Dao ascends to the mysterious,
the mysterious, boundless, beyond the heavens.
The numinous origin expands,
the eye’s vista of wind and light, empty and reliant.
Vast and unbounded,
drifting into the Jade Palace, scattering treasures.

The mouth of wondrous penetration,
facing the southern window, gazing at the Northern Dipper.
The jewel, immaculate and serene—
a single luminous pearl rolls into the heavens.
Nonaction, purity, and stillness,
unmoving, unshaken, nurturing nature and life.
A stream of cold light
pervades Penglai, entering the great square.
Boundless and without limit,
coming and going like a passing traveler.
The Dao naturally penetrates the numinous,
the eyes send the returning soul into the distant obscurity.
The wondrous principle of pure vacuity,
profound and perfectly luminous, merging to the depths.
The sea clears, the sky empties—
within emptiness, the knowledge of sacred work.
The heart-pearl surges and leaps,
flames bursting in streaming radiance, flashing and sparkling.
The phoenix ignites the golden crow,
flying past Sinra to the Jade Capital.
The Primordial Mystery’s subtle secret,
silent and desolate, seamlessly entering.
Probing the marvelous work,
the *Yijing*’s images align with the sacred mechanism.
Merged in a single qi,
filling and surging through the void, nothing left unfulfilled.
Gazing to the horizon’s clear light,
suddenly, the harmonizing wind cools Heaven and Earth.

Amid the fiery household, sons and daughters, wives and servants—all bound by craving.
Awakened, delusion dispelled, the belly full, songs rise in joy unspent.
Where lies true freedom? Turning back, the homeland beckons for return.
The vast and open celestial realm—
the moon bathes the limpid river, the sacred cassia blooms full.
Within, the Northern Dipper turns,
revolving the Heavenly Gate to open the Gate of Wisdom.
Within yin, yang arises,
smelting the three *hun* and seven *po* into oblivion.
The jade crucible’s work complete,
the golden elixir in the precious tripod gleams bright.
The radiant cinnabar shimmers,
the sun blazes in the clear sky, emerald clouds descend.

Life is but an illusion, a fleeting transformation—
even at arm’s length, impermanence holds no fear.
Do not long for the next life,
for who can say where the next life will lead?
The road ahead is treacherous,
bristling with swords and spears, the path too perilous to tread.
I urge you to turn back,
and wander with me beyond the world’s confines.
Gazing inward at the Three Luminaries,
the numinous cinnabar fills the tripod to overflowing.
The radiance illumines the sacred infant,
transmuting the cosmos into crystalline purity.
The river and sky at night—moonlit tablets,
the precious cassia, exquisitely clear, gleams pristine.
Only I have nurtured it,
like a jade flower blooming amidst flames.
Floating without blemish,
grasping firmly, preserving spirit, cheeks filled with primordial *qi*.
The mysterious frost of the valley nourishes,
the divine cinnabar ripens, the tripod fragrant.
Pure as the blazing sun,
auspicious *qi* congeals in the void, filling the chamber.
Merged in the primordial unity,
the *Yijing*’s celestial patterns guide to wondrous mystery.
Turning inward to question the self,
recognize the true marvel of the Unborn.
Within, the numinous light unfolds,
ascending to the Moon Palace to anoint the cassia frost.
Heavenly Water harmonized,
ethereal clouds of radiance merge to the depths.
Balancing yin and yang,
the immortal’s work shines in the Northern Emperor’s realm.
The primordial *qi* unites,
earth and heaven born from emptiness, all fulfilled.
The precious and pure, exquisitely formed—
the cassia falls, the golden crow sinks into the azure sea.
Nurturing essence, securing the root,
the dazzling divine pearl follows the wind away.
The moon mirrors the heart of the waves,
the Heavenly Eye crystal-clear, water yields gold.
The hidden dragon at the first nine,
the soaring dragon at nine-five—none lead the flock.
Great indeed is the Creative,
all things flourish in purity, naturally attained.
Nature and appearance draw near,
the Dao manifests in kindness, concealed in function.
Essence and luminosity intermingle,
spirit’s transformations—no fixed path.
The mysterious jade, refined and pure,
the precious and pure, numinous splendor, wind-borne auspice.
Within, all merges and congeals,
stars cluster, auspicious light fills the chamber.
The Pure Yang immortal’s form,
countenance resplendent, riding the phoenix’s wings.
Light as frosted clouds,
ascending into the depths of the heavens to roam the Jade Capital.
From the jeweled palace, exiled and descended—
a single point of fetal light, jade-like in hue.
Virtue’s transformative wind and rule,
spirit’s brilliance, essence’s radiance—countenance ever refined.
Like the wind’s own kin,
naturally attuned to emptiness, worthy of trust.
The immortals’ banners gather,
through the night, pure songs call out in jade tones.
Silent and vast, profoundly still—
the Dao, great and perfectly luminous, like a precious mirror.
The frosty night sky,
things pure, stars sparse, the sea’s cassia full.
Secluded and serene,
alone by the mountain stream, the wind vast and boundless.
Waters emerald, mist clear,
the heart at ease, wisdom pure—beyond the world’s immortal.
The numinous source, empty and still,
things shift, yang flows—like a precious mirror.
The eyes filled with pure light,
solitude and non-action—function lies in constancy.
Rooted in the one nature,
returning to reflect true emptiness, endlessly cycling.
Nature and life both complete,
the Yang Spirit refined, naturally attained.
Congealed in empty stillness,
the dazzling divine wind shines, self-illuminating.
Penetrating the distant heavens,
the one nature, vast and solitary, anoints the cassia’s fullness.
No one, pure and quiet,
profoundly still—cool waves, the wind vast and boundless.
The precious incense’s wisp of smoke,
piercing the cinnabar clouds, descending auspicious immortals.
Grasping the wondrous principle,
in the quiet chamber, deep contemplation—clarity to the depths.
Form released, heart congealed,
light mirrors the vast void, the *qi*-image pure.
The Dharma-body, light and resplendent,
luminous Yang Spirit follows the wind away.
Following the Middle Prime,
essence dense, filling the void, merging with the Emperor’s origin.
No glory, no disgrace,
within, guarding the true origin, ever self-sufficient.
Externally, no fixed abode,
above and below, circulating through the Six Voids.
The Kunlun’s mysterious jade,
borrowing the sun’s light, filling the land.
Merged into a single pearl,
the precious and pure, numinous splendor—five hues unfurl.
The secret transmitted,
the Dharma-eye clear, the divine gaze transcending eons.
Like the moon over the stream,
jade flowers drift, filling the Great Void.
Cool and crystalline,
auspicious light, radiant splendor—ice and jade pure.
Resplendent as the stars,
another true visage emerges from the embroidered curtain.
Suddenly awakened,
sons and daughters, wives and servants—all forgotten.
All affairs cast aside,
the one nature serene, the Dao naturally constant.
The celestial rainbow’s pure blessing,
harmonizing with the Dao, ascending to truth, illuminating supreme virtue.
Virtue’s banquet, the heart’s light,
cinnabar and azure jade—longevity ever increasing.
Breaking open the demon’s den,
vast and obscure, essence flickering in uncertainty.
The eyes filled with splendor,
Yang’s radiance, the luminous pearl gleaming like sunlight.
Utterly true, without thing,
the precious and dazzling, essence’s brilliance—returning and repeating.
Even unto death, unchanging,
surrounded by stars in the cinnabar clouds—enduring and long.
The ignorant rustic,
blindly trusting, madly wandering without aim.
The Great Dao, level and smooth,
yet the heart strays, chasing illusions down forked paths.
Observing the Gate of Wisdom,
the distant and subtle Yang Spirit—existing within the nonexistent.
Daydreaming in the land of Hua Xu,
the luminous soul of the youthful immortal soars in celestial play.
Abandoning greed, severing attachment,
nature still, heart clear—illuminating the precious realm.
The precious realm of Yang’s splendor,
transmuting the body, crystalline as snow, hidden frost.
Empty whiteness shimmering,
beyond the pavilion, the spirit still—relying on self-reflection.
Breaking through the murky crossroads,
revealing the perfect and all-penetrating five-hued pearl.
The Three Passes sealed,
bathed in jade nectar—countenance can be fulfilled.
The divine cinnabar nurtured,
eyes gleaming, exquisitely formed—enhancing the precious radiance.
The mysterious essence, profound and secluded,
the golden palace, the solitary Yang—clear and auspicious.
Two azure lads,
bearing the mysterious pearl into the Crimson Palace.
The spirit still, seated alone,
advancing sharply amidst the tumult—often self-humbled.
The outer gate forever barred,
the inner treasury sealed—guarding the precious vessel.
The mysterious light soars past,
piercing the void, the heart’s crucible shattered.
Golden and azure, cinnabar and jade,
the eyes filled with numinous mushrooms, the *qi*-image pure.
No words, no speech,
trusting in conditions, dissolving past karma.
Self and things both forgotten,
concealing traces, veiling light—virtue naturally grows.
The root of illusion extinguished,
awareness and illumination perfectly merged—forgetting the moon’s reflection.
Directly following the light,
a single heart-pearl merges with the sun’s radiance.

The esoteric formulas of true immortals
demand unwavering faith and loyalty to transmit.
When facing righteousness, be vigilant—
never trust the deceptive words that weigh short and long.

The jade mechanism leaks its secret,
the Dharma-eye’s numinous light pure and bright.
Penetrating the subtle and profound,
the sacred cassia blooms in the wintry forest as white feathers take flight.

Turn the head to reflect and awaken,
seeing through floating life as but a dream.
Abandon things to seek the real,
forgetting thoughts and form to exit the six dusts.

Heaven clear, earth still,
above and below, the void shines with the sun’s brilliance.
The radiant original spirit
roams the Yellow Capital and Purple Court in spring’s embrace.

Forgetting form, relinquishing illumination,
spotless and empty—truly the ultimate subtlety.
Beyond things, rosy clouds glow,
the celestial shore’s waves settle, merging with the Great Subtlety.

The cinnabar apertures unfold,
awakening to the profound mystery’s essential truth.
Emerging as stellar transformations,
the wind rides the numinous gale, the Changes’ images at play.

Silently guard within,
the inner yang pours forth from the midst of nothingness.
What is within this nothingness?
The solitary body, perfectly merged, illumines the sea-pearl.

Spirit clear, *qi* refined,
roaming the cinnabar heavens, bright as day.
Unrestrained above and below,
numinous blossoms densely fill the Great Void.

The scene-wind first appears,
auspicious clouds ride the nine transformations.
Only then is clarity trusted,
roaming the Southern Mound, pouring forth the white orb.

The numinous spirit barely glimpsed,
and already the new spring threads through a single line.
Wandering immortals beyond images
behold the Jade Pool’s five-colored lotuses.

The blind excel in hearing—
a single *qi* of clarity awakens wisdom’s nature.
The deaf can awaken—
two points of spirit enter the precious vessel.

Return from deception to truth,
like a jade mirror hung high in empty space.
Only when reflection is distinct
does one trust the golden elixir forms in a day.

Turn the head to question oneself,
returning the light to Penglai, utterly transparent.
A single mysterious pearl
circulates above and below, emerging from the six voids.

Perfectly merged with Heaven’s essence,
the image adapts, round and penetrating, essence flowing ceaselessly.
Unrestrained within and without,
roaming the midst of heaven without contraction or expansion.

The feathered one’s clarity and refinement
can turn midnight into spring’s daylight.
Roaming and guiding the central heavens,
exquisitely pure and wondrous—profound, yet again profound.

Subtle and dense, the essence-jewel,
scattered scenes of jade flowers stretch across the azure sky.
Sunlight on langgan jade,
the wind stilled, yet the chill of jade pendants lingers.

Meeting thus,
you say my soul flies and my heart trembles.
Seek not, search not—
when we meet, no good intention remains.

Tell them not to bow,
lest the poor remember old debts.
Each turn your head—
even slight deviation makes one a beast of burden.

**Seven Poems on Longing for Immortals**

Mountains link to waters, waters to mountains.
Waters graceful, mountains bright amid the scenery.
Clouds and rosy clouds—one taste of leisure.

Dawn wind wanes,
night deepens.
Moon ascends the plum’s tip, its shadow covering the altar.
The immortal’s sound, the chill of jade pendants.

The plain sky clears,
petals scatter like jade.
Faint numinous mist spreads across the earth.
Cold light, crisp *qi*, pure.

Precious essence congeals,
jade dawn stills.
The two luminaries’ radiance dazzles the sun’s brightness.
Langgan dots the Star of Longevity.

The Dao-heart tranquil,
the wisdom-lamp bright.
The jade-playing lad opens the Dao-scriptures.
Clear as the sound of jade pendants.

Serene and still,
radiant and congealed.
The swallow rests by the flowery pool, swallowing jade essence.
Returning to purity, the body naturally chaste.

Within, peace;
without, uprightness.
Within and without, no dwelling—all surveyed in clarity.
Every thing, every head, awakened.

*Qi* pure,
wisdom numinous.
Cold light reflects into the precious vessel.
Effortlessly transforming into jade essence.

Extinguish worldly passions,
awaken true sincerity.
Retreat to forests and springs, wandering clouds and waters.
Mist-light fills the eyes.

Radiant and still,
penetratingly clear.
Form released, heart congealed—the Dao naturally manifests.
Ascend the mysterious, illuminating the Jade Capital.

Diligently cultivate,
awaken to non-action.
Only wish the heart wise, the world unconfused.
Know clearly the mechanism of heaven and earth.

Precious rosy clouds glow,
brilliant and subtle.
The Purple Court and Green Capital await their time.
The Jade Palace reveals its sacred form.

The wisdom-blade appears,
slaying the Three Corpses.
Abide in integrity, purity, and detachment from love.
Serenely guard the plain essence.

Eyes bright,
the Dao full.
The azure sea’s cinnabar blossoms reveal the Jade Clarity.
Still, a single star.

**Six *Daolianzi* Poems**

Illumine the ancestral origin,
awaken to the true Chan.
A single point of numinous light emerges from before heaven.

The Changes’ green, cinnabar red,
yellow and plain mystery.
Still and auspicious, filling the mountains and rivers.

Frosty sky, wind stilled—naturally congealed.
Scattered jade flowers,
precious cassia round.

Speak not of the Dao,
seek not Chan.
Non-action and purity—excellent causes and conditions.

Awaken to the mysterious—
mysterious, yet again mysterious.
Cultivate true awakening,
seize the immortals’ authority.

Piercing gaze, radiant play in the cinnabar heavens.
The Five Numinous Ones take flight,
the Changes’ feathered immortals.

The practice of cultivation—
diligently inquire.
The unborn, undying Dao bears its task.

The Changes’ clear sky—
know the original heart.
Illumine movement and stillness,
stabilize the floating and sinking.

The jade infant ever guards the golden vessel.
Rosy clouds glow,
scattering precious peaks.

Truth conceals falsehood,
falsehood conceals truth.
Released, the solitary body severs distant and near.

Within the primordial chaos,
no self, no others.
Spirit communicates with the Dao,
the Dao with spirit.

Still as empty jade, like the ice-wheel.
Rolling the celestial river,
emerging from the six dusts.

From this head it arises,
to that head it proceeds.
Through the face’s gate, it enters and exits freely.

Heaven’s light appears—
a single star.

The true aspect,
the originally formless body—naturally bright.
Appearing in the vast yang,
entering great accomplishment.

Beneath the brows, the eyes—
the eyes’ essence.
The essence-light shines, brilliantly awakened.

Appearing in perfect merging,
illuminating beyond things.

Ascend to the Supreme Emperor,
circling the celestial court.
By the Moonflower Peak, play with cloudy blossoms.

Meeting the golden lad,
the Jade Clarity appears.

**Eleven *Xijiangyue* Poems**

Between the brows, intertwined amber,
the eyes’ pupils refined like dragon’s saliva.
Within the tripod, smoke curls to the Chan heavens.
A single point of numinous light emerges.

The Supreme Clarity illuminates this jade image,
the Tathāgata verifies this golden immortal.
The clear stream’s divergent branches share a single source.
Only by awakening to the principle does one know the highest good.

Vast *qi* congeals into a precious seal,
the clear wind scatters the clouded obscurity.
A wheel of bright moon illuminates the void.
Best to dance the spirit’s play.

Piercing through the Jade Capital above,
breaking open the Golden Gate within.
The original spirit sits alone in the Palace of Broad Cold.
Leading the host of immortals in ancestral veneration.

Regarding this body of mine, fraught with afflictions,
gazing upon the real—non-action, non-doing.

The Dipper’s handle turns the jade pivot of nature,
sun and moon cycle through heaven and earth in fullness.
Marking the ice-ash and snow-char,
firing them into flame-jujubes and intertwined pears.
All at once bestowed upon the lofty and graceful,
enhancing my wisdom and intelligence.
Yet all is blocked by household affairs and eaves,
obstructed by karmic hindrances.
Who can distinguish *li* from *wei*, right from wrong?
Turning away from the sacred offerings and Daoist discourse.
Clouds part, and every household sees the moon;
timely rains bring blossoms everywhere.
The pupil-child deeply enters emerald mist and rosy clouds,
guided to the everlasting spring of unending night.
No attachment to wind, flowers, snow, or moon,
casting aside wealth, honor, and fame.
Hollowing the heart, abandoning ambition, dismissing cleverness,
washing clean the illness of ignorance.
Shattering all illusions of the human realm,
only then does one penetrate the perfect completion beyond things.
Forgetting form, forsaking reflection, *qi* and spirit congeal.
Devoted to the root, delighting in heaven, knowing fate.
A staff bears a gourd of spring’s brew,
a case holds three feet of lustrous jade-sword.
The precious mirror between the brows subdues demons and evil,
sitting guard through the deep of midnight.
The golden tripod burns white snow,
the jade furnace refines the yellow sprout.
Elixir-light shimmers, rippling with jade brilliance,
heaven and earth intermingle in misty radiance.

Delusion sinks the body in seas of suffering,
awakening brings the moon forth on the western river.
A gentle breeze stirs the fragrance of osmanthus,
startling awake from a dream of roaming immortals.

Where do crane and phoenix lead?
A servant boy laughs, pointing toward the boundless dawn.
A jade tablet with golden characters bears the name "Southern Flourish"—
another realm between heaven and earth.

No need to gaze at stars or worship the moon,
why chant precepts or pore over scriptures?
Today I entrust you with this earnest charge:
life and death must rely on nature and destiny.

The Dao reveals all-knowing, supreme,
spiritual powers and the dharma-realm made perfectly clear.
No labor is needed—merit completes itself.
The will rests in non-action and purity.

Do not cling to gold, silver, or treasures,
nor covet jade-like beauty or flower-like faces.
A hundred years end in empty nothingness—
turning away from the Dharma of the Unborn.

To grasp the profound truth of the Mysterious,
one must understand the ancestral ways of the Most High.
The utterly divine, utterly sagely—awakening knows no bounds.
This freedom and ease arise of themselves.

Sever the copper ropes and iron nets,
strike open the jade locks and golden shackles.
Upon the stormy seas of suffering, board the spirit raft—
roam and play beneath the shade of the Tree of No Shadow.

No need to forget the signpost pointing at the moon,
why pluck osmanthus or pluck flowers?
Within the cauldron of the Great Void, refine cinnabar,
condensing the priceless Mystic Pearl.

Hold fast to the fundamental principle of nurturing life,
delusion leads to the mechanism of death.
Abandon the perverse, uphold the upright—what doubt remains?

There exists a wondrous and mysterious delight—
the infant frolics in the Jasper Park,
the azure youth laughs and points toward the Jade Pool.
Within the Moon of the Western River, cinnabar branches are plucked,
preserving and enhancing the spirit for enduring vision.

*Fisherman’s Pride, Five Poems*

Sunlight refines the yang soul in empty space,
the turning jade pivot revolves the celestial net.
Though near at hand, none perceive the man before their eyes.
A single thread connects—
the furnace opens, the cauldron splits, and celestial light appears.

Auspicious jade blossoms scatter in flakes,
fragrant winds softly brush the divine countenance.
In cold purity and serene emptiness, the feast is refined.
Truly enviable—
the Jade Emperor ascends the Liao Yang Palace.

Earthly po and heavenly hun diligently refined,
the essence of sun and marrow of moon yearn for each other.
The two luminaries exchange radiance like flashing lightning.
Clearly seen—
within the jade furnace, ten thousand golden flowers bloom.

Gently gathered and hammered into flakes,
round and round, shaped into a luminous form.
Dazzling the Great Void, jade hail is refined.
The divine light dazzles—
flying cinnabar pierces into the Hall of Pervading Clarity.

A century’s span races like a galloping steed,
floating splendor dazzles the eye through fleeting dust.
Mysterious vision cleansed, the spirit’s power set in motion.
The message is clear—
on the path of the Unborn, the truth is known.

Mists disperse, jade pupils ascend in celestial play,
yang light gradually reveals as pure yin withdraws.
Ten thousand specks of numinous cinnabar gleam on the void’s wall.
Bright and resplendent—
the elixir’s luster matches gold and jade in hue.

Chaos and obscurity traverse the cosmos,
colored clouds disperse, revealing the luminous jade hare.
The sun sets in the Salty Pool, then turns back to gaze.
The heart awakens—
congealing the hun and obscuring the po, the Golden Crow delights.

Fair and graceful, bearing the cold radiance of the ritual vase,
the triple-hued mist swirls in pure simplicity.
Directly encountering the Jasper Heaven, she carries the Woman Comet.
Unstained—
the cinnabar script forever binds her to the Jade Palace.

The Great Dao, most true, requires no words,
its radiance concealed, hidden in profound secrecy.
Preserve and refine the original essence without loss.
Dissolve the yin substance—
auspicious clouds bear forth the numinous yang sun.

Illuminating and shattering the gloom, it commands Heaven’s awe,
in utter vagueness and indistinctness, emptiness holds reality.
Luminous and immaculate, pure and white, they assist each other.
Attaining true unity—
the cinnabar script on jade tablets completes the immortal’s work.

*Immortal Homeland, Four Poems*

Easily attaining the pavilion of spontaneity,
beyond its eaves, pure splendor blends with freshness.
Cloud-linked peaks soar at the corners of the eaves,
numinous springs—
willow banks and misty waves connect to distant rivers.

Virtuous scholars conceal themselves in mystery,
mysterious vision cleansed, things naturally relinquished.
Within the empty altar, true delight is found,
dragon’s saliva—
sacred talismans lightly float, plucking the plain strings.

The Great Dao is fundamentally non-action,
within and without, serene in the wondrous mechanism.
In stillness and emptiness, true flavor is savored,
eyebrows raised—
the cold and pure divine light shines everywhere.

Graceful and elegant in bearing,
whether sitting, lying, walking, or dwelling, she follows at hand.
Winged, she ascends the central heavens, becoming a jade figure,
without doubt—
her place is in the Southern Palace, manifesting the Purple Tenuity.

The ancestral Dao is secretly transmitted,
having caught the rabbit, discard the snare and abide in spontaneity.
The eye’s horizon expands, revealing the Great Simplicity,
pure yang—
the sun’s radiant essence makes all things fresh.

Vague and indistinct, pervading the three thousand worlds,
foreknowing the shifting tides of hills and streams.
At the ocean’s depths, waves surge as the dragon emerges,
thrusting through the mysterious—
divine light bursts forth into the nine heavens.

The ancestral Dao is intermittently transmitted,
only then is the lineage’s wind confirmed to harmonize with nature.

The movement and stillness, being and non-being—guest and host in harmony,
the earth and heaven.
Above and below, the circling sun and moon shine fresh.
Radiance fills the three thousand worlds,
piercing valleys with numinous splendor, ever unchanging.
Within the void, a true jade figure takes form, ascending to heaven.
The Treasure Ease Child holds the elder’s white mystery.
The jade cage gleams,
guarding purity—
with steadfast resolve, utterly sever all dissipation.

Hold the inner realm,
moonlight piercing twin forests.
The jade child plays,
pointing afar to the heart of the azure pool—
scoop up the gold from the water.
The numinous treasure glows,
the lamp of wisdom shines,
divine light bears its task.
Face-to-face, yet none seek to grasp it.
If you awaken,
seeing clearly,
disaster and misfortune will not approach.
Dragons and tigers submit, ghosts and spirits revere.

**Two Poems to "The Courtyard Fragrance"**

The Dipper’s handle turns,
the Purple Tenuity first appears,
distant plains merge in pure clarity.
Cloud jade is ground away,
heaven’s treasure gleams with infant radiance.
Jade osmanthus and jasper forests, pristine feathers,
ascending the mysterious, they ride the dazzling flow of essence.
Cold and wondrous,
cinnabar and gold,
the mighty beacon transforms into a faint star.

Star emblems,
elegant and serene feasts—
pure wind conceals its rhythm,
forgetting form, forgetting appearance.
May our lineage awaken to understanding,
the heart released from floating glory.
Do not dwell on the distance of clouded mountains,
lift your gaze—
let not the numinous brightness dim.
In such truth,
the Azure Child flies away,
piercing the great Orchid City.

Again—
washing the belly, fasting the heart,
through frost and snow,
seeking the divine treasure’s essence-jewel.
Rely on your single act,
the pupil beholds the azure void.
The four bright heavens, free of floating veils,
ice cracks open—
all suspended images grow clear.
In the Starry Dawn Lodge,
jade tablets and golden characters—
who shall bind their fragrant name?

On the path,
people remain deluded,
their hearts straying onto crooked trails,
erring their way forward.
Returning to listen, long lost to the past,
movement and stillness arise anew.
The road to the divine Brahma palace is steady,
feasting in jasper forests,
light scatters like misty clouds.
The divine work is wondrous,
pure yang refined—
at dawn, the Purple Tenuity star appears.

**Three Poems to "Slow Voices"**

Beside misty waters, I dwell,
my humble abode on Song Peak,
the ends of heaven distant, communication cut off.
Yet enlightenment is not far—
before my eyes, the undivided pure wind.
The solitary precious moon, lofty and penetrating,
imprints a thousand pools,
illuminating the mysterious cavern.
No self, no other—
the primordial immortal scene of blended splendor,
one true emptiness.

With such understanding, heart-bound friends,
why offer tribute horses
or tread the dust of post roads?
I, weary in form,
need not travel far to meet you.
Bowing deeply,
flowing together—do not blame,
extend boundless compassion,
let not the heart be troubled.
Open the azure eye,
cast the divine light into the body,
entering the unmoving ancestral Dao.

Again—
the original unity of nature—
where was it arranged?
It came from the vague and indistinct void.
Receiving qi, forming shape,
father’s essence and mother’s blood congeal into an embryo.
Gradually, the fetus completes and descends,
before it can grow,
emotions turn wayward.
Self-inflicted ruin—
on the road, toiling endlessly,
slowly entangled in dust.

Vainly, a lifetime spent in inversion,
obscuring heaven’s natural treasure,
buried for ten thousand ages.
If you awaken to life’s prior truth,
the mysterious crucible splits the heart open.
Merging with the sun, congealing pure yang’s elegance,
gathering the five directions,
rosy clouds swirl back.
The jade morning manifests—
then forget form, abandon reflection,
ride straight to the Jasper Terrace.

Again—
hewing open chaos,
striking through Kunlun,
the Dipper’s handle turns the wheel of heaven.
On the winding shore, the crow and toad,
exchanging soaring, fleeing souls.
The mercury tripod and lead furnace blaze,
refining golden essence,
wood’s liquid and cinnabar’s dawn.
Starlight manifests,
dispersing the primordial one qi,
ten thousand lands veiled in rosy mist.

Luminous, still, without obstruction,
clashing mountains, rivers, forests, and gardens—
ten thousand gleams shimmer.
High and low, no difference—
distant plains merge in pure essence.
Face-to-face, who awakens to this?
In vain, laboring,
turning from enlightenment to chase illusions.
Cease anger—
like a blind man groping an elephant,
erring, losing heaven’s truth.

**Two Poems to "The River All Red"**

Spring flowers, autumn moon,
from ancient times to now, but a fleeting moment.
Wealth and nobility, wisdom and folly—
how many times have they turned?
Life and death, like ants, follow their cycles.
The immortal realm, though near,
its path beyond the dust—
as if separated by ten thousand mountains.
Awakening, return—
truly nurture simplicity in tranquility,
rejoice in pure leisure.

Worldly affairs, all unstained—
a body of purity,
a heart of non-action, observing with stillness.
Jade’s brilliance, gold’s radiance—look outward.
Bursting forth, ten thousand measures of bright pearls,
pushed through the two gates.
Within the Supreme Ultimate’s palace,
the inner elixir congeals.
Pure wind, fragrant and resplendent, pierces jade branches.
Ten thousand qi circulate, returning to one body—
a thousand true wondrous uses,
emotions without duality.
Merging into the Middle Primordial realm,
flutes and cranes drift ethereally,
auspicious qi coils and lingers.
The jade decree fills the empty azure,
names inscribed for immortal ascent—
riding chariots, driving phoenixes and simurghs.

Again—
raising the hairpin, staff in hand,
enjoying the moon, the wind’s message along the path.
Embracing the one, harmonious and balanced,
nurturing the knife-point’s mercury and lead.
Golden essence, wood’s liquid, moisten the radiant field.
Securely guarding the three spirits, returning to the fire palace,
five-colored clouds cover the earth,
light piercing the Brahma heavens.
Tiger and dragon intertwine—
the cosmos’s bright pearl is seized,
qi’s image trickles like a stream.
Treasure clouds glow with the sun,
brilliant yang’s radiance blazes,
reflecting back into the mysterious cavern.
Within the merged, dawn and dusk blend.
The dharma of ten thousand images, clear and round,
competing in freshness with all things.
Profound stillness, cold source—
ever before the eyes.
Within the void, rippling waves surge in the essence’s abyss.
Nine-hued yellow clouds shroud the night’s mist,
three peaks’ blue haze
reach far to ten thousand rivers.
The Dao complete, pure and refined—
yin’s mists scatter,
all things come to life.
The treasure’s image holds the spirit’s essence—
amid the six dusts’ heap,
lifting forth a blessed immortal.

**A Leaf Boat**

Ten thousand images surge open, vast and boundless,
the primordial qi blends in empty support.
The sea’s moon, tranquil and golden,
illuminates the heart of heaven.
Beyond the eyelashes, majestic spirit’s radiance unfolds,
an ice body, snow skin, graceful and delicate.
Steadily crossing jasper forests,
ascending the jade peak.

**Two Returning Songs**

The principle of cultivating truth—
where lies the mechanism of the Dipper’s meditation?
Vast thoughts of tangled vines, empty strife—
many efforts, all vain labor,
how could they compare to awakening to non-action?

Open the Dao’s eye,
the single nature emerges from confusion.
Dense bamboo does not hinder flowing water,
lofty mountains cannot block white clouds in flight.

Ascending the subtle purples of the Empyrean,
the Void-and-None Dao,
where primordial qi harmonizes of itself.

The dark mirror’s cleansing—few worthy scholars remain,
while those who cling to dust and turn from awakening are many,
frittering days in vain.

Open the Dharma-eye,
a single nature pierces through Saṃsāra.
Luminous, clear as autumn’s cold moon,
crystalline, like rippling waves of jade.
Pouring forth to moisten the numinous bough.

**Waves and Sands**

Seeking the Dao, consulting masters,
pledging vows, submitting petitions.
Be vigilant from beginning to end, diligent in cultivation.
Yield to others, advance the self, ever patient in humility,
all affairs governed by boundless compassion.

The mechanism of ascending immortals lies broken—
hold fast to rectitude, unwavering.
Uphold the practice of the Primordial Jade Purity.
When the sun of wisdom shines in the void, who shall illuminate it?
Stellar eyes, lingzhi brows.

**Two Songs of Picking Mulberries**

Strength and fate deride each other—
rely on truth to see who is right, who is wrong.
Once I sought the Western Gate at the Northern Palace;
know then the Eastern Wall’s words,
sincere and fair—why doubt the nurturing of simplicity?

The vulgar cannot comprehend.
Awaken the worthy and wise,
to walk my path in shared principle.
Rejoice in heaven’s decree, pass through life by following conditions.
When merit is complete in years to come,
the old path to the Divine Empyrean
holds our immortal tryst.

Our kind may well lament—
discarding the dark pearl,
adrift at the edge of heaven.
Floating clouds, flying catkins, rootless and anchorless,
the heart strays down divergent paths,
each rising thought leading steps astray.

Hear early the call of mist and rosy clouds—
within the immortal realm,
how fine to press onward!
The Three Mountains lie close, not far,
where the Jade Hall of Ever-Spring,
the twin shores of Lingxi,
brim with jasper blossoms.

**Two Songs of Wandering Hua-Xu**

On ancient banks, peach buds unfurl,
the new moon’s pure light intertwines in splendor.
How many in the dusty world glimpse this?
Only I fix my gaze with lofty intent.

A sigh—
a sigh—
turning back, the distant journey to immortal realms.

Roaring through the ancient wind, beneath the moonlit stream,
radiance gleams through the vast, limpid void.
Lovely eyes glance, clear and round,
vanishing, then waxing full again.

Light connects—
light connects—
jade osmanthus in frosty groves, crystalline and pure.

**Two Songs of Voicing Grievances**

Forest springs, a reclusive livelihood,
forsaking the clamor of prosperity.
The immortal of verdant Zhongshan peaks,
eyes brimming with numinous cinnabar.

Congealing the white elixir,
blending with cinnabar clouds,
bursting forth jasper blossoms.
Cloud waves, misty billows—
beyond the isles, Fanghu’s abode,
where dwell the people of that realm.

The Great Void, boundless and fathomless,
where no-qi blends at the center.
Glancing back, the revolving tripods,
jade liquid overflowing with golden sand.

Radiant spirit’s glow,
flashing beams of light,
shimmering jasper blossoms.
Clouds recede, waves subside,
the sea stills, the sky clears—
the vast expanse’s home.

**Night Travel by Boat**

Within the snow-washed pouch, no worldly things.
Carefree and indolent—who would constrain me?
No fear of hollow fame,
no glory, no disgrace.
How few follow in such lightness!

Alone I sit, plucking strings, the goblet brimming with fine wine.
With hairpin raised, I watch the drifting clouds unbroken.
Turtles glide on the pond,
cranes stride before the grotto,
wind and moon, water and mountain, pine and bamboo.

Alas for the splendid years spent plumbing profound truths—
midway stalled,
the teachings left masterless.

**The Daoist Abbey**

The abbey stands desolate,
old friends grown distant and faint—
how much worse the gloom of dusk’s sorrowful rain.

Alone I sit, a guest in silent emptiness,
my crimson heart laid bare—
who would fathom its depths?
Sweeping my sleeves, I return to the mountains,
to the depths of emerald streams,
to whisper to falling blossoms and flowing waters.

**Two Libations to the River Moon**

I. The wondrous Dao of serene emptiness,
merged with the dim and boundless,
pervades the subtle, the pure, the absolute.
Emerging before heaven, it illumines the Lord of Images,
filling the eye with streaming fragments of radiant mist.
The impure form dissolves,
jade scrolls flourish,
the sacred tripod’s elixir congeals.
The cinnabar bloom gathers its splendor,
pristine and profound, a single hue of clarity.

Essence □□□ fills the void,
clear as an autumn night,
the sea’s osmanthus untouched by wax or wane.
Shining through ancient and present, it pierces the luminous qi,
brimming like a jade flask of spring snow.
Resplendent as the sun’s pure essence,
the steadfast heart’s hidden purity,
it nourishes the true immortals’ delight.
The cinnabar script summons the decree—
ascending to the Three Luminaries in array.

II. The primordial Dao of the Mysterious Origin,
boundless, formless,
stands solitary in stillness and silence.
Pervading all directions, it links above and below,
its gaze stretching to the faintest glimmer of celestial light.
Concealing and revealing, vanishing and enduring,
piercing non-being to thread being,
its benevolent work leaves no trace.
Resonant and unconstrained, it releases transformation—
a single numinous essence in the vast expanse.

Ascending the forest, it penetrates true yang,
its perfect brightness illuminating all,
allowing not a speck of dust to hide.
The principle must inevitably unfold—yet still ungrasped,
I explain it plainly to my disciples.
The sun’s hall gleams with auspicious light,
the moon’s palace shimmers with propitious hues,
a thousand streams enriched by jade waves.
Spirit congeals, form dissolves—
the jasper cliffs stand as before, verdant and sheer.

**Three Southern Branch Songs**

I.
A blink—lost through kalpas,
a glance—separated by ten thousand peaks.
A single truth divides its auspice through twin gates,
merged with primordial chaos—
what difficulty remains?

The body crumbles, golden wings take flight,
yang’s doubt pierces the jade ring.
Suddenly awakened, I wash the dream-soul’s realm.
The lotus petals drift away, heartless,
beyond the world, alone in purity.

II.
The heart’s resolve is pure and steadfast,
the will’s truth unyielding and true.
Transcending the pitfalls of cessation and permanence,
the eye’s horizon widens,
radiant, illuminating the luminous clarity.

The brocade of heaven and earth gleams,
the intricate world shines.
The limpid void, like a flawless jade disc, instantly rounds into perfection.
Shedding the husk, the essence (目十爫十缶)—
a single star in the azure sky.

III.
Weary of stillness, I once dwelled in the marketplace;
disdaining clamor, I then lived in the mountains.

Where in the communion with the True is there no purity and leisure?
Within and without, I roam carefree,
unfettered by the climb for profit or renown.
The husk shed, I manifest in emptiness,
the form forgotten, I gaze beyond the world.

The two spirits congeal in pristine clarity, emerging through the Gate of Yang.
The crane’s nature, light and fleet,
departs for ancient Chang’an.

**Two Red-Window Poems**

Seek the Mystery Gate—cease your vain quests.
I point to you the true aim of cultivation:
ever pure and still, the mind unadrift,
preserve the primordial essence without loss.

Refine the yang soul, dissolve the yin substance.
Between the brows, the divine radiance takes flight.
Through the Dipper’s handle, turn the Celestial Pivot,
embrace the single wheel of the red sun.

Again—

Cast off worldly passions, return to true principle.
Strike the double gates, the Mystery Gate swings wide.
Spit forth the divine light, piercing the curtains and veils,
revealing the wondrous yang body.

The Golden Crow’s essence, the Jade Hare’s marrow—
illuminating heaven and earth, the pupils gleam with luminous clarity.
The distant red window blazes with radiant perfection,
shining through Penglai’s depths to the very end.

**Two "Pointing Crimson Lips" Poems**

Sword at back, staff in hand,
I tread the path, piercing the clouds.
The green moss parts—
beyond the misty pine screen,
I brush the stone and sit by the stream.

Wine drunk from a single cup,
a clear tune played in harmony.
Nothing is amiss—
who could compare as companion?
The bright moon, the pure wind, and I.

Lush hues swirl in mist,
thick and curling through the vast expanse.
Light flashes and flickers—
in dreamlike ease, a pearl is swallowed,
a single fetal star descends.

Exiled to the mortal realm,
I regret the errors of old.
Passions fade and wither—
I summon my disciples,
together we keep our pact with the Azure Capital.

**The Moon Shines on Layered Mountains**

The Dipper’s handle turns, uniting the single nature;
the jade pivot revolves, unlocking the double gates.
Towering waves churn, snow-like blossoms whirl—
mid-autumn night,
the moon shines on layered mountains.

Alone I pace the starry altar.
Sword-light slashes the corners of the heavens, chilling all who near.
Five Immortal Spirits cradle green simurghs,
soaring into the Hua-Xu paradise of dreams.

**The Peaceful Command**

In the Hall of Fungi, at ease, I open the cinnabar scriptures.
Incense smoke curls, the wisdom lamp burns bright.
Voices harmonize with flowing waters, the jade tones pure.
Clouds disperse, mists withdraw—
in a single glance, the Jade Pool’s purity spreads.
The Grotto-Heaven’s mystery shines, auspicious light congeals.
Clearly seen, suddenly awakened—
turning back, I re-enter the perfected Dao.
The form forgotten, I ascend in feathered transformation,
the Void Sovereign entrusts me with the celestial talisman.

**Two "Wu Ling Spring" Poems**

The Supreme’s Primal Unity qi,
luminous and pure as finest jade.
Clearer than drifting white clouds, unrolling or furling,
in clarity, the presence of non-being within being.

The cool, serene divine light sways in emptiness,
transforming without constraint.
Flowing above and below through the six voids—
a single night-shining pearl.

A single parasol leaf falls beyond the window,
golden chrysanthemums rise from the sparse fence.
Staff in hand, cap askew, I wander at ease,
bewildered by the winding Pool of Qujiang.
The crane’s chariot hurries back along the old path—
turning my head, I hasten toward the immortal’s tryst.
Clouds reflect the laughing Blue Lad’s query:
“Where is your home? By the Wu Ling Stream.”

**The Oriole’s Song**

Foolish old man, foolish old man,
deluded by illusions, lost in dreams,
a lifetime of confusion.
Why each day knit your brows,
vexing body and heart?
I urge you: turn back, return to the Great Dao,
plumb the profound mysteries of the arcane.
Refine the elixir’s light, merge with the Middle Origin—
reveal the jade countenance of the celestial hour.

**Cherishing the Tender Babe**

Suddenly awakened, I turn my head,
casting aside worldly affairs.
Swiftly gather the heart, hasten back to the Great Dao.
In emptiness seek the true,
transmit the luminous teaching from the formless.
Best of all—
the cinnabar blossom appears, the light returns in reflection.
Probe the subtle and profound, manifest the heaven’s abstruse depths.
Illumine within and without, the floating and sinking, the inversion.
One qi through the double gates,
blending the hundred spirits, dividing the three essentials.
Mysterious and wondrous—
auspicious clouds bear aloft
the jade countenance of the celestial hour.

**Variation on "Plucking the Cassia Branch"**

Clearly, beyond appearances, return to the ancestral origin—
the Dao-eye complete.
Coming and going, continuous and unbroken,
rising and falling, floating and sinking, free to wander.
Most profound and abstruse—
the sun’s essence, the moon’s marrow, placed within the furnace,
one qi refined and simmered.
The elixir congeals, firm and bright,
its radiance ascending to the heavens in dazzling purity.
Transformed, I fly as an immortal.

**Gazing Afar**

The Supreme Mystery’s wondrous secret—
once awakened, no need for words.
The mind-ground suddenly opens in enlightenment,
pure coolness pervades within.
Piercing the five aggregates’ mountain peak,
the mountain’s frosty sky reveals the bright moon,
illuminating all through the ages,
without wax or wane.

The Jade Child rests in the numinous palace—
nimbly pluck the cinnabar branch.
Delight in the realm of eternal spring,
penetratingly discerning the separation from birth and death.
Beneath the tree of no-shadow,
alone I sit in perfect stillness and freedom,
listening to the tuneless melody—
within it, a world apart.

**Ascending the Western Heights**

Awaken the mysterious essence, clarify the true qi,
penetrate the primordial within.
By day, the yang soul; by night, the yin spirit—they merge.
Internally divided into three hues,
yet blended into one like the lotus.
The jade hour’s round mirror,
auspicious clouds floating, their light striking the Jade Palace.
Dispersing the yin vapors, congealing the pure and refined,
returning the spirit to transformation, moving through the numinous void.
The bright image hangs suspended,
brilliant and resplendent.
Roaming the central heavens,
the lush rosy clouds’ jade tones pure.
Rainbow banners and feathered standards,
bearing the jade chariot, the treasure-scented immortal winds.

**Two "Spring in Qin Garden" Poems**

In this world, as a person,
none surpasses parents in profound virtue and deep grace.
From the ten months in the womb, three years of nursing,
turning dry for wet, how much toil endured?
Grown to adulthood, the five eyes of the heart arise—
outsiders sow discord, each leading their own gate.
Who awakens?
Like the owl facing its nest,
the karmic retribution circles back.

Cease this vain toil of the spirit.
Never forget the grace of the womb and nursing.
Recall the crow’s filial return, the gibbon’s evasion of arrows—
with sincere filial reverence, what curse could befall one?
In all matters, do not defy,
follow their countenance, harmonize their needs.
In food and drink, cold and warmth, use them in due measure.
Preserve this from beginning to end—
the Dao’s light shines across the four seas,
virtue spreads in pure sincerity.

Again—

In youth’s bloom, I suddenly awakened and turned back,
indulging my nature, following my truth.
Abandoning father, mother, brothers, and sisters-in-law,
wife, sons, nephews, and daughters—
a solitary cloud, a wild crane, for over twenty springs.
Like a drifting duckweed, I followed the winds,
settling wherever fate allowed,
letting others laugh at my indolence.
Do not blame me—
weary of life’s falsity and pretense,
I awakened to my former existence.

Clearly knowing the primordial spirit beyond appearances.

Radiant treasures, immaculate without blemish, unstained by dust.
Mastering the four seasons’ chariot,
pointing to heaven as canopy,
earth’s authority as carriage,
sun and moon as discourse.
Rolling through the starry river,
breaking through the Ox and Dipper,
gathering and dispersing the five-colored clouds afloat in the void.
Traversing the Three Realms,
manifesting the August Sage Ancestor of the Void,
the Celestial Worthy of Primordial Beginning.

*To the tune of* "Court Full of Fragrance"

With grain sacks and bamboo hats,
through cloud-capped mountains and waterways,
enduring distant roads, undaunted by wind and frost.
To seek the celestial treasures,
I lay bare my heart to you.
First, the supreme principle reveals the One Nature;
then the Two Modes appear,
and the Three Palaces shine resplendent.
Beyond the Mystic Pass,
hovering in the void, luminous—
the rising sun spreads its crimson light.

All spirits,
each receiving their mandate—
who can preserve
the primal yang within the Jade Treasury?
Myriad gods intermingle in splendor,
the ninefold qi blends at the center.
A single Mystic Pearl is formed,
its divine radiance
illuminating the Southern Prosperity.
In the Liao-Yang Lodge,
entering and exiting the Flowering Chamber,
all join in singing *Court Full of Fragrance*.

*Upper Clarity’s Grand Mystery Collection*, Scroll Nine, concludes.

*(This tune was originally titled "Reduced-Character Magnolia Flower.")*

*Upper Clarity’s Grand Mystery Collection*, Scroll Ten
Composed by Gu Shehou Shanyuan

**Quatrain: Nurturing Vitality in Forest and Spring**

In quiet solitude, mountain dwelling excels—
a lone household ‘midst verdant peaks.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the cave’s rosy clouds.

In quiet solitude, mountain dwelling excels—
deep streams mirror the heavens.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the jade-green river.

In quiet solitude, mountain dwelling excels—
facing the wind beneath the moon’s glow.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the emerald mist.

In quiet solitude, mountain dwelling excels—
clouds stretch o’er the azure gorge.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to frost in snow.

In quiet solitude, mountain dwelling excels—
haze lingers ‘twixt verdant ridges.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I ask the white clouds.

In quiet solitude, mountain dwelling excels—
forest and spring span a jade flask.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to a lone crane.

In quiet solitude, mountain dwelling excels—
yellow plum blossoms scent the garden.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to light filling the sky.

In quiet solitude, mountain dwelling excels—
a solitary cloud seals the jade peak.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the crane soaring heavenward.

In quiet solitude, mountain dwelling excels—
green pines cling to the half-sky.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the Upper Numinous Palace.

In quiet solitude, mountain dwelling excels—
a brushwood gate half-closed, aslant.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to luminous sand.

**Seeking Truth by Abandoning Thoughts**

No clinging to parents’ love,
cultivate resolve with wholehearted intent.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to wisdom’s radiant embrace.

No clinging to siblings’ love,
cultivate resolve with steadfast effort.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to wisdom’s illumination.

No clinging to spouse and children’s love,
cultivate resolve with unyielding will.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to wisdom’s brilliance.

No clinging to sons and daughters’ love,
cultivate resolve with searching mind.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to wisdom’s flowing light.

No clinging to affection’s love,
cultivate resolve with penetrating force.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to wisdom’s measured glow.

No clinging to fame and profit’s love,
cultivate resolve with discerning heart.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to wisdom’s unfolding.

No clinging to wine and sensuality’s love,
cultivate resolve with earnest seeking.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to wisdom’s clear gaze.

No clinging to wealth and vigor’s love,
cultivate resolve with exhaustive pursuit.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to wisdom’s pupil.

No clinging to riches and honor’s love,
cultivate resolve with diligent search.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to wisdom’s heart.

No clinging to worldly attachments’ love,
cultivate resolve with lucid intent.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to wisdom’s bright eye.

**Dispelling Delusion and Returning to the True**

Seek not mercury within lead,
nor hunt for lead in mercury’s embrace.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the jade lotus.

No need to search heart and kidneys,
nor weary over lungs and liver.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to ancient Chang’an.

Speak not of celestial cycles,
nor exhaust the work of fire and timing.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the crystal palace.

No need to cultivate yin’s nature,
nor nurture the illusory mind.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to gold in water.

Seek not dragon and tiger,
nor chase the maiden and infant.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to dusk’s clearing clouds.

Ingesting elixirs breeds illness,
fasting leaves the belly hollow.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the sun’s resplendent pearl.

Swallowing saliva worsens ailments,
consuming mist vainly taxes the spirit.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the city of quicksilver.

Why refine, O enlightened one?
Deluded disciples speak of harvesting yin.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to Qujiang’s heart.

No need for frequent prayers,
nor daily fasting’s toil.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to osmanthus in bloom.

Speak not of essence and qi,
nor exhaust the tiger and dragon.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the jade hibiscus.

**Forging the Mind and Quieting Thoughts**

Crude in nature, the heart resists awakening,
deluded in passion, the Dao remains blocked.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the Purple Tenuity Palace.

Cast off the bonds of fame,
break free from profit’s chains.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the ancient stream’s edge.

Worldly affairs entangle endlessly,
yet the principle of cultivating truth is not complex.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the fire dragon’s ascent.

Innate purity averts calamity,
a straight heart avoids misfortune.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to fallen red plum blossoms.

Passions forgotten, the heart returns to simplicity,
desires extinguished, nature regains purity.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the sacred camphor.

Realizing truth transcends clinging to forms,
awakening to principle spares the body toil.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the revolving lantern’s court.

Defiled thoughts hinder awakening,
deluded passions breed doubt.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the Great Abyss.

Fame and profit gradually wane,
meritorious practice steadily grows.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the emerald vine.

A broad heart embraces the Dharma-realm,
a narrow mind cannot hold a hair’s breadth.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the crane soaring o’er the marsh.

Lust and greed dull the heart’s nature,
abstaining from sensuality invigorates spirit and qi.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the moon’s radiant clarity.

**Expounding the Profound and Transforming the Ignorant**

Enlightened ones return to truth,
while common folk all fall into error.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the moonlit stream.

Putting others first is true conduct,
prioritizing others embodies sage virtue.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the white clouds.

To ascend to immortality’s rank,
one must rely on unwavering resolve.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the moon at the window.

Visitors seek essential teachings,
none grasp the wondrous mystery.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the *Five Thousand Words*.

Non-action is still illusion,
action again becomes error.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the purple灵芝.

The Three Teachings merge as one,
the myriad methods all converge.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the Great Void’s center.

All are obscured by ignorance’s veil,
all are bound by karma’s fiery chains.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the sun’s fresh brilliance.

Guiding the lost is like threading a needle,
awakening is like piercing the eye.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the golden jade flask.

To see existence is not to grasp it,
to speak of emptiness is not yet empty.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the union of Kan and Li.

If you seek the pure Dharma,
shun the company of fame and profit.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the drifting white clouds.

The subtle essence revealed—
a jade maiden veils in sheer silk,
a golden infant swaddled in crimson gauze.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the sun’s crystalline radiance.

The ocean’s vault congeals pearl and jade,
the dragon palace guards quicksilver.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the jade capital’s spring.

Ghostly lads pass through golden gates,
divine lords pierce jade windows.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the Miluo River.

The Yellow Dame rides a white horse,
the Red Child straddles a green ox.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the autumn moon.

Heaven and earth alternate in closure and openness,
sun and moon naturally exchange their light.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the flowing quicksilver.

Drawing and adding to separate water and fire,
increasing and decreasing to balance yin and yang.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the white cloud chamber.

A golden dragon coils around the precious tripod,
a jade tiger encircles the elixir furnace.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to a flask of ice.

The wind sweeps the cosmos still,
twilight passes and evening clouds clear.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the Great Void’s brightness.

The profound and subtle elude even spirits,
the mysterious and wondrous baffle even ghosts.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the cold jade furnace.

Auspicious qi soars to the heavens,
spirit sand overflows the earth.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the golden flower’s beauty.

Expelling evil and deciding the true—
the tripod refines and the three corpses perish,
the furnace burns and the five ghosts vanish.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the endless azure sky.

Sever the green dragon’s tail,
cleave the white tiger’s head.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the moon’s radiant tower.

Split open the golden water’s shore,
shatter the jade capital’s mountain.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the sunset pass.

The wisdom blade slays specters,
the divine sword severs demons.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the celestial river.

The dragon’s roar stirs green mist,
the tiger’s howl summons black wind.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the sun’s star.

The sword seals and the three realms grow still,
the talisman guards and the five directions find peace.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the jade void altar.

Mighty arms dispel the six harms,
victory slays the three corpses.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the revolving light banner.

Strike open the seamless lock,
shatter the ghost gate’s barrier.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the jade-linked rings.

Curb desire with the divine sword,
eliminate passion with the wisdom blade.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the moon’s ascent.

Wine, lust, wealth, and wrath—
all are swept away by a single sword stroke.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the soaring white clouds.

Discerning truth from falsehood—
clinging to doctrine obscures the ancestor,
exhausting scriptures fails to reveal the source.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to Jade Flower Peak.

Seeing form within the formless,
illuminating emptiness yet finding shape.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the ancient wind’s courtyard.

Alas, the fleeting affairs of mortal life,
how briefly they endure in the body.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the dragon’s radiant light.

Aiding others yet failing to clarify nature,
turning inward to recognize the original heart.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the abyss’s depths.

Above, it reaches the distant three realms,
below, it penetrates the profound nine netherworlds.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the azure wave’s heart.

All speak of having within the non-having,
all declare non-having within the having.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the Great Mystery’s pearl.

The earth splits to reveal golden wells,
the heavens open to gush forth jade springs.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the moon’s immortal.

Delusion and heresy lie a thousand leagues away,
awakening to truth is not remote.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the jade mushroom’s sprout.

Clinging to having is not true having,
knowing emptiness is not yet emptiness.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the emerald pool’s midst.

The heartless create their own obstacles,
forming appearances becomes demonic.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the stilling waves.

Blending with the world without杂念,
harmonizing light without defilement.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the natural person.

The moon clarifies and heaven and earth grow resplendent,
the wind stills and the Great Void expands.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the purple-golden pellet.

Cloud roots birth auspicious herbs,
water valleys nurture spirit sprouts.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the Jade Emperor’s abode.

Striking things, the three rivers resound,
knocking on emptiness, the four seas echo.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the city of Luochang.

Within the flask, sun and moon are gathered,
within the tripod, heaven and earth are grasped.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the Great Mystery’s gate.

The red serpent turns beneath the water,
the black tortoise faces within the fire.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the cinnabar heavens.

Light mist rises over the mountains,
thin smoke stretches to the horizon.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the rain’s first clearing.

In the water, the azure leech,
in the snow, the white toad.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the great ox-cart.

The golden rooster strides like jade,
the jade hare flies like gold.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the fivefold clouds’ depths.

The will pure as jade’s clarity,
the mind serene as ice’s stillness.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the jade capital.

The Three-in-One’s primordial unity—
the eastern sea’s sunlight gleams,
the western river’s moonlight shines.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to earth and heaven.

Two tripods’ medicine refined,
one furnace’s elixir completed.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to Jade Capital Mountain.

Nurturing spirit like the bright moon,
pervading the Dao like the clear wind.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the Jade Dawn Palace.

Two jade staffs,
a pair of heaven-piercing gates.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the three snow chambers.

The wooden man with three eyes,
the stone maiden with two brows.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the water buffalo.

Before the cliff, the two luminaries open,
atop the peak, the three stars appear.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the cave’s completion.

Split open the heavenly tripod’s eye,
reveal the profound and obscure essence.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the purple mushroom’s growth.

Open the eye beneath the brow,
reveal the pupil within the eye.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the flawless crystal.

The Dao-heart remains ever unobscured,
the Dharma-eye naturally clear.

When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the pure and luminous light.

Unfurrow the brows to open the wisdom-root,
the hindmost eye reveals divine radiance.
When asked, “What is the Dao?”
with a smile, I point to the unveiled Hall of Light.

A poem of one to seven characters,
Inscribed, inscribed, inscribed.
The formula is correct—dispel delusion.
Unfold the wondrous teaching, expound the true mechanism.
A clear and true indication, free and unhesitating.

False words bring heaven and earth to ruin,
swift retribution follows karmic consequences.
Both eyes weep blood congealed,
the whole body topples into peril.
In Fengdu, forever endure the knife-mountain tribulation,
a myriad blades pierce the body to muddy flesh.

The formula, the formula, the formula.
Expedient means, uplifting guidance.
Save all beings, without distinction.
The Great Dao is openly transmitted,
heavenly secrets are divulged.

Cultivate nature like silver frost,
