penetrate into delicate, crystalline snow.
Release the two streams of pure light,
embrace firmly the wheel of bright moon.
Lifespan equal to heaven and earth, everlasting,
never straying from the present audience at the Golden Gate.

Cultivate goodness, goodness, goodness.
Compassion, expedient means.
Act with grace, merit spreads everywhere.
Universally aid all beings, without regard for high or low.
Respond to things to reveal the true constant,
unveil the numinous, cloud-like visage.
One thread of qi-flame illumines the void,
two points of divine light appear.
Secretly receive the celestial talisman, proclaimed by the Jade Emperor,
the Golden Youth leads into the Palace of Longevity.

Evil, evil, evil.

Disdain the poor, bully the weak.
Erode virtue and power, make frivolous promises.
Withhold kindness and favor, delight in cruelty and arrogance.
Cunning and flattery harbor a tiger’s heart,
venomous malice spies like poison in others.
The Fengdu courts condemn without plea,
sin meets the searing blade of righteous flame.
A thousand layers of icy, gleaming swords—
the body suffers regret, the path ahead in ruin.

**Beware, beware, beware.**
For the self, steadfast and swift.
Cast out the Three Poisons, purge the Six Harms.
Sever perverse views, shun the strange and aberrant.
If truth is not cultivated in this life,
the next will but replay old debts.
Be pure, prudent, selfless—
abide in oneness, let no attachment arise.
Gathering and dispersing, misty fragrance spills from the celestial garden,
auspicious light weaves into a canopy of heavenly blossoms.

**Still, still, still.**
Nurture spirit, sustain life.
Guard the true source, return to authentic rightness.
Silent and limpid, vast and serene.
The profound root of emptiness is firm,
the heart attuned to the Dao communes with the sacred.
Naturally, all monstrosities withdraw,
only then do the myriad spirits rejoice as one.
Merging with numinous light into the Great Beginning,
in the void appears the luminous mirror of the mind.

**Pure, pure, pure.**

Sever thought, forget emotion.
Cultivate right awakening, swiftly attain perfection.
The sea stills into emptiness, vast and boundless as the celestial forest.
A jade flask chills with autumn waters, a golden well pours forth icy jade-green.
Clouds part to reveal the lofty heavens,
the spirit-terrace gleams bright and clear.
Above the three thousand realms, the mind clarifies and expands—
in the moonlit tower, one sits alone gazing toward Penglai.

**Still, still, still.**
Empty the heart, enter samādhi.
Establish true practice, cultivate true conduct.
Cool and refreshing, limpid and awakened,
the profound essence shimmers like deep autumn waves,
mirroring the distant autumn river.
The moon of the Three Heavens shines dustless,
the immortal winds of ten thousand leagues gleam jade-green.
With a single stroke, all things are severed—
solitary, one sits in cultivation of body and life.

**Steady, steady, steady.**
Return to the origin, restore the beginning.
From being arises, from non-being emerges.
The spirit roams the boundless void, piercing inner and outer.
Within and without, awareness merges with emptiness,
the three yang currents flow into the body.
Self and world dissolve into the origin,
the ten thousand transformations arise from no-other.
A single ripple of cold light rises from the azure pool,
illuminating Penglai’s isles to their radiant depths.

**First, first, first.**

**Through the spirit, gate and window.**
Gaze upon the Southern Apex, glance at the Northern Dipper.
Lord of a thousand transformations, master of ten thousand changes.
The handle of the celestial Dipper turns the mechanism,
the pivot of the Gate of Yi revolves the elbow.
Revealing the Jade Hare’s golden essence,
merging with the numinous void’s wisdom-mouth.
Vast, it overflows the eyes and fills all existence—
ascending the mysterious Dao, the Great Non-Being within Being.

**Precious, precious, precious.**
No old, no new.
Cast off noble and base, sever near and distant.
Naturally ascending and descending,
darkly drawing in ghosts and spirits.
Radiance surges like the blazing sun,
luminous purity gleams without dust.
The Great Dao observes as one body—
awakening, there is no self, no other.
In the Seven Treasures Grove, Infant and Maiden play,
the high void’s wind and moon become close neighbors.

**Profound, profound, profound.**
No limit, no end.
Sun and moon as one, heaven and earth together.
Pervading empty space, unshaken and unmoved.
Resplendent, flawless, without blemish,
brilliant, boundless, seamless.
Wielding my great power and divine penetration,
crushing the minute and subtle to draw near.
Let the Crow and Hare fly to and fro as they will—
the spirit’s light first awakens to the constant use.

**Cultivate, cultivate, cultivate.**

Fierce resolve, a turn of the head.
Opening the Dao-eye, unfolding the clear gaze.
The Flowery Pond brims full,
spirit-water overflows in its course.
Sunlight illumines the pure realm,
moon’s luster shines on clear autumn.
Seated, one beholds the celestial script of jade,
moving, one rides the earth’s golden ox.
The vast expanse traversed without trace,
stepping beyond the heavens, roaming beyond things.

**Walk, walk, walk.**
Vigilant, utmost sincerity.
Cultivating the superior adept,
abiding in non-contention.
Nurturing spirit, fostering qi,
preserving life, attaining long life.
Treading the void to commune with the Great Dao,
circling and stepping through empty clarity.
The ancient path stands level and true,
no straying into wilds or reckless flight.
Red dust of the worldly road never drifts near—
a single journey to wander the Jasper Capital.

**Blade, blade, blade.**
Three feet long, fine as a breath.
No filth or clamor,
cutting off dust and noise.
Shearing away ghosts and demons,
cleaving asunder worldly toil.
On mountain peaks seizing rhinos and tigers,
in the sea’s depths slaying dragons and serpents.
By night entrusted to the Southern Asterism and Northern Dipper,
by day enfeoffing the sea’s peaks and heaven’s waist.
Its form enters the void, unknown to others—
a single thread of pure qi ascends to the cinnabar heavens.

**Spear, spear, spear.**

**Spear, spear, spear.**
Attaining the great, boundless in form.
Radiant as the sun’s brilliance, illuminating heaven’s light.
Virtue subdues ghosts and demons,
battle repels demon kings.
Cleaving open the sea of perfect enlightenment,
piercing through the azure vault of heaven.
Upright, it thrusts through sky and props up earth;
held crosswise, it pacifies the frontier.
Disciples who master the golden spear technique
no longer cling to the stench of maggots and festering sores.

**Dragon, dragon, dragon.**
Emerging strange, surpassing the crowd.
In motion fierce, in stillness heroic.
Mouth spewing flames of fire,
ears sipping the cold wind.
Its two eyes conceal sun and moon,
its belly encompasses the cosmos.
Unfurls its claws to overturn the dharma-realm,
grinds its horns to scrape through Kunlun.
A single thunderous roar shakes the heavens—
the three rivers and four seas all hear its name.

**Tiger, tiger, tiger.**
Central, the primal mother.
King of all beasts, ancestor of the mountains.
Fierce and heroic,
lord of heaven and earth.
A single hair devours the four plums,
its two eyes dissolve past and present.
Pulls mountains to shake earth and sky,
paces the void to tread open the Purple Palace.
In furious roar, it deafens the celestial thoroughfare—
a single cry startles the Dark Warrior.

**Spirit, spirit.**

Formless, the dharmakāya.
Heart’s treasure, Dao’s rarity.
Vast it encompasses heaven and earth,
minute it enters the tiniest dust.
Pushes aside the handle of stars,
turns the pivot of sunlight’s wheel.
Darkly conceals the unerring mechanism,
clearly discerns the primordial mystery.
Shatters a thousand gates to open ten thousand dharmas—
the boundless sky blazes, transmuting into pure yang.

**Qi**
**Qi, qi.**
Unobstructed, unclosed.
Root of heaven and earth,
thread of the Void.
The Great Dao flows through,
spiritual mechanism interlocks.
Permeates the cosmos with primordial chaos,
chaotic harmony universally sustains.
Ceaselessly circulates breath in fusion—
silently nurtures the true form’s restraint.
Naturally the empty valley transforms the spirit,
jade blossoms scatter where they ascend to the Celestial Emperor.

**Luminosity**
**Luminous, luminous.**
Earth still, heaven clear.
The Great Void expansive,
vast and boundless.
Within the realm, emptiness and stillness—
island seas, clouds serene.
Scorching sun blazes resplendent,
divine radiance gleams concentrated.
Illumines and reflects all things at dawn,
silver abyss fills the eye, level and smooth.
The numinous void lets my spirit play freely—
jade lads leap into the crystal city.

**Essence**
**Essence, essence.**

**Penetrating Sun, Sinking Seas.**
Vapors rise in lush profusion,
auspicious qi takes form.
Wind stills, waves settle—
ripples drift like shooting stars.
Intertwined radiance simmers jade snow,
luminous moonbeams gleam bright.
Heaven and earth stand as a golden crucible,
brimming full with liquid silver’s sheen.
Dawn’s sky strikes jade-green clouds of emerald haze,
brilliant and boundless, the Great Purity appears.

**True**
**True, true.**
Limpid and pure,
light renewed.
Subtle beyond measure,
vast beyond end.
Pervading the primordial beginning,
the Brahmā heavens stretch boundless.
Wind clears, wafting through Kan’s gate;
moon shines, piercing Li’s palace.
In desire, the spirit’s abyss is desireless;
amid dust, the great Dao is dustless.
The Dao—though not the Dao—knows the constant Dao;
spiritual transformation—though no-spirit—is thus spirit.

**Empty**
**Empty, empty.**
The Great Ultimate,
interconnected.
Embracing the great image,
all-encompassing.
Five Phases cannot reach it,
Eight Trigrams cannot fathom.
Vast and void, above and below,
unbound, east and west.
No trace, no form, no shadow—
neither blue nor green nor red.
From ancient past to present, hard to discern,
yet by force of name, the great Dao establishes heaven and earth.

**See**
**See, see.**

**Originally,**
**the head and face.**
Opening the eye of wisdom,
divine radiance shines forth.
Mirroring brilliance without form,
the great void manifests.
Twin streaks of lightning fly,
dazzling as silver silk.
Following the moment, self and things dwell as one;
in application, knowing the constant amid ten thousand changes.
A single wheel of wisdom’s eye illumines the celestial steps—
the Jade Infant leaps into the Hall of Luminous Pervasion.

**Hear**
**Hear, hear.**
Examining intent,
profound and still.
Returning to original nature,
awakening the true heart.
Washing away Zheng and Wei,
sound and color cannot invade.
Right and wrong—how could they enter the ear?
Ever hearing the tiger’s roar and dragon’s chant.
Unplayed, the celestial music arises naturally;
the primeval tone resounds, deep and ancient.
The valley of wisdom rings with pure resonance—
a single note pierces the ninefold forest of clouds.

**Know**
**Know, know.**
Within and without,
heaven’s mystery.
Communing with true subtlety,
attaining the profound and minute.
No cultivation, no attainment,
no action, no striving.
Luminous as kingfisher jade,
the Dragon Child gleams in crimson robes.
Inner and outer shine through, clear and bright;
the heart opens—all dharmas are not.
The vast sea reveals the heart-moon’s single wheel,
its essence flashing forth in radiant splendor.

**Awake**
**Awake, awake.**

On all sides, a single circuit.
With spiritual penetration, yet nameless simplicity.
The body entire—empty space;
dharma and not-dharma alike.
The adept fundamentally non-acting,
yet the unenlightened—both eyes blind.
The mystery plainly revealed,
yet face-to-face, the spirit’s thought drifts distant.
A single celestial path, immaculate and dustless—
golden crow scattering, silver light cascading.

**Exhaust**
**Exhaust, exhaust.**
Earth quakes, heaven turns.
Piercing the valley’s spirit, penetrating the mysterious female.
The more one practices, the farther it seems;
the more one employs, the nearer it grows.
Gazing afar, it spans heaven’s thoroughfare;
drawn close, it pervades a single inch.
Seeking, the earth’s corners yield no trace;
vast, the sahā world remains unmoved.
The luminous inscription—pure emptiness, the body of great void;
the sunlit abyss—who lacks its boundless share?

**Virtue**
**Virtue, virtue.**
Fathomless, evanescent.
Externally, an empty heart;
internally, a full belly.
The moon encircles the Li Palace,
a pure breeze enters the kingdom.
A single pearl blazes in the sky,
illuminating the darkness of ignorance.
Radiant, it merges with the dust in harmony;
pervading the world, utterly void of obstruction.
As one yin dissolves, one yang arises—
the flawless jade of emptiness suffuses all.

**Attain**
**Attain, attain.**

**No Cause, No Effect.**
Sever greed and wrath, dissolve self and other.
Still the mind—smoke dissipates;
clear the heart—fire is extinguished.
Shatter the patriarch’s barrier,
unlock the dragon-phoenix shackles.
Jewels of flawless jade abound,
yet within lies a single Mystic Pearl.
The Mystic Pearl divides as the Jade Infant pays homage,
a golden lotus bud held firm in the embrace.

**Attain**
**Attain, attain.**
Illumine Kan, brighten Li.
Spirit meets in harmony, the Dao walks hand in hand.
Grasp the void—no delusion remains in the heart.
Heaven’s clarity transmits the wondrous dharma,
earth’s stillness reveals the subtle and profound.
Heaven and earth share one heart,
luminous yet vast beyond kalpas, beyond sound.
From ancient times, unbroken, boundless—nothing to grasp,
the spirit roams the azure vaults, level with the Great Abyss.

**Act**
**Act, act.**
Awaken to truth, free from delusion.
Unseal the nature’s awareness, realize the heart’s wisdom.
Wash away all contrivance,
no thought of Chan’s mechanism.
Strike through each and every one,
every thing withdraws its radiance.
The body merges with heaven’s emptiness, the sea’s stillness;
awakening reveals the ten thousand dharmas as nonexistent.
Within the Mystery, a fragrant breeze stirs,
the spirit transforms—moonlight spills full in the west.

**Eternal**
**Eternal, eternal.**

Still the sitting, dissolve the details.
Suddenly the still realm—awareness turns cool and clear.
The Radiant Youth opens the way,
guides into the immortal land.
Seal-script smoke veils earth’s beauty,
bright candles illuminate heaven’s light.
Bestowed with peach of immortality and cassia wine,
drunk and drowsing in lofty halls.
Suddenly a pure melody arises,
jade maidens vie to support me into the grotto chamber.

**Yang**
**Yang, yang.**
Pervading, filling all directions.
Virtue manifests transformation, the Dao expands.
Golden essence flows and scatters,
treasured seals emit radiance.
Light soars through the Milky Way’s bones,
crimson dyes the vast azure.
Reflecting back, not beyond daily use,
returning to the origin, first awakening to true constancy.
Stripping away pure yin, the ancient Dao is revealed,
the spirit elixir unimpeded—heaven’s eternity attained.

**Leisure**
**Leisure, leisure.**
Utmost sageliness, beyond the ordinary.
Morning in the still realm, departing the dusty world.
Truth intermingles with truth, each thing without attachment.
Water and clouds ever companions,
wind and moon the homeland.
Thirst quenched with cassia wine from the gourd,
drunk, alone reclining on Kun Mountain.
A single dream of roaming immortals—
freely, carefree between heaven and earth.

**Vermilion**
**Vermilion, vermilion.**

**Youthful Spring**
**Youthful spring, youthful spring—**
at sixteen, naturally paired,
breath shared in perfect accord.
Jade countenance, fair flesh,
elegant and refined.
Matched beneath embroidered curtains,
dreaming as one, startling awake.
Suddenly leaping from the silken chamber,
golden blossoms scattered in disarray.
Eyes fixed, never to part,
hearts in bright union circling the Morning Palace.

**Breath**
**Breath, breath—**
breath. Solitary, self-standing.
No outward invasion,
no inward intrusion.
Born of the true heart,
formless in essence.
Silent, the hall of utmost emptiness;
desolate, the chamber of stillness.
Two painted candles illumine the void,
their light mirroring a blazing sun.
What doubt remains in this truth?
In pure quiescence, all affairs are complete.

**Mystery**
**Mystery, mystery—**
mystery. Radiant, yet not dazzling.
Gazing at heaven,
soaring through the boundless sky.
The Supreme Polarity’s subtle profundity,
vast, without limit.
Moon on water mirrors the azure void,
reflecting back in luminous return.
Myriad methods awaken to the One Method,
the One Method held in three essentials.
Preserving the Three, guarding the One—qi and spirit clarified,
transmuting yang essence to descend through the nine apertures.

**Law**
**Law, law.**

No question,
no answer.
Penetrating the mysterious vision,
dwelling in absolute learning.
Beyond names and words,
knowing emptiness in sudden awakening.
Sudden awakening—Dao is without mind,
through mind, the same as the chick’s first peck.
Fused, sun and moon shine as one,
pervading mountains, rivers, seas, and peaks.
Heaven’s nature in humanity,
humanity’s nature in heaven—
naturally, a single nameless simplicity.

**Dao**
**Dao, Dao—**
Dao. Subtle,
profound.
True reality,
without form or appearance.
Mystery within mystery,
wonder within wonder.
Myriad things flourish of themselves,
their arising not by contrivance.
Revolving, sun and moon soar through the void;
scattered, they illumine the ten directions.
Awakened, there is no earth, no heaven—
the sage merely posits an empty name.

**Virtue**
**Virtue, virtue—**
Virtue. Nourishing,
all things.
Pervading east and west,
penetrating south and north.
Resplendent yet formless,
the great void silent.
Splitting open the marrow of dragon and phoenix,
shattering the sinews and bones of heaven.
Golden essence scatters in streaming radiance,
piercing through the cosmos in vagueness.
Spirit-light, dazzling, coalesces into a crimson mass—
gathered, it enters the cavern of the golden crow.

**Water**
**Water, water.**

**Trickling, trickling,**
unceasing.
Above, no waves;
below, no bottom.
Welling and surging in the void,
dragon’s fat and phoenix’s marrow.
A single taste irrigates the heart-field,
moistening and nurturing the body of cultivated truth.
Skin pure as frost and snow,
pure yang naturally void of yin ghosts.
Bright eyes lift the brows beyond the great void—
without moving a step, one rises in empty space.

**Pool**
**Pool, pool, pool.**
Willow banks,
dikes that droop.
Dividing water-valleys,
illumining cold streams.
Golden waves lightly ripple,
jade liquid pours in abundance.
The silver toad casts snowy billows,
dazzling the eye with boundless depths.
A single moistening sets valley streams flowing in relief;
harmony surges, myriad transformations rest in ease.
The flowery pool’s divine water exists in every household—
the adept acts without acting, without striving.

**Fluid**
**Fluid, fluid.**
Spontaneous,
ebbing and flowing.
Nurturing clear flesh,
cultivating numinous substance.
Externally aligning with the celestial circuit,
internally merging with the chamber of spirit.
The Palace of Fire brims and overflows,
the eye beholds pristine light dripping.
Mysterious frost congeals into a rich balm,
essence blazes red as the scorching sun.
A single speck of the fetal star transcends the immortal palace—
the face reveals the Three Clarities’ work complete.

**Elixir**
**Elixir, elixir.**

**Heaven and Earth,**
**between them.**
Soaring phoenixes distant, fire dragons wheeling.
Pivotal mechanisms gather the essential,
revolving the Golden Gate.
Gathering the essence of the Three Luminaries,
reversing the cycle through the Seven Apertures.
A single pellet enfolds the cosmos,
transforming to inhale plum blossoms and swallow mountains.
Feeding on enlightenment, ascending to court the Purple Palace—
inscribed in the Jade Register, ranked among the immortals’ host.

**Nature**
**Nature, nature.**
Numinous source,
communing with the sage.
No awareness, no seeing or hearing.
Clear as a cold spring,
luminous as a precious mirror.
Reflecting yet formless,
things arrive and respond in kind.
Knowing the heart departs from desire to contemplate emptiness,
facing circumstances, right and wrong distinguish themselves.
Lodging at night in the Toad Palace to pluck osmanthus,
at dawn leaping into the Golden Crow’s path.

**Life**
**Life, life.**
Let it not
contend or compete.
Move with the seasons, respond to their flow.
Pure, still, and serene,
perfect in bearing, qi abundant.
Essence securely preserved, spirit whole—
only then does the true heart settle.
Blood within the body transmutes to balm,
flesh and bone equally fuse, lustrous and clear.
The elixir perfected, pure yang emerges from the Five Phases—
a decree descends from the Jade Void, proclaiming the mandate.

**Lead**
**Lead, lead.**

Boundless, without edge.
Essence dense and lush, qi unbroken and flowing.
Movement gives birth to the ten thousand things,
stillness of the sea, profound and dark.
The profound and dark—marrow of heaven and earth,
movement and stillness—root and origin of the Dao.
Seen, yet neither nonexistent nor existent,
heard, yet silent and hushed.

A jade flask, ice-pure, cleanses heart and bone,
deep and vast as clouds, the sky of snow and moon.

**Mercury**
**Mercury, mercury.**
Still,
unmoving.
The Dao’s passage,
the spirit’s function.
Piercing gold, penetrating stone,
a sword cleaving the seamless.
The jade infant cradles the precious moon,
playfully toying with crystal.

A day of silver mist, interwoven with light,
glittering neither far nor near.
Wielded as the sacred ancestor’s Daoist wind,
ancient tones pierce the pure, pure resonance.

**Principle**
**Principle, principle.**
Sun’s essence,
moon’s marrow.
Above, it connects to heaven,
below, it penetrates earth.
Within and without, they merge—
its spirit not spectral.
Radiant, blazing the celestial thoroughfare,
brilliant, its light enters the body.
Square or round, curved or straight, following form,
supreme goodness—heart deep as water.
Congealing in emptiness, crystalline and clear,
profound and luminous, fused to the very depths.

**One**
**One, one.**

**Difficult to embody, difficult to practice.**
Crooked yet aligned with the upright,
bent yet attuned to the straight.
The great square has no corners,
solitary in vast stillness.
Clear as day before one’s eyes,
yet the man facing it does not recognize.
Grasping or relinquishing—neither adds nor subtracts,
seeking yields no end, no limit.

From ancient times, the one luminous true nature manifests,
turning light back to fill the true void of the Great Emptiness.

**Profound**
**Profound, profound.**
Vast as the boundless paths,
minute as the distant byways.
Beyond all seeking,
without flaw or blame.
Neither being nor non-being,
neither void nor form.
Vastness so immense it has no breadth,
subtlety so fine it has no narrowness.
Ponder it—spirit scatters in silent vastness,
contemplate it—soul dissolves like drifting clouds.
Endless, infinite, unknowable,
now departing, now arriving, like a passing traveler.

**Vague**
**Vague, vague.**
Heaven and earth,
sealed and brimming.
Within the primordial chaos,
congealed in the valley of emptiness.
Empty yet not empty,
things yet no things.
Something exists, merged with the mysterious origin,
the mysterious origin surging with supreme virtue.
Divine radiance—dim and obscure,
Dao’s transformation—hushed and silent.
Suddenly, one truth seizes heaven’s mechanism,
the true rule of the Great One within the alchemical crucible.

**Mysterious**
**Mysterious, mysterious.**
The Supreme Ultimate,
boundless.
Below, it shifts earth,
above, it connects to heaven.
Essence of the Three Luminaries refined,
one qi luminously transmitted.
The furnace gate opens two paths,
dragon and tiger contend in the vanguard.
Playfully coaxing the bright pearl from the sea,
casting it skyward, rolling earthward with thunderous clamor.
Once the elixir is formed, shedding the husk to wander the Three Isles,
carefree in the Penglai gardens, years uncounted.

**Numinous**
**Numinous, numinous.**

Qi flourishes, spirit clarifies.
Congealing to chase the moon, dazzling to outrace the stars.
In high emptiness, gracious illumination;
across the great earth, purity and brightness.
Luminous as ice and snow,
translucent as crystal.
Vast and shimmering, heaven and earth gleam immaculate;
radiant and resplendent, the realm knows perfect peace.
The five directions’ rosy hues gather into the crucible,
the twin luminaries’ intersecting light enters the precious vase.

**Heaven**
**Heaven, heaven.**
Profound, profound.
Master of a thousand mechanisms,
wielder of ten thousand transformations.
Gazing upward—ever more lofty;
delving deeper—ever more steadfast.
Above, it invades the realm of Primordial Beginning;
below, it blankets the boundless vast.
Limpid beyond the Five Phases,
obscure before the Eight Trigrams.
At first division, one qi at the head of the Three Powers;
alone and solitary, it precedes the Emperor of Images.

**Mechanism**
**Mechanism, mechanism.**
Embodying the Dao, the heart knows.
Opening the eye of wisdom,
awakening to the subtle and silent.
Shifting spirit through ten thousand changes,
wondrous transformation through non-action.
Non-action generates one qi,
one qi moves the Three Marvels.
Blending the refined and the anciently pure,
passing through movement, stillness, and abiding without doubt.
Perceiving things, the heart illumines—yet the heart departs from things;
in profound obscurity, bearing and demeanor transcend convention.

**Stream**
**Stream, stream.**

Ancient banks, golden dikes.
Filling the Dao-eye, wisdom’s radiance shines.
Trickling without cease,
flowing into the celestial pool.
Azure waters open the pure valley,
profound depths stir the boundless vast.
Along the banks, fish sport in play;
from the wave’s heart, a sacred tortoise leaps forth.
Its mouth sprays crimson mist where golden sands congeal,
nurturing the divine elixir to match the sacred mechanism.

**Pill**
**Pill, pill, pill.**
Gathered in a pinch, brows knit in concentration.
Piercing the Dao-eye, embodying the profound mystery.
Responding to things, the mechanism appears;
adapting to all shapes, assuming every form.
Illumining the numinous yang’s awakening,
the mind’s clarity expands the dharma-realm.
Heaven and earth cycle with sun and moon;
in the void, tigers coil and dragons entwine.
The elixir terrace cradles the Three Luminaries’ blaze,
a flawless, gleaming orb of jade.

**Sprout**
**Sprout, sprout, sprout.**
Merit deepens, wonders multiply.
Rooted firmly, let nothing stray.
Constantly replenish mercury’s waters,
daily advance lead’s sands.
The numinous shoot first emerges from soil,
unfolding into golden blossoms of beauty.
Tender beyond Chang’e’s cinnamon,
verdant as the Queen Mother’s immortal blooms.
Gathered, it may attend the Ever-Spring Assembly;
boldly, it may boast in Jasper Pool or Penglai’s gardens.

**Snow**
**Snow, snow.**

No cold, no chill.
Within existence it arises, in emptiness it is arrayed.
Ethereal without gap, crystalline and translucent.
Shimmering, the Great Void brightens;
resplendent, its light gleams pure.
The boundless sky, silken as a silver river;
the vast earth, cleansed like jade dust.
The scorching red sun cannot melt it—
through all seasons it keeps company with the high moon.

**Thus**
**Thus, thus.**
Most wondrous, profoundly mysterious.
Illumining true nature, nurturing the numinous source.
Transmitted yet not conferred,
its meaning grasped beyond words.
The Three Fields brim with lush essence;
with every breath, qi flows unbroken.
Inhaling and exhaling, never leaving the Mysterious Female—
do not take mouth or nose as the cause.
Within the wuwei crucible, the Three Flowers bloom;
from the red furnace, the seven-petaled lotus emerges.

**Secrecy**
**Secrecy, secrecy.**
No form, no trace.
Drawing in the pure wind, summoning the gracious sun.
Serene and solitary,
vast and independent.
A thousand points of pristine light,
ten thousand streams of numinous essence.
Within it, a luminous pearl is born—
once refined, the Embryonic Immortal is complete.
Leisurely, it emerges from the Three Realms’ surging waves,
knowing the destination on Penglai’s path.
